# ROADMAP ‚Äî Living Frontier Ledger
> The persistent, dynamic task ledger for an exploratory project. Survives across sessions (unlike a session's scratch task list). Update it at the end of every session: move items between **Inbox / Now / Open / Parked / Done**. This is where "what were we doing?" gets answered without re-deriving it.

## Inbox ‚Äî capture diversions here, DON'T chase them
> The rule (Chris's): when something shiny appears mid-session, it gets a ticket here ‚Äî it does **not** hijack the current focus. "Ooh, something new!" ‚Üí write it down, keep going. Triage Inbox ‚Üí Open/Parked at session end. A diversion captured is free; a diversion chased costs the thread.

- ~~**‚ñ∂üî¥ FOUNDATIONAL DECOMPILER BUG ‚Äî compare opcodes render INVERTED direction**~~ **FIXED 2026-06-04 (ORACLE-CONFIRMED, commit pending).** `vm_decompile.py`'s hand-written opcode‚Üímnemonic map had **FOUR** compares wrong (the oracle sweep found one more than the first triage): the regular layout is signed `[lt,le,gt,ge]`=C2-C5, unsigned `[lt,le,gt,ge]`=C6-C9, but the map had **C3/C5 le‚Üîge swapped** (`sge`/`sle` ‚Üí should be `sle`/`sge`) AND **C6/C9 lt‚Üîge swapped** (`uge`/`ult` ‚Üí should be `ult`/`uge`). Each verified vs the live ROM handler (`step_one_vm_op`, regL/regR matrix incl. ‚àí1-vs-1 for signedness); the **opcode table `vm-opcodes-v2.toml` was RIGHT all along** (SCMP*/UCMP*) ‚Äî only the decompiler's map drifted. **Blast radius: 323 comparison sites flipped** across all 4 banks (e.g. `seek_enemy‚Ä¶` `} while (local11 >= 6)` ‚Üí the correct `< 6`; `if (rng_mod(100) >= threshold)` ‚Üí `< threshold`). It survived because the **arithmetic** formulas are oracle-verified but comparison-DIRECTION in control flow was never exercised ‚Äî the exact [[feedback_foundation_discipline_early]] trap. **The gates structurally can't catch it** (round-trip = bytecode untouched; CFG-gate orientation flips consistently on raw+structured) ‚Üí built **`tools/probe-compare-opcodes.py`** as the permanent primitive-layer validator (oracle truth table vs decompiler map + `_BINOP` + toml; exit 1 on drift). All gates stay green post-fix (cfg 495/495, round-trip CLEAN, drift CLEAN, --check 0 BAD, test-vm-cfg 74). **LESSON (Chris): the VM is more robust than it first appears ‚Äî keep oracle-verifying primitives; structural gates pass over semantic-direction bugs.** [[feedback_foundation_discipline_early]] [[feedback_silent_tool_failure_hallucination]]
- ~~**‚ñ∂ DECOMPILER BUG ‚Äî value-producing conditional (ternary) renders as empty `if(){}else{}` and DROPS a value**~~ **FIXED (forward cases) 2026-06-04 ‚Äî and the same trap as the compare bug: gate-invisible, oracle-validated.** A value-diamond (`regA = cond ? a : b` ‚Äî two value-loading arms converging) was rendered as empty `if(){}else{}` / gotos-to-empty-labels with only ONE arm's value surviving (e.g. `spawn_zealot(...)(1)` instead of `(flag ? 0 : 1)`; `min_word`/`max_word` returned a single hardcoded arg). **Confirmed a 2nd surface form Chris found (`$A7DC`): the empty-`if/else` scan (72) UNDER-counted ‚Äî a bytecode scan for the converging value-diamond shape found 80 sites / 65 subs, incl. 24 feeding `return` (functions returning the wrong value) + 22 call-args + stores.** **FIX = coordinated expression-engine + CFG-gate change:** (1) `vm_cfg.value_diamonds` detects the shape (forward layout `head<fall<taken<merge`, each arm sole-pred = head, call-free cond); the decode loop folds it to `(cond ? vt : vf)` (`_ternary_expr`; polarity from branch_z/nz + which arm is fall vs taken), suppressing the head branch + fall jump + now-dead labels. (2) `vm_cfg.bytecode_cfg` CONTRACTS the same diamonds into their merge (a value-diamond is an EXPRESSION, not control flow ‚Äî like C `?:`) so `lower(raw)==bytecode_cfg` stays valid; both sides use the one detector so they can't disagree. **53 of 80 diamonds folded** (after recovering the 27 call-headed conds ‚Äî a call-valued cond is fine because capturing `dia_cond = state.regA` READS regA, which the getter treats as consuming the pending call, so the arm's later write won't double-render it; e.g. `return (test_map_cell_bits(arg1, arg2, 194) ? 0 : 1)`, `province_ai_state[x] = (get_province_ai_state(y) ? 5 : 0)`), incl. corrected `return`s + `min_word`/`max_word` now read as real min/max. **KEY: the CFG gate CANNOT see the ternary VALUE** (the contraction is symmetric on raw+structured, so a flipped polarity passes every structural gate ‚Äî the compare-bug blind spot again) ‚Üí built **`tools/probe-ternary-folds.py`** (runs min/max through the live handler; a polarity flip swaps them) ‚Äî ORACLE-CONFIRMED correct. Gates green: cfg 495/495 + 495/495 (**fallbacks 35 ‚Äî baseline, ZERO regression**), round-trip CLEAN, drift CLEAN, --check 0 BAD, test-vm-cfg 74‚Üí86.
  - üü¢ **SHORT-CIRCUIT BOOLEAN REGIONS ‚Äî DONE 2026-06-04 (the multi-predecessor compound conditions).** The 25 multi-pred sites the simple diamond left behind are short-circuit `&&`/`||` chains: a value arm reached from ‚â•2 branch points (e.g. `is_tile_in_bounds`'s `load 0` is the fail-exit of BOTH conditions). `vm_cfg.boolean_regions` detects a K‚â•2 region (K cond blocks + exactly 2 value blocks + 1 merge, single-entry, every branch stays in-region, forward layout); `recover_bool_formula` reconstructs the boolean by recursion over the branch DAG (`formula(block) = (c && reach-true) || (!c && reach-false)` with `_combine_bool` algebraic simplification ‚Üí a clean chain collapses to `c1 && c2 ‚Ä¶`). The decode loop captures each cond at its branch + each value, builds `(formula ? a : b)` at the merge (`_bool_ternary_expr` simplifies `(B?1:0)`‚Üí`B`); `bytecode_cfg` contracts the WHOLE region entry‚Üímerge. **14 regions folded (incl. 2/3/4/6-condition).** `is_tile_in_bounds` = one line `return (arg1<=10 && arg2<=4)`; the 4-cond `$970A` = `return !(x<xmin || x>xmax || y<ymin || y>ymax)` (combat-arena containment). Same gate-blind-spot as the rest ‚Üí **`probe-ternary-folds.py` gained `is_tile_in_bounds`** as an oracle fixture (a wrong &&/||/negation flips the truth table; ORACLE-CONFIRMED 8/8). Gates green, **fallbacks still 35**; test-vm-cfg 86‚Üí94 (region detected / `&&` emitted / witness ~= CONTRACTED / != UNcontracted). **TOTAL value-selection folds now 67 (53 diamond + 14 region); empty-if/else 72‚Üí43.** ‚ñ∂ REMAINING (SAFE honest gotos): 5 boolean regions excluded by single-entry/forward guards + 2 backward-layout diamonds + the cosmetic `if(C){}else{body}` invert / trailing-empty-else drop. - ~~**Extend var-walk to far-frame locals `*(word*)(fp ¬± N)`**~~ **PLUMBING + PILOT DONE 2026-06-03.** Subs with >12 locals or odd-aligned slots address spill locals as raw `*(word*)(fp - 38)`. Now nameable end-to-end: (1) **schema** ‚Äî `[vars.bankN."0xADDR"]` accepts quoted far keys `"fp-38"`/`"fp+40"` (`load_var_names` slot_re + `var-walk-apply.py` SLOT_RE + writer quotes them, `+` isn't a TOML bare-key char); (2) **substitution** ‚Äî `apply_var_names` (the existing LAST text-pass at `vm_decompile.py:1065`, NOT render-site ‚Äî keeps it one mechanism, no module global) replaces the whole rendered lvalue: deref `*(word|byte*)(fp - 38)` ‚Üí `name`, address-of `(fp - 38)` ‚Üí `&name`; derefs for all keys first, then bare addr, closing-paren-anchored so `fp - 3` can't prefix-match `fp - 38`, and nested derefs resolve inner-first; (3) **guard** ‚Äî `walk_guard.norm_lines` collapses the three far forms to `ID`/`&ID` so a far substitution reads as a pure rename (else the guard false-flags expression‚Üíidentifier as a logic change). **Pilot:** `draw_daimyo_portrait` ($E76F) 4 spill locals ‚Üí `pal_idx`/`descriptor_buf`/`descriptor_ptr`/`face_buf`; body now reads as source (`if (pal_idx >= 4) goto`, `syscall16_sram_wrap(8, descriptor_ptr, &descriptor_buf, 4)`, `unpack_composite_face_record(&face_buf)`). **Inert with no far keys (decompiled byte-identical); all gates green** (round-trip 495/45024 CLEAN, --check 0 BAD, drift-guard CLEAN, regen-guard reads it as pure rename). **Census of the SWEEP remaining: ~35 subs / ~77 distinct slots / ~311 refs** ‚Äî bank_00 6/9, bank_01 5/16, bank_02 3/12, **bank_15 21/40** (heaviest: `format_string` 10, `redraw_window` 3; `draw_daimyo_portrait` done). **Two design findings for the sweep ‚Üì (next two tickets).** [[project_nobunaga_daimyo_portraits]]
- ~~**‚ñ∂ FAR-FRAME SWEEP**~~ **COMPLETE 2026-06-03 ‚Äî all 4 banks, `--far` reports 0 remaining everywhere.** Tooling: (1) **`var-walk-apply.py --merge`** ‚Äî per-SLOT collision instead of per-sub refuse; splices slot lines into a sub's EXISTING `[vars.*]` section (or creates one). `render_block` split into `render_slot_lines` + `section_span`/`existing_slot_keys` (parse named `"fp-N" = {` AND left-positional `# fp-N left positional`). (2) **`var-walk-prep.py --far`** ‚Äî surfaces raw `*(word*)(fp - N)` as keys `fp-38` with per-SLOT done-tracking (`recorded_slots`); **NEGATIVE offsets only** (in this VM locals grow downward, so positives are args arg1=fp+11 ‚Ä¶ arg5=fp+19 ‚Ä¶ or frame-header, never spill locals ‚Äî this subsumed the old +11..+17 note); `FAR_SEEDS` role vocabulary. **Sweep RUN (single-agent `/var-walk`, 4 Workflows, 20 agents): 55 far slots named across 24 subs** (4 pilot + 51 swept: bank_00 8/5, bank_01 14/4, bank_02 9/2, bank_15 20/9), one commit per bank, every gate green per bank (round-trip 495/45024, --check 0 BAD, drift-guard, regen pure-rename). **Highlights now readable as source:** `format_string` = full printf engine (`vararg_ptr/width/pad/has_precision/fmt_cursor/ch`); `bfs_path_distance_to_target` = `dist_grid`(11√ó5)/`queue`/`queue_end` ring buffer; `resolve_siege_assault_outcome` defender pointer chain; `build_blit_fief_tile_block` tile assembly. **1 coordinator-AMEND:** single-agent mode mislabeled `atoi_decimal` fp-3 `cursor_ptr` (its summary described arg1) ‚Üí corrected to `digit` via independent C re-read ‚Äî a single-agent verification miss the coordinator-verifier caught ([[feedback_coordinator_subagent_context_transfer]]: coordinator = single writer + verifier). - ~~**‚ñ∂ POSITIVE `*(word*)(fp + N)` (N‚â•11) are ARGS via the general signed-offset opcode, rendered raw**~~ **DONE 2026-06-03 (teardown task "C").** arg1 = fp+0x0B = +11, arg2 = +13 ‚Ä¶ argN = +0x0B+2¬∑(N‚àí1). - ~~**EXPORT THE BUILT-IN TEXT FONT (CHR-RAM glyph set)**~~ **DONE 2026-06-02 ‚Äî `tools/render-text.py`.** The font is **bank-0 `$B2BA`** (2bpp CHR; uploaded to CHR-RAM by `render_boot_title_screens $88AC` via `ppu_upload_block_wrap(81,$1000,$B2BA,0)` right before the first menu text is drawn ‚Äî found by reading the title-sequence VM, not the static upload list). Char‚Üítile = `char_classify $CDCA`, **piecewise** (the font drops some punctuation between ASCII runs, so offsets differ per range): digits `c‚àí40`, upper `c‚àí43`, lower `c‚àí47`, named punctuation explicit. `render-text.py "STRING"` renders any text in the game font (PNG, configurable fg/scale; `--atlas` dumps the glyph set ‚Üí `atlas/font-glyphs.png`); `from render_text import render_text` for import. **Wired into `build-command-page.py index`** ‚Äî the command numbers + names + "LORD COMMANDS" title on `commands/index.html` are now drawn in the cartridge's own font (45 embedded PNGs). The static hunt below is preserved for the record. [[project-nobunaga-visual-extraction]]
  - *(static-hunt postmortem, kept as a lesson)* goal was: export the cartridge's built-in font (used for ~all nametable text) so we can render labels (e.g. the command-index numbers/names) in the authentic game font. **PIPELINE FULLY DECODED this session:** `format_string $CFFC` (printf-style, builds an ASCII buffer; `%C/%D/%S`, `num_to_ascii $CF98`) ‚Üí `redraw_window $CEC9` / `char_advance_width $CE81` (putstring) ‚Üí **`char_classify $CDCA`** maps each ASCII byte ‚Üí tile index, essentially **`tile = ascii ‚àí 40`** (digits '0'=48‚Üí8, 'A'=65‚Üí25, 'a'=97‚Üí57, 'z'=122‚Üí82; punctuation via a switch) ‚Üí glyph blitted from the pattern table via `syscall_ppu_blit_nobank` / `syscall_ppu_blit_from_bank`. So the font occupies **PT1 tiles ~8‚Äì82** and is **CHR-RAM** (cart is CHR-RAM, iNES byte5=0) uploaded at boot. ‚öÝÔ∏è **STATIC HUNT FAILED** ‚Äî decoded every `ppu_upload_block_wrap(count,dst,src,bank)` site (banks 0/1/2/15): the $1000-dst uploads are all fullscreen graphics ($9D04/$AF64/$B2BA bank6/0 = title/victory screens; $AC4A bank0 = the "KOEI PRESENTS/NOBUNAGA" logo graphic), NOT a clean glyph grid; the font is NOT in a simple block in bank 4 (that's map/terrain tiles). The font likely loads via the **multi-phase `display_fullscreen_graphic_sequence $8003`** or a reset-path loop (`reset_ppu_init $C757` uploads only $30 B = palette). **DO: runtime CHR-RAM capture** ‚Äî `run-animation.py` already has the machinery (`chr_ram = bytearray(0x2000)`, intercepts `PPU_UPLOAD_WRAP $CF7C` with `(bank,src,dst,count)` from the VM stack, `count*16` bytes 2bpp). Build `tools/dump-chr.py`: drive the boot/title/menu init in the emulator, accumulate chr_ram, slice tiles 8‚Äì82 ‚Üí the font; then a `render-text.py` that lays a string via `tile=ascii‚àí40` for NES-authentic labels. Swap the monospace stand-in in `commands/index.html` (the `.fontnote` block flags this). Reusable "dump CHR-RAM" tool = bonus (helps the strategic-map render task too). [[project-nobunaga-visual-extraction]]

- ~~**EMULATOR RNG STUB IS A NO-OP ‚Äî blocks probing every RNG-dependent formula**~~ **FIXED 2026-06-02** (`nobunaga_vm.py` `_syscall_dispatch` task $11). The rng syscall stub advanced an LCG and wrote brk_scratch ($66/$67) but returned `None`, so regL was never set ‚Äî `rng_next_wrapper` (just `push $11; syscall; RETURN`) left a leftover in regL and `rng_mod`'s SIGNED `SMOD` produced negatives (`-13752 smod 10 = -2`). Fix: the stub now returns the LCG value masked to 15 bits (`& 0x7FFF`, non-negative so SMOD yields a clean 0..n-1 for every modulus the game uses ‚â§ ~2025). **Verified end-to-end:** `probe-espionage.py` ninja-drain bands now match `{5,10,‚Ä¶,X√ó5}` exactly across the rng distribution; probe-math32 + run-effect grow unaffected (no rng there). **This unblocks emulator-probing every RNG-dependent formula** (drains, defection size, event spawns, combat rolls). [[feedback_silent_tool_failure_hallucination]]-adjacent: a stub that silently returns None reads as "no input," not "broken."
- **VM CALL frame-arg mapping is REVERSE push order** (confirmed 2026-06-02): the LAST-pushed call arg lands in frame slot `fp+0x0B` = the callee's `operand $0C` ("arg1"). Evidence: the `$8BD0 DEREF` only works on the pointer arg (which is 2nd-pushed) + probe-math32's documented reversal note. **This flipped the bribe contest direction to the intuitive one** (see Now). Keep in mind when hand-reading any multi-arg sub: the decompiler's `local12/local13` are the reverse of source push order. **NOW ORACLE-CONFIRMED 2026-06-02** (executed a real `$E9 CALL`): args are purely stack-passed (zero-copy ‚Äî CALL repoints `fp` so `fp+0x0B‚Ä¶` overlap the caller's pushed args; regB is NOT an arg-passing register). Captured during the frame-arg `?` fix (see Now ‚úÖ).
- **‚ñ∂ NAMED FRAME VARIABLES ‚Äî "var-walk" / the 3rd sibling (Chris, 2026-06-02)** ‚Äî replace positional `arg1‚Äìarg4` + `local0‚Äìlocal11` with semantic names (`fief`, `amount`, `drain_pct`, ‚Ä¶). Chris's worry: args live on the STACK, not a static address, so we can't label them like a data table. **Resolution: the name comes from ROLE, not location** ‚Äî recoverable two ways now that pushes are modeled correctly: (a) **usage role-inference** inside the body (`argN->output` ‚áí province ptr; `daimyo_record_ptr(argN)` ‚áí daimyo idx; `pct_op(argN,‚Ä¶)` ‚áí percent); (b) **caller propagation** ‚Äî every call site now shows the real expression pushed into each slot (e.g. callers always push `selected_province_idx` ‚áí that arg is a province idx). Same multi-pass back-inference as [[project_nobunaga_label_walk_skill]] / [[project_nobunaga_data_walk_skill]], aimed at frame slots. Storage: per-function arg/local table in `mesen-labels.toml` keyed `(sub, slot)` (e.g. `[args.bank01.$87F0]`); `vm_decompile.py` substitutes like it does sub/data labels. **DEPENDENCY: do the VM-teardown display-order fix FIRST** ‚Äî else caller-propagation maps the pushed expr onto the wrong slot number (reverse-push). `local0‚Äì11` is the bigger win by volume than args. Pass-2 / post-combat. The "variable naming" limitation noted in [[project_nobunaga_vm_decompiler]] is exactly this.
- **‚ñ∂ ENGINE PROVING-GROUNDS (Chris, 2026-06-02, "maybe a test or 2")** ‚Äî two ideas to validate the decompiler/VM toolchain is a real *engine*, not a one-off. (a) **C ‚Üí bytecode round-trip**: compile the decompiled C back to Sea-16 bytecode, assert byte-identical to ROM ‚Üí proves the decompiler is lossless + the VM model complete (the ultimate regen-guard). (b) **Cross-game one-shot**: take another KOEI/Sea-16-era title, verify it runs the SAME VM (opcode table/ABI match), then try to one-shot the disassembly with the existing tools. Both are post-pass-1 stretch goals, not committed ‚Äî capture only. Pairs with the VM teardown (a complete opcode model is the prerequisite for both).
- **‚ñ∂ END-OF-PROJECT VM TEARDOWN (Chris, 2026-06-02)** ‚Äî register/variable/stack tracking in the Sea-16 VM is "weird and hard to keep track of." Once the subsystems are done, a dedicated **byte-by-byte pass**: every opcode's true semantics ($E8‚Äì$FF handler set), the full ABI, the **reverse-push display-order quirk** in `vm_decompile.py` (multi-arg calls show `f(c,b,a)`), cleanup of the now-DEAD `recent_pos_writes`/`/*via argN*/` fallback, and any other stateful/mis-modeled opcodes. Seed evidence = this session's oracle traces (`$E9` CALL ABI, `$30‚Äì$3F`=`PUSH_quick`). Goal: decompiled C that reads naturally with ZERO `?` and no tool round-trips. Spawned from the frame-arg `?` fix, which proved one mis-modeled opcode ($30‚Äì$3F) was responsible for 996 markers ‚Äî there may be more.
  - **‚ñ∂ Task "D" ‚Äî the VM/decompiler WIKI writeup (do AFTER the control-flow structuring epic, so it shows clean `while`/`if`/`switch` C).** **Material sufficiency CHECKED 2026-06-03: abundant ‚Äî every fact captured + cross-checked by Pass 2.** Narrative home already exists (chapters `05-bytecode-vm.md` / `06-vm-disassembler.md` / `08-vm-instruction-set.md` + the `build-*.py`‚ÜíHTML wiki precedent), so D is **NOT greenfield**. ‚öÝÔ∏è **BUT those 3 chapters are stale May-13/14 drafts (pre-Pass-2)** ‚Äî staleness measured by grep of post-validation terms: ch6=**0 hits**, ch5=1, ch8=6. Ch6 predates the vm-disasm REBUILD entirely; none cover round-trip / stack-audit / `$30-$3F` fix / reverse-push / table-driven dispatch / var-walk. **So D = RECONCILE-AND-REWRITE, not assembly:** treat the VALIDATED ARTIFACTS as authority and CORRECT the drafts (same trap combat ch14/17 + AI ch12 hit ‚Äî early docs contained claims later overturned; [[feedback_documented_vs_actual_behavior]]). **Source manifest (write FROM these):** *VM-arch* ‚Üê CONTEXT glossary + `vm_stack_effect.py` header (stack model: descending word stack `$02`, regL `$08`, regR `$0C`) + `vm-opcodes-v2.toml` header + M3 ABI (CALL frame-args/reverse-push/frame layout). *Toolchain* ‚Üê `vm_decompile.py` docstring + table-driven dispatch + `vm-disasm.py` header (length authority, `$D5/$D9`, exact-tiling) + `decompiled/README.md` + "See the whole picture" EPIC + the `$30-$3F`/arg5+ fix stories. *Instruction set* ‚Üê `vm-opcodes-v2.toml` (the 256-op spec + `verified=`) IS the table + `STACK_EFFECT` + the audit (184/208) + `EXT_OP_TABLE`/math32. **Biggest ADD the drafts lack = the VALIDATION/TRUST narrative** (round-trip byte-identical + audit-vs-live-handler + drift-guard) ‚Äî turns "what we think the VM does" into "what's proven"; it's the spine of credible pages.
  - ~~**Task "C" ‚Äî positive args (arg5+) + real arity**~~ **DONE 2026-06-03** (see Done). Last raw `fp¬±N` in the C eliminated.
  - ~~**Task "A" ‚Äî table-driven dispatch (family consolidation)**~~ **DONE 2026-06-03.** The literal "decompiler reads a table to drive dispatch" rewrite M3 deferred ‚Äî done for the **mechanical opcode families** (the ~50 near-identical `regA = <formula of regA/regB>` arms). Three data tables + two generic blocks now replace them: `_BINOP` (arith/compare/logic/shift-by-reg, with a `none`/`both`/`lhs` signedness-cast field), `_UNARY_A` (inc/dec/shift-by-1/zero-test/negate/deref templates), and `_op_hex`/`_op_int` operand-parse helpers (killed ~14 copies of the `re.search` idiom). **Net ‚àí45 lines in `vm_decompile.py`** (‚àí129/+84 incl. tables+comments). Caught + dropped a **dead duplicate `div` arm** (two `'div'` keys; first=unsigned won, second=signed never fired ‚Üí preserved unsigned). Pure refactor: **decompiled/*.c BYTE-IDENTICAL** (empty diff after each of 3 verified chunks); round-trip 495/45024 CLEAN, --check 0 BAD √ó4, drift-guard CLEAN. **Deliberately NOT consolidated** (kept as explicit named handlers ‚Äî they're genuinely one-of-a-kind or irregular, so table-driving would *reduce* readability, against "high-quality not more code"): `host_call`/indirect (arity_map), `switch` (comment-parse), `ext_op` ($B7 EXT_OP_TABLE, the only live un-gated op, 49 sites), the general frame-access `$81-$88`/`$A0-$A3` block, branches/jumps/return, and the frame-local quick loads `$00-$3F` (storeA_local_neg also tracks `state.locals`, breaking family uniformity). **Skipped Task "B"** (opcode `verified=` coverage): the audit proved the only un-gated opcode with real sites is `$B7` (already modeled); the other ~24 are 0-site, so verifying them is spec-completeness for the deferred cross-game proof, not a teardown blocker.
- **RUN THE REST OF THE BANKS FOR LABELS** (Chris, 2026-06-01) ‚Äî banks 3-14 are DATA (0 bytecode subs, so /label-walk doesn't apply), but we want named labels we can USE when tracing. Approach: a **/data-walk** sweep over the data banks ‚Äî name the big tables/blobs by the named code that references them (cross-bank pointers like the portrait case: the referencing sub is in bank 0/1/2/15, the data is in bank 3-14). Needs rom-xref to resolve the cross-bank pointer's TARGET bank (the ppu_upload/memcpy_banked bank arg), not assume same-bank ‚Äî that's the limitation the portrait find surfaced. Bank 8 = portrait/face graphics (started). Likely others: map tiles, text/font, sprite/unit graphics, audio (bank 10). Good standing task to make traces readable.
- ~~**PORTRAIT ‚Äî SHELVED 2026-06-01**~~ **RESOLVED 2026-06-01 ‚Äî and the old premise was WRONG.** Historical daimyo's fixed faces do NOT come from a preset base-5 face code in $6EB1 + the composite system. They use a **separate DEDICATED-CHR preset path** (hand-drawn portraits in banks 7-8 via the `$BBD0` descriptor table ‚Äî see the ‚úÖ in Now). `$6EB1` (the base-5 composite code) is written ONLY by `assign_unique_daimyo_face_code` ($DB97) on succession ‚Äî i.e. the composite system is for RNG-generated REPLACEMENT daimyo only, never the canonical roster. The `record[+6]` status byte (0=original‚Üípreset, 1=generated‚Üícomposite) selects the path. Anthologies rendered: `atlas/daimyo-anthology-{17,50}.png`. [[project_nobunaga_daimyo_portraits]]

- ~~**B7 extended-opcode table ‚Äî CHECK NESDEV FORUMS before deriving**~~ ‚Äî **CLOSED 2026-05-31 (native walk increment 4, no forum needed).** The table is `ext_op_table` ($F263), dispatched by `ext_op_dispatch` ($F246, VM opcode $AB); its ~44 entries point at the 16/32-bit math/logic/bitfield runtime in $EC-$F6, now all named in `mesen-labels.toml` (umul32/udiv32/cmp32/bitfield/etc.). Decoded straight from THIS ROM's disasm ‚Äî the nesdev t=15931 lookup turned out unnecessary. The 3 composite helpers ([[project_nobunaga_math32_cracked]]) remain the formula interface; the individual sub-ops are now readable too for the decompiler's `// TODO:` reduction.
- **Minimal live PPU memory model ‚Äî for the rendering/animation arc, NOT logic** (Chris, 2026-05-30) ‚Äî idea: stop fully stubbing PPU writes and instead keep PPU-side memory live (nametable, palette, OAM, CHR). **Verdict: red herring for mechanics/logic decode** (game logic never reads PPU back; the data path is ROM/SRAM ‚Üí compute ‚Üí CPU-RAM *shadow* buffers ($0600 OAM/$0700 palette/$7BFD map staging) ‚Üí blit syscalls ($01/$14/$0C/$0D) ‚Üí PPU, and we already intercept at the shadow/staging level ‚Äî PPU is a write-only output sink, only $2002 status is timing, already handled by `wait_for_nmi`). **But genuinely valuable for the *visual* arc.** Two paths to ROM‚ÜíMap: **(A)** decode the `$7BFD` staging buffer ourselves ‚Üí render via the existing metatile renderer (89% working, zero PPU needed ‚Äî use this for the immediate ROM‚ÜíMap tool); **(B)** implement a minimal PPU model (2KB nametable + palette RAM + `$2006/$2007` latch + the `$14`/`$01` blit syscalls), run the real render path, and read the final nametable = exactly what the game draws. **Key fact: this cart is CHR-RAM (iNES byte5=0), not CHR-ROM** ‚Äî tile bitmaps are *uploaded* by the CPU, not static in ROM, so pixel-exact rendering LATER (animation chapter) will need to capture CHR-RAM the upload routines produce. **Cheap experiment worth doing before grinding Path A's last 11%:** stand up just nametable + `$2006/$2007` + `$14` blit, run full `$AFE1`, see if the final nametable is a complete map ‚Äî if so, Path B may be the *cleaner* ROM‚ÜíMap (reuses `$885E`/`$CC54`'s own metatile expansion). Defer the full model to the animation/display chapter.
- ~~**Decompiler enhancement ‚Äî indexed-base label resolution**~~ ‚Äî **DONE 2026-05-30** (`annotate_array_access`): `*(byte*)((idx + 0xNNNN))` ‚Üí `array_label[idx]` when `0xNNNN` is labeled (byte derefs, non-strided index; word-stride records stay with `annotate_field_access`). `ui_helper_d772` now reads `return fief_to_daimyo_map[arg1]`, etc. Propagates automatically as array bases get labeled.
- ~~**`native-call-index.py` misses VM-internal bytecode CALL edges**~~ ‚Äî **CLOSED 2026-06-01 (label-walk automation pass).** Root cause was worse than "misses some edges": `VM_HOSTCALL_RE` matched only an **obsolete `host_call` mnemonic (0 occurrences in today's disasm)** instead of the live `CALL_abs`/`CALL_abs_imm1` form (2400+ edges) ‚Äî so the ENTIRE bytecode call graph was absent, which is why every bank_00 batch's verifiers got "0 callers" and recovered via grep, AND why `--by-callgraph` clustering had been silently falling back to ~address order. Fixed `parse_bytecode` (`VM_CALL_RE` matches both forms). Verified: `callers 8377` ‚Üí `init_daimyo_arms_record √ó4`; `stats` shows `call_abs 2415`. Leaves-first clustering is now genuinely call-graph-driven.
- **Data-element labeling via code back-reference ‚Äî the variable-side twin of the label-walk** (Chris, 2026-06-01) ‚Äî the asm dumps carry DATA sections (blobs/tables) that code references; a named function infers its data. E.g. a `play_growth_animation` sub that references `blob_999` ‚üπ `blob_999` is the growth animation; that label then propagates to every other referencer (same multi-pass-linker / toml-as-hub trick as the code walk, [[feedback_re_is_multipass_compilation]]). Builds on the captured "who-reads/writes $addr data-xref tool" nicety (the variable-side of `native-call-index`) ‚Äî that tool is the enabler. Not urgent; the natural FOLLOW-ON after the code banks are named (bank_02 next). Could become a `data-walk` sibling skill. Several hot DATA addrs already queued for labels (Session C list: `$6DA2/$76A9/$6193/$6D2D/$6E4A/$F930-$F95D`).
- **Committed `disasm/*_vm.asm` carry stale per-line annotations for `$40-$4F`** (captured 2026-06-01 during the qimm fix) ‚Äî the `.asm` listings (hand-curated semantic comments, generated by an older tool rev) still show `$46 clearA ; regA = 0 (shared handler $E9F6)`, whereas current `OPCODE_INFO` correctly says `LOADL_qimm` and the handler is `regA = opcode&0xF`. **Cosmetic + the decompiler is immune** (it reads opcode BYTES not the listing mnemonic, see `vm_decompile.py:170-172`), and each line already prints the true `inline operand = N`. The fix is a disasm regen, but that risks losing the hand-curated `; <semantic>` comments ‚Üí defer until a deliberate disasm-refresh pass. Not blocking anything.

- **Build animation may be NAMETABLE-driven, not metasprite** (Chris, 2026-06-02) ‚Äî Chris's read: the house *frame* is a static picture and the motion is a **nametable rewrite at the top of the original picture**, not the sprite/CHR motion the anim-VM models. Evidence: `run-animation.py 24` renders only **2 frames / 1 CHR upload** ‚Äî suspiciously thin. The animation VM intercepts CHR upload / palette / set_sprite but likely does NOT model a per-frame nametable-region rewrite. ACTION: capture Build in-game (Mesen) to see the real motion; if confirmed, the anim tool needs a nametable-write capture path (ties into the parked minimal-PPU-model idea). May affect other "scene" animations too.
- **Tax-DOWN animation (id 18) vs id 19** (Chris, 2026-06-02) ‚Äî the tax driver plays **id 19** on a raise ("peasants protesting") and **id 18** on a cut ("peasants delighted"). The two share `data_src $BE8A` but have DIFFERENT command streams ($AED8 vs $AEE7), so 18 is NOT literally 19-reversed ‚Äî likely distinct motion. Quick `run-animation.py 18` + in-game capture to characterize; minor, fun.
- **Grow-vs-Dam decision rule ‚Äî DERIVE the switch** (Chris, 2026-06-02) ‚Äî now both formulas are exact. Marginal-rice analysis (both feed `output√ódams` in the harvest): Grow Œîrice ‚àù `dams √ó 10¬∑amt/‚àöoutput`, Dam Œîrice ‚àù `output √ó 2¬∑amt/‚àöoutput` ‚Üí ratio `5¬∑dams/output` ‚Üí **crossover at output = 5√ódams** (Grow below, Dam above; Dam also drain-free while Grow bleeds loy+dams; dams caps 100 so output>500 forces Grow). ‚öÝÔ∏è This SUPERSEDES the older `output¬≤ > 38√ódams` heuristic in [[project_nobunaga_dam_doctrine]] ‚Äî reconcile + bake the `output‚âà5¬∑dams` rule into `econ_sim.py` and the doctrine. (Quick win, high strategic value.)
- **Give turn-economy: sell-rice‚Üígive-gold vs give-rice-direct** (Chris, 2026-06-02) ‚Äî Give treats gold and rice **1:1** (gain depends on quantity, not resource), but the MARKET sells rice at ~2 gold. So: (a) rice is the cheaper "give currency" ‚Üí give rice directly when you have it; (b) Chris's reverse ‚Äî sell 1 rice‚Üí2 gold‚Üígive 2 gold ‚âà ~2√ó the loyalty ‚Äî is real but costs a TURN + needs the merchant present (turn-economy thesis: 4 slots/yr is the binding constraint, so this usually loses). Model when the merchant+turn cost is worth it; a nice edge case for the optimizer.

> **Sea-16 VM**. Plan file: `~/.claude/plans/quizzical-hugging-hearth.md`. Decided scope (Chris, auto mode,
> rest-between-steps OK): push from VM validation through to the var-walk, as a ladder of deterministic gates.

> byte-identical round-trip is **shelved as a real future proving-grounds milestone** (gated on a lossless
> decompiler ‚Äî goto-structuring), not dropped.

>   operand-layout + length + endianness model is provably complete & correct. Both tools registered in tools/README.
> - **‚úÖ M2 ‚Äî RUNG 2 (emulator stack-effect / MEANING audit) ‚Äî DONE 2026-06-03.** New `tools/vm_stack_effect.py`
>   (the single per-opcode `STACK_EFFECT` authority ‚Äî pops/pushes/reg/class, extracted from the `vm_decompile.py`
>   dispatch, NOT re-guessed) + `tools/vm-stack-audit.py` (drives every opcode occurrence through the **live ROM
>   handler** `step_one_vm_op` and asserts observed SP/regL/regR/depth deltas match the table + qimm/abs value-checks).

>   `$30-$3F`-class meaning bug is provably absent. `verified=` in `vm-opcodes-v2.toml` driven **18 ‚Üí 75** (`--write-toml`
>   added pops/pushes + verified to confirmed sections; 14 unobserved + 12 probe sections honestly noted, not faked).
>   **Findings the audit surfaced (model corrections vs the decompiler's claims):** POPSTORE `$B1`/`$D4` pop the
>   pointer INTO regR (regR clobbered, not kept); shifts `$BD/$BE/$BF` consume regR as a decrementing count (clobbered);
>   table-switches `$D5`/`$D9` scratch both regs. RETURN `$CF` can't be isolated (no caller) ‚Üí validated via a paired
>   CALL‚ÜíRETURN micro-test; `$DD`/`$EA` need a valid regL target. `$B2` left **probe** (OPCODE_INFO=NOP vs decompiler=PUSHL
>   ‚Äî observed dSP varies, deferred to M3). Decompiler + `decompiled/*.c` untouched (M2 is pure validation); `--check`
>   + round-trip still green. Tools registered in tools/README.
> - **‚úÖ M3 ‚Äî VM teardown corrections ‚Äî DONE 2026-06-03.** Five fixes to `vm_decompile.py`, all gated
>   (round-trip + `--check` + audit stay green; regen-guard diff is intended-only, proven token-preserving):
>   - **Reverse-push display FIXED.** Dropped the `args.reverse()` in both call paths (host_call + indirect) so
>     call-site arg order matches callee param numbering (arg1 = last-pushed = first-popped). `effect_grow` now reads
>     the verified formula left-to-right: `math32_3arg(arg2, (6-const_two), sqrt_int(output+arg2)) << 1`. Independently

>     Regen-guard: every non-signature changed line is a pure token-preserving permutation; **0 structural changes**.
>   - **Real per-function arg counts.** Signatures now declare the true arity (`_body_arg_count`: highest arg slot the
>     body references via the quick arg-opcodes) instead of hardcoded `arg1..arg4`. Distribution over 495 subs:
>     195 `void`, 153√ó1, 113√ó2, 25√ó3, 9√ó4. **Chose body-usage over caller-arity** (deterministic per-sub ‚Üí bank_NN.c

>     decompiler's PUSHL was wrong (harmless: never emitted). Fixed decompiler ($B2‚Üí`nop_B2`), toml `[op_B2]` ‚Üí
>     `verified=true`, `vm_stack_effect` note. **BONUS: the reverse-push fix surfaced a syscall-resolution bug** ‚Äî
>     `annotate_syscall` read the syscall ID from the *trailing* arg (only true under the old reversed display); now
>     reads it from the *leading* arg, so wrappers render `syscall_memcpy_banked(arg1,arg2,arg3,arg4)` (friendly name
>     + natural order) instead of the raw `syscall_dispatch(16, ‚Ä¶)`.
>   - **STACK_EFFECT integration ‚Üí bounded DRIFT-GUARD** (full table-driven rewrite DEFERRED to the teardown, Chris's
>     call). `py -3 tools/decompile-all.py --self-check`: with `vm_decompile.SELF_CHECK` on, the decompiler logs the
>     data-stack depth per instruction (top-of-loop ‚Üí `continue`-proof; default-off ‚Üí production C byte-identical),
>     and `check_stack_trace()` asserts each gated opcode's OBSERVED Œî (from the REAL handlers ‚Äî no parallel table)
>     matches `vm_stack_effect.STACK_EFFECT`. **CLEAN: 179 gated opcodes, 0 exclusions.** Negative-tested: injecting a
>     push-as-noop bug fires on all 12 `$30-$3B` (+ cascade). This is the standing guard against the next $30-$3F/$B2
>     bug class; the literal "decompiler READS the table to drive dispatch" rewrite lives in the teardown ticket.

> - **üü¢ M4 ‚Äî var-walk (Layer 2) ‚Äî PLUMBING + PILOT DONE 2026-06-03.** The mechanism is built and
>   proven end-to-end on `effect_grow` (bank1 `$87F0`). **Storage:** `[vars.bankN."0xADDR"]` sections in
>   `mesen-labels.toml` ‚Äî one `slot = { name="...", comment }` line per renamed frame slot (the variable-side twin
>   of `[prg.*]`). **Decompiler:** `vm_decompile.load_var_names()` parses them; `apply_var_names()` runs as the LAST
>   emit pass (after `annotate_field_access` et al. form `arg1->output`, so the base just gets renamed ‚Üí
>   `fief->output`); `decompile-all.py` threads the per-sub dict (module-level `VAR_NAMES`) so `bank_NN.c` AND the
>   merged `all_banks.c` get identical renames. Single-pass word-bounded alternation (no cascade; `local1` can't eat
>   `local11`). **Pilot result:** `effect_grow(word fief, word amount)` with `gain` for the output-gain slot now reads
>   the verified formula as source: `gain = math32_3arg(amount,(6-const_two),sqrt_int(fief->output+amount))<<1; ‚Ä¶
>   fief->output += gain; return gain/2;`. **Design rule surfaced + adopted:** ONLY name a slot with ONE coherent role
>   ‚Äî `local10` (reused scratch: headroom, then drain%/2) was correctly LEFT positional as the honest scratch signal.
>   **Guards all green** (isolated M4-only delta = effect_grow alone in both views, pure renames; round-trip 495/45024
>   CLEAN; `--check` 0 BAD; drift-guard CLEAN; `mesen-labels.py` tolerates `[vars.*]`).
>   **NEXT:** crystallize a `/var-walk` skill (3rd sibling to `/label-walk` + `/data-walk`) and fan out ‚Äî
>   `local0-11` is the bigger win by volume than args. Role-inference lanes: (a) usage-role in the body
>   (`argN->output` ‚áí province ptr; `pct_op(argN,‚Ä¶)` ‚áí percent), (b) caller propagation (the expression each caller
>   pushes into the slot, now visible since the M3 reverse-push fix).

> ### ‚úÖ PRESET DAIMYO PORTRAITS ‚Äî CRACKED + ANTHOLOGY RENDERED 2026-06-01 (`render-portrait.py anthology`)
> The pinned task is DONE. The preset (historical-daimyo) path in `draw_daimyo_portrait` ($E76F, `record[+6]==0` branch) is fully decoded and the two anthologies render NES-exact with names: `atlas/daimyo-anthology-{17,50}.png` (17 + 50 recognizable faces, real palette).
> - **Descriptor table = bank 8 `$BBD0`**, **4 bytes/entry** `{chr_bank, tile_count, src_ptr_LE}`, indexed by `fief_to_mapid(fief)` (the `*4` is the 4-byte stride; the `len=8` syscall copy just over-reads the next entry harmlessly ‚Äî so the "8-byte descriptor" framing was wrong). Self-validating: each entry's `src + count*16` = the next entry's `src`, chaining cleanly. The decompiler's `msg_ng_to_pieces` resolution was the known cross-bank-pointer trap; real table is bank 8.
> - **Portrait CHR packed contiguously in banks 7-8** (mapid 0-28 ‚Üí bank 7, 29-49 ‚Üí bank 8). `count` ‚âà 28-35 tiles each.
> - **Layout = bank 8 `$B144`, a PER-PORTRAIT 6√ó6 tile-index map at `$B144 + mapid*36`** (the bytecode at `$E7E4` computes `fief_to_mapid*36 + $B144` as the blit's map pointer; the blit `ppu_blit_from_bank_wrap` gets bank-arg 8). CHR uploads to `$15B0` = PT1 tile **`0x5B`**, so map cell `v` ‚Üí uploaded tile `v-0x5B`; `0x5B` = each portrait's background/border filler. ‚öÝÔ∏è **GOTCHA (found via Chris's Miyoshi screenshot):** the map is per-mapid ‚Äî using the FIRST 36 bytes (mapid 0's map) for every portrait renders only Kakizaki correctly and scrambles the rest (face-like but wrong-arrangement = "a couple bad tiles ‚Ä¶ most tiles bad"). Fixed ‚Üí all 17+50 match the game.
> - **Palette = `$F7CC`** (bank 15): 4 NES indices `0x3E,0x38,0x28,0x30` (black/cream/gold/white) ‚Üí BG palette 0.
> - **Names**: bank 3, 9 B/entry ‚Äî 50-fief `$97AB`, 17-fief `$B7AB`. **Mapid mapping**: 50-fief daimyo idx == mapid (identity); 17-fief ‚Üí `province_to_mapid_table $F70E` `[15,9,13,20,21,17,19,23,22,31,26,27,25,30,32,14,24]`. CROSS-CHECK: 17- & 50-fief Oda both resolve to descriptor[24] (same portrait) ‚úì.
> - **OPEN (optional):** add `[prg.bank8]` labels for the `$BBD0` descriptor table + `$B144` template + the bank 7-8 portrait CHR region (currently mis-named `msg_ng_to_pieces`/`jumptab_b144`). And the GENERALIZED "render graphics bits from code" tool (below) would subsume this renderer.
> - **GENERALIZED TOOL IDEA (Chris, 2026-06-01): "render graphics bits from code."** A tool that, given an upload/blit call site (or its `(bank, src, count)` args), extracts + renders the CHR it moves ‚Äî code-driven graphics extraction. Would crack the logo, title, map tiles, etc. in one place; the cross-bank bank-arg resolution is the same primitive the parked "run the data banks for labels" sweep needs. High value, reusable. > ### ‚úÖ THE MAIN TURN LOOP ‚Äî DECODED 2026-06-02 (decode-first; polished format deferred per Chris)
> **`vm_bootstrap $A778` (bank 0) IS the loop**, walked end-to-end & verified vs bytecode (not just the decompiled C). Full writeup: [[project_nobunaga_main_turn_loop]]. Skeleton: init_new_game_state once ‚Üí **per-season loop**: `ai_strategic_turn_planner $A455` (the tick) ‚Üí battle-resume block ‚Üí `spawn_zealot_uprising_force_from_province $A5E6` ‚Üí resolve staged combat (`call_bank_wrap(2)`) ‚Üí `shuffle_fief_turn_order_array $A742` ‚Üí command sub-loop (`call_bank_wrap(1)`‚Üí`ai_per_fief_command_driver $B89B`) ‚Üí game-over‚Üí`display_fullscreen_graphic_sequence`.
> **3 keystone findings (+ 2 label fixes, regen-guard clean):**
> - **Season-phased economy.** `per_period_fief_daimyo_update_driver $A30D` does `switch(current_season)`: **1**=highwater reset, **2**=`harvest_income_sweep_all_fiefs` (THE harvest, once/yr in season 2 ‚Äî confirms the "fall harvest" memory), **3**=relations decay; aging + natural-death + loyalty-decay-to-90% run EVERY season.
> - **`config_block $6D5F` ‚Üí renamed `current_season`** (0-3 counter). `season=(season+1)&3` per period; `current_game_year++` only on wrap to 0 ‚Üí 4 seasons = 1 year. Drives the season switch + planner event-select (season==1) + a kernel switch (bank15 $D68F).
> - **Turn-order array is `$6F1B`, NOT `$6F0B`** ‚Äî the toml label was mis-addressed ($6F0B has ZERO refs). Relocated `daimyo_turn_order` to $6F1B; **fixed a latent bug in `sram-decode-province.py`** (hardcoded the wrong $6F0B). Shuffled each season ($A742), read by command driver ($B918): `selected_province_idx = daimyo_turn_order[ai_per_fief_loop_index]`.
> - **Elegant mechanic ‚Äî the command pass RESUMES across combat.** `ai_per_fief_loop_index $6001` is a persistent global restored into the frame at $B8A4; a mid-pass war saves the index ($B996), bootstrap loops through bank-2 combat, then re-enters and resumes at the next fief. Each fief dispatches on `province_ai_state` (6 Grant policies) ‚Üí AI econ handlers ‚Üí `issue_province_command`; resting daimyo skipped via `rest_turns_remaining`.
> **‚úÖ HTML HUB BUILT 2026-06-02 ‚Äî `tools/build-turn-loop.py` ‚Üí `turn-loop.html`.** The loop as a status-tracked MAP of its 7 phases (badges `dived`/`has page`/`to do` = the remaining-work tracker); command palette + future combat page are the two branches. Reuses `build-command-page.py` CSS via importlib; registry-driven (edit NODES/SEASONS/KEYSTONES + regen, never hand-edit HTML). Chris chose HTML over md: source stays editable, HTML is derived so it can't go stale. **Also emits per-phase deep-dive pages** (`turn-loop-<id>.html`); a node flips `stub‚Üípage` by adding a PHASE_PAGES entry.

> ### ‚úÖ PHASE 0 (init_new_game_state) ‚Äî DEEP-DIVE PAGE DONE 2026-06-02 (`turn-loop-init.html`) + THE SKILL-LEVEL FIND

($8AD6) writes `number_input(1..5)` into it. const_two is NOT a constant; it's a **global difficulty multiplier read in ~35 sites across all 4 banks.** Headline: the 5 develop commands use `(6‚àískill)` as the gain multiplier ‚Üí `Grow gain = 2¬∑‚åäamount¬∑(6‚àískill)/‚àö(output+amount)‚åã`, **emulator-confirmed** (`tools/probe-skill-impact.py`): amount 100 ‚Üí 76/60/46/30/14 for skill 1‚Äì5 (5.4√ó swing). **This solves the long-standing "√ó5" mystery** ‚Äî every early Grow/Build derivation ran at skill default; the "5" was 6‚àí1. Three anti-player pressures from one dial: (1) your economy ~5√ó slower; (2) `apply_scenario_starting_stat_boosts $83E2` buffs **AI-only** daimyo (gated `province_ai_state==0`; daimyo-create marks YOUR fief state 5 Direct ‚Üí excluded ‚Äî CONFIRMED, the recipient question Chris flagged); (3) bigger uprisings `(skill+1)√ó10` + combat casualties `rng(6‚àískill)`. const_two label comment updated with the full footprint + validated formula (comment-only, decompiled byte-identical).

> ### ‚úÖ DECOMPILER FRAME-ARG `?` ‚Äî FIXED 2026-06-02 (ROOT CAUSE = mis-modeled opcode, not a dataflow gap)
> **The "frame-arg ?" turned out to be a one-line semantic BUG, not a heuristic seeding job.** Investigation (oracle-driven, see below) traced ALL of `/*via argN*/ ?` (281) + bare `= ?` (318) + `/*stack underflow*/` (397) ‚Äî **996 markers** ‚Äî to a single cause: the decompiler modeled VM opcodes **`$30‚Äì$3F` as `storeB_local` (store regB ‚Üí slot)** when **`OPCODE_INFO` (the semantics authority) says the whole range is `PUSH_quick`** ‚Äî push a frame slot's VALUE onto the data stack (`$30‚Äì$3B`=push localN, `$3C‚Äì$3F`=push argN, arg-forwarding to a call). The old "store" model both fabricated bogus `argN = ?` assignments AND starved every downstream call of its pushed args (‚Üí the underflows). **Fix:** `tools/vm_decompile.py` ‚Äî remapped `$30‚Äì$3F` to `push_local_neg`/`push_local_pos`, handlers now `state.stack.append(slot_name)`. **RESULT: all 996 markers ‚Üí 0; net ‚àí2058 lines** of decompiled C (the phantom duplicate statements the mis-model produced are gone).
> - **ORACLE-CONFIRMED, not guessed** (`nobunaga_vm` real-stack dumps): executed a real `$E9 CALL` ‚Äî the pushed word lands at new-frame `fp+0x0B`=arg1, NOT regB (kills the "arg1 in regB" red herring; args are purely stack-passed, zero-copy overlap, `adj/2`=argcount). Then single-op traces: `$38` pushes local8 (sp‚àí=2); `$3C` pushes arg1 (fp+0x0B) ‚Ä¶ `$3F` pushes arg4 (fp+0x11) ‚Äî matches `local_name('pos')`. `$2C‚Äì$2F` (STORE_quick) are LEFT as real stores (the `arg1=arg1+1` loop-counter at `$CA88` proves they store) ‚Äî only `$30‚Äì$3F` was wrong.
> - **VALIDATED vs known-good:** `effect_grow` now decompiles to **exactly the verified formula** ‚Äî `math32_3arg(sqrt(o+a),(6‚àískill),amount)` reads (through the decompiler's pre-existing reverse-push display convention) as `‚åäamount¬∑(6‚àískill)/‚àö(output+amount)‚åã`; the old output had `arg2 = const_two` *corrupting the amount* + phantom `local10 = 2` / duplicate `pct_op` lines ‚Äî all gone. The `apply_unit_damage_over_30` loop (bank-2, was riddled with `?`) now reads cleanly (`unit_record_ptr(local8)`, real `local9/10`). Only files touched: `vm_decompile.py` + `decompiled/*.c`.
> - **Tech debt noted:** the `recent_pos_writes` / `/*via argN*/` host_call fallback in `vm_decompile.py` is now DEAD (never populates, never fires) ‚Äî harmless safety net, leave for the teardown. The **reverse-push display order** for multi-arg calls (`math32_3arg(c,b,a)` shows reversed) is a separate pre-existing readability quirk ‚Äî candidate for the teardown, NOT bundled here (would change arg-order interpretation project-wide).
> - **NOT chased (still true): full control-flow STRUCTURING** (the ~1437 gotos ‚Üí if/else/loop). Genuinely hard; gotos are readable-with-effort; bytecode/emulator settle ambiguity in seconds. [[feedback_transpilation_as_grounding]] [[feedback_re_is_multipass_compilation]] [[project_nobunaga_vm_decompiler]]
> - **‚ñ∂ CAPTURED TASK (Chris, 2026-06-02): END-OF-PROJECT VM TEARDOWN.** Register/variable/stack tracking is "weird and hard to keep track of" ‚Äî once the subsystems are done, do a dedicated **byte-by-byte VM pass**: pick apart the Sea-16 VM opcode by opcode + variable by variable (ABI, the full `$E8‚Äì$FF` handler set, the reverse-push display convention, the dead `recent_pos_writes` cleanup, any remaining stateful opcodes). The oracle traces gathered this session ($E9 CALL ABI, $30‚Äì$3F PUSH_quick) are the seed evidence. Goal: a decompiler that needs NO `?` and reads naturally without the tools. (See Inbox.)
>
> ### ‚ñ∂ ARTIFACT (Chris, 2026-06-02): the DAIMYO-ATTRIBUTE reference ‚Äî "what does each stat do" (the daimyo analogue of the skill-level footprint)

> ### üü° COMBAT ENGINE ‚Äî DIVE STARTED 2026-06-02 (spine mapped + the big correction landed)
> The bank-2 combat dive (the last pass-1 subsystem) is **in progress** ‚Äî [[project_nobunaga_combat_engine_decoded]]. Done this session, all vs the clean post-fix C:
> - **Spine mapped.** `battle_init_driver $AFE1` = the **WHOLE battle** (not "per-day" as the old memory said): init ‚Üí `deploy_both_sides_units_loop` ONCE ‚Üí **31-day loop** (`run_both_sides_combat_turn(day)` + `apply_unit_damage_over_30`) ‚Üí resolution. `battle_setup_select_province_phase $AF3B` is **MISNAMED = the battle aftermath/resolution handler** (outcome code ‚Üí announce ‚Üí transfer fiefs ‚Üí conquest); rename candidate.
> - **üî¥ MAJOR CORRECTION (oracle-confirmed, `tools/probe-combat-arena.py`): the "4-quadrant damage formula" was never damage.** `$9675` (renamed `set_combat_arena_rect_by_approach`) sets the **tactical-arena deployment RECTANGLE** `$6FF6-$6FFC` (renamed `combat_arena_x_min/y_min/x_max/y_max`) to the attacker's entry strip by the **compass bearing between the two fiefs' strategic-map coords** (`$B0BA`/`$B0EC` = `strategic_map_fief_x`/`_y`, not attribute tables). Returns an edge code {1=N,2=S,3=W,4=E} consumed by **unit placement**, not damage. Default rect (0,0,10,4)=the 11√ó5 grid. The `{1,2,4,7}` "magnitudes" were rect coords. `$9B08` (renamed `deploy_both_sides_units_loop`) is the setup deploy pass, not a damage loop. Toml relabeled + regen-guard clean (pure rename). The stale memory [[project_nobunaga_combat_damage_formula_decoded]] is marked ‚õî SUPERSEDED. **Bonus:** caught a decompiler store-annotation bug (vertical branch N/S words swapped) ‚Üí seed for the VM teardown.
> - **Real model surfaced (static).** Army split into 5 unit-type slots by province composition `$76A9` (`distribute_damage_across_unit_types` is really distribute-MEN). Per-attack casualties = a `rng(6‚àískill)+morale+charisma` contest with a men-capture branch (`resolve_attack_apply_casualties $9E73`), accumulated per-side, applied at `/30`/day (`apply_unit_damage_over_30 $830B`). Combat reads **Charisma + skill** ‚Üí confirms two daimyo-attribute footprint entries.
> - **‚úÖ CASUALTY FORMULA EMULATOR-CONFIRMED 2026-06-02 (`tools/probe-combat-casualty.py`).** The attack is a **CAPTURE/DEFECTION CONTEST**, not a kill-counter: `atk_score = rng(6‚àískill)+morale(atk)+charisma(atk_daimyo)` vs `def_score = morale(def)+charisma(def_daimyo)+2¬∑skill`; if `atk>def`, `pct_op(math32_2arg(atk,atk‚àídef), enemy_slot_strength)` men **defect from the enemy's slot to the attacker's slot 0** (cap 9999); on loss/zero, enemy province morale ‚àí= skill. **Charisma is the decisive combat stat** ‚Äî in the Oda matchup the attacker won at *every* morale 40‚Äì120 on charisma alone. Resolved the reverse-push arg binding (body arg1=slot, arg2=men) by internal consistency + the AI caller. Toml `$9E73` annotated; probe registered. **Combat = absorbing the enemy army, not annihilating it.** [[project_nobunaga_combat_engine_decoded]]
> - **‚úÖ DAMAGE MODEL CLOSED 2026-06-02 ‚Äî THREE decoupled mechanisms (`tools/probe-combat-bleed.py`).** The per-side battle record `$6F7D+6*side = {+0 gold, +2 rice, +4 men}` (the `$8BEA` Gold/Rice/Men triple). **(1) The legendary "/30" is the RICE/SUPPLY clock, NOT damage** ‚Äî `apply_unit_damage_over_30` ‚Üí renamed **`consume_daily_battle_rice`** ($830B): `rice(+2) ‚àí= men(+4)/30` per day ‚áí army eats ~men rice over a ~30-day battle, rice 0 ‚Üí **"you have no rice!"** = the rice-exhaustion/doughnut mechanic + the real "31-day limit." Cross-dump proof: rice drained men-proportionally (‚àí12/‚àí8 = the 32:21 men ratio) while men + `$6FBC` slots held constant. **(2) KILLS** = `apply_pct_reduction_to_unit_strength` ($9D03) via `tally_..._parity_50` ($9DFB): strength-ratio split `local11 = math32_2arg(A,B)=100A/(A+B)`, defender loses `local11%`, attacker `(100‚àílocal11)%`. **(3) CAPTURE** = the morale+charisma contest ($9E73, done above). toml renamed/annotated, regen-guard clean. **This also closes the rice/supply half of Task #4.**
> - **‚úÖ TERMINATORS + RESOLUTION CLOSED 2026-06-02.** `battle_init_driver`'s 31-day loop exits to `battle_setup_select_province_phase` ‚Üí renamed **`dispatch_battle_resolution`** ($AF3B) with an OUTCOME CODE that indexes the loser table `battle_conclusion_msgs_loser` ($B640) + observer table `..._observer` ($B650): **3**=day-31 timeout ("your men are exhausted!"), **4**=rice‚â§0 ("supply... out of rice", the `$B06D` SCMPLE on `unit_record+2`=rice), **5**=commander killed (unit **type-0** absent, `check_commander_alive_both_sides` $AB8E, checked after every action), **6**=annihilation (5 escalated when `war_side_state_flag[0]&31`==0); plus retreat ("%s has retreated", Flee). **Unit type-0 = the COMMANDER.** The "You have no rice/soldiers!" strings ($FDEB/$FDFD) are the bank-1 strategic *pre-battle* checks, not tactical terminators. **Aftermath** `apply_conquest_outcome` ($E03C): winner **absorbs BOTH sides' surviving gold/rice/men** into the conquered fief, **‚àí10‚Äì19% output pillage** (`pct_op(rng(10)+10, output)`), ownership transfer + defeated daimyo's other fiefs neutralized (`province_ai_state=-1`) + `install_new_daimyo`. toml renamed/labeled (incl. the 10 conclusion strings), regen-guard clean. **Task #4 DONE.**
> - **‚úÖ DAIMYO-ATTRIBUTE COMBAT FOOTPRINT DONE 2026-06-02.** Stats split into two roles: **Charisma drives the damage** (capture contest); **Health/Drive/Luck/IQ drive the AI's engage decision** via `ai_sum_battle_strength` ($8E5D), a weighted attacker-vs-defender stat tally with weights `battle_strength_stat_weights $B5B1` = **[HEALTH 5, DRIVE 10, LUCK 10, CHARISMA 5, IQ 20, morale 10, skill 25]** ‚Äî **IQ (20) is the top daimyo term**, province skill (25) the biggest overall. (`ui_helper_d7ea`‚Üí`selected_province_daimyo_record`; both renamed, regen-guard clean.) Task #3 DONE.

> ### üü° AI DEEP-DIVE ‚Äî COMMAND PASS DONE + WAR-TARGET RE-WALKED & ORACLE-CONFIRMED 2026-06-03 (`turn-loop-command.html`)
> The "how does the AI play each turn" half is decoded fresh against the post-fix decompile (the old notes were stale) and shipped as a deep-dive page. Done this session:

Grudge override via rival `$6E7F`; diplomatic pick gated on Drive‚â•50 + relations.

The 6 Grant policies are a **player affordance** ‚Äî every ordinary save reads `province_ai_state {Home:49, Direct:1}` (all 49 AI fiefs at 0, only the human's fief at 5); states 1‚Äì4 appear ONLY where the player conquered+granted (scale with player-owned fiefs). So state 0=Home (‚Üí`ai_econ_command_dispatch`, the Balanced RNG loop) is the AI's **universal** per-turn behavior; per-fief variety = resource state+RNG+daimyo stats, not policy. Locked into the `province_ai_state $6CF7` label + `turn-loop-command.html` (new "Does the AI pick a style? No" census section, page now reframes the policy table as the player's Grant menu).

> - **üéûÔ∏è THE ANIMATION VM ‚Äî CRACKED + PULLED PURE-FROM-ROM.** Animations are a bytecode scripting VM: `ui_helper_e80c(id)` writes id‚Üí`$7FCB` ‚Üí bank-14 `$80AD` indexes a 5-byte descriptor table at **bank-14 `$AF80`** `{bank, data_src, command_stream}` ‚Üí runs a 22-opcode interpreter (CHR upload / palette / `set_sprite` metasprites via `sub_801D` / sound / delay / FOR-loops). **`tools/run-animation.py <id>`** drives `$80AD` headless, intercepts the graphics syscalls, renders frames ‚Üí `atlas/anim-<id>.gif`. Grow (id 9) = a recognizable peasant-farming animation. **This is the "render graphics bits from code" tool (frontier B) for ANIMATED assets** ‚Äî `--list` shows all 22; every command/event animation is now pullable. [[project_nobunaga_animation_vm]]

> **‚úÖ‚úÖ THE ATOMIC WALK ‚Äî COMPLETE 2026-06-02.** All 8 atomic command pages built (`commands/{grow,build,give,train,tax,send,hire,dam}.html`), each = driver-flow walkthrough + bytecode-validated formula + ROM-executed validation table + embedded from-ROM animation. Index + `appendix-formulas.md` updated; `tax.md`/`send.md` stubs created. **Dam (the last OPEN formula) is DERIVED + verified.** Findings this walk (several CORRECTED prior docs ‚Äî the bytecode arbitrated, as warned):
> - **Build** ($88A6, anim 24): no "secondary town bump" ‚Äî ONE `town += 2g` routed through `helper_dam_rounding` ($887D, war-halves + caps); pct computed LIVE (not 20). 5/5 ROM-executed.
> - **Give** ($AA1F‚Üígive_a/b/c‚Üí`give_transfer_apply $A8D3`‚Üí$891D/$896F/$89C1, anim 6): pure benefit, NO drain; pair-averaged Grow kernel; +1 charisma to the giver. In-game test exact on both loyalty+wealth.
> - **Train** ($9586, anim 10): `(rng%20+10)√ó4` = **40‚Äì116** (appendix said 40‚Äì80 ‚Äî WRONG, corrected); +10 aptitude bonus; needs soldiers; animates before applying.
> - **Tax** ($999A driver + `$82D6` generic signed-pct primitive, anim **19** raise / **18** lower): SYMMETRIC ‚Äî loyalty AND wealth ¬±pct_op(stat,|Œîtax|) opposite the tax move; charisma ‚àì1; scales with the CHANGE ‚Üí set high once.
> - **Send** ($9A5D + `$8BE5`, anim 17): `min(header‚àícurrent, available)`, **NO attrition** (the "~3% attrition" was a misread); ships rice AND gold in one command.
> - **Hire** ($A5F4 driver, "(Men/Ninja)?"): **`$A2D2` is the NINJA/sabotage path** (anim 12) ‚Äî was MISLABELED "effect_hire"; recruit-men is **`$A553`** (+ dilution `$8BF4`, anim 33). Recruits dilute army stats by men-weighted average ‚Üí elite armies are TRAINED not hired. Hire-rate re-rolls per turn.
> - **Dam** ($9B7E driver ‚Äî formula is INLINE, not in `$87D8` which is just `sqrt(output)`; apply via `$887D`, anim 21): **`gain = max(1, ‚åä2√óamount √∑ ‚àöoutput‚åã)`**, dams the ONLY 0‚Äì100-capped stat; spend cap `min(gold, (100‚àídams)√ó‚àöoutput√∑2)` = exactly enough to reach 100. Validated vs `dam-mikawa` capture (+56 exact). [[project_nobunaga_dam_doctrine]]

> **‚ñ∂‚ñ∂ NEXT SESSION = THE FUNCTIONAL / THIN PAGES.**
> **‚úÖ ESPIONAGE PAGES DONE 2026-06-02 (out-of-order walk):** `commands/ninja.html` + `commands/bribe.html` built ‚Äî AND the walk RESOLVED a long-standing mis-attribution. The 5-op sabotage menu (Uprising/Revolt/Dams/Assassin/Arson, `$BD8F`) is **Hire‚ñ∏Ninja** (`effect_ninja_sabotage $A2D2` ‚Äî was mislabeled `effect_hire`; recruit-men is `$A553`), NOT Bribe. **Bribe** (`$8D4D`) is the separate **gold-for-spy peasant-defection**: a loyalty+charisma contest (`bribe_success_check $8D02`) that steals ~30‚Äì55% of the target's output. Toml label fixed + regen-guard clean (banks 00/02/15 byte-identical); memory [[project_nobunaga_sabotage_and_ui_strings]] rewritten. `build-command-page.py` functional template extended (optional `flow`/`table`/`callout`). **FORMULAS WALKED (2026-06-02, vs Chris's "do we still need to walk it?"):** ninja drain `$A255` = `(rng%max(1,‚åäfield¬∑‚àö(your_skill+30)/100‚åã)+1)√ó5` (clamped to field) ‚Äî **EMULATOR-CONFIRMED** via `probe-espionage.py`; bribe contest `$8D02` resolved to the **INTUITIVE** direction ‚Äî success when YOUR loy+cha > target's + rng%10, then 50% (an earlier draft had it backwards; the VM passes call args into frame slots in REVERSE push order ‚Äî confirmed by the `$8BD0` pointer-DEREF). Bribe transfer `$8BC1` **fully derived + emulator-confirmed**: `peasants_moved = loyalty ‚àí (‚åä(30+rng%25)¬∑(min(loyalty,‚àögold)+1)/100‚åã + 1)` (op-by-op trace + closed-form check reproduces every band; `‚àögold` = ‚àö of the "Gold for spy?" amount) ‚Äî **NOT a % of output** (corrected). Quirk: more spy gold ‚Üí larger ‚àögold ‚Üí larger resistance ‚Üí *fewer* peasants (gold-independent success roll), flagged for an in-game check. Tech debt fixed en route: the **emulator rng stub** (was a no-op ‚Äî see Inbox, now RESOLVED). **Espionage subsystem (Hire‚ñ∏Ninja + Bribe) is now fully decoded ‚Äî formulas emulator-confirmed.**
> **‚úÖ THE 7 THIN / TURN-SKIP PAGES DONE 2026-06-02** ‚Äî `commands/{pact,marry,rest,grant,map,other,pass}.html` built, every one grounded in its decompiled driver (NO guessing ‚Äî the bytecode arbitrated, and it reclassified the batch). Findings:
>   - **Two are genuinely thin** (no `ui_helper_e80c`, no state write): **`map`** (`driver_map $AF38`, pure strategic-map view, returns 0 ‚Üí doesn't even spend the turn) and **`pass`** (`driver_pass $B2A1`, a 3-line driver: print "What a waste." ‚Üí consume the slot).
>   - **`other`** (`driver_other $B23E`) is the **system/options menu**, not a game command: 7 entries via `jumptab_b9e8` / labels `$FF1A` = **Sound / Animat / Wait / Save / Battle / End / Menu** (decoded from ROM). The **Animat** toggle is the master switch for the very command-animation VM the other pages render; **Save** is the only persistence path; only **End** consumes the turn.
>   - **`pact`** (`driver_pact $9C4F`, anim 3) + **`marry`** (`driver_marry $9DC4`, anim 16) are **diplomacy** commands (no formula ‚Äî cost is set by the relations state). Both pay gold to a rival house for an alliance; Marry additionally rolls a **composite bride portrait** (`rng%22+53 ‚Üí draw_daimyo_portrait`) and, on **refusal, drains the player's OWN daimyo stats** (records +2 / +3 skill / +4 charisma each ‚àí1) ‚Äî the only command that snubs you back. Both write the relations matrix (`diplomacy_helper2/3`).
>   - **Chris's reclassification CONFIRMED from code:** **`rest`** (`driver_rest $ADB3`, anim 32) = a **multi-season self-lock** ‚Äî prompt "Seasons" ‚Üí `number_input(1..10)` ‚Üí `rest_turns_remaining[daimyo]` ($6D67); the counter gates the daimyo out of actions in ‚â•5 per-turn check-sites across banks 0/1/2. (The recuperation it buys ‚Äî the health write ‚Äî is applied in the per-turn tick, not the driver; pinning that exact write is a small open thread.) **`grant`** (`driver_grant $AF66`, anim 11) = **delegate a fief to AI governance**: sets `province_ai_state[fief]` to one of 6 policies decoded from `$F7D4` ‚Üí **Home fief / Industrial / Military / Balanced / Farming / Direct** (0 = keep manual control). It's the player's hook into the AI command driver + the same field `neutralize_fief` resets.
>   - **Template extended:** `build-command-page.py` functional renderer now handles `anim_id: None` (instant commands get an "‚ö° instant ‚Äî no animation" badge instead of a broken anim block) and omits the rabbit-holes section when there are none. The 7 specs added to the `COMMANDS` registry; `commands/README.md` index updated (Rest row promoted from "stub").
> **‚úÖ MOVE / ASSIGN / VIEW DONE 2026-06-02** ‚Äî three more functional pages, bytecode-grounded:
>   - **`move`** (`driver_move $96D1` ‚Üí `effect_move $8CA5`, anim 8) = **internal troop logistics** (NOT War/Send): shift men between fiefs you own (dest list = `deduped_owner_list`), cap `min(dest.header‚àídest.men, src.men)`; `effect_move`‚Üí`scaled_transfer_da24` men-weight-blends 3 dest stat fields (morale/skill/arms ‚Äî same dilution as Hire). Quiet power: **"Will you lead them personally?"** relocates the daimyo (clears src `$6DA2`, sets dest, dest `province_ai_state=5` Direct).
>   - **`assign`** (`driver_assign $AD67` ‚Üí `effect_assign $AC11`, no anim) = **interactive arms-allocation editor**: needs soldiers + flat **30 gold**; `render_arms_edit_screen` over the province arms region `$7017` with a 5-row (unit-type) d-pad cursor loop. Sets the foot/cav/musket composition that feeds the combat damage multipliers. (toml doc said "place a retainer" ‚Äî the bytecode shows an arms editor; described from the code.)
>   - **`view`** (`driver_view $A6C7` ‚Üí `effect_view_a/b/c/d`, anim 14) = the **intelligence command**: inspect any fief (own free, **enemy = 10 gold spy**, contest via `effect_view_d` ‚Üí `"Our spy was caught."`), vassal lists, AND an embedded **strategic-map sub-screen** (`map_helper_e5f2/af10` ‚Äî same render core as Map + the `$E694` standalone viewer ‚Üí the 3rd caller noted in the map-render-tool Inbox ticket).

> ### ‚úÖ MERGED PRG-KEYED DECOMPILER VIEW ‚Äî BUILT 2026-06-01 (`tools/decompile-merged.py` ‚Üí `decompiled/all_banks.c`)
> Chris's readability ask: reading `bank_00.c`, cross-bank refs like `call_bank_wrap(2)`/`call_bank10_entry(1)` are dead ends (defined in bank 15, opaque args), and the switchable `$8000-$BFFF` window means no single flat address space to grep. **Fix:** a new tool emits ONE file (all 4 code banks) keyed by **PRG offset** (`bank*0x4000+(cpu&0x3FFF)`) ‚Äî goto labels `L_pPPPPP`, comments `// PRG $P`, so the same `$8003`-in-two-banks gets distinct identities and ctrl-F a label finds one def. Each named call annotated `// -> bankT $CPU` (follow cross-bank); the entry trampolines resolved to the REAL bytecode entry they JMP into (read from ROM): **`call_bank_wrap(2)` ‚Üí `bank2 entry battle_init_driver $AFE1`**, `call_bank_wrap(1)` ‚Üí `ai_per_fief_command_driver $B89B`, `call_bank10_entry(c)` ‚Üí bank-10 audio `$8003`. 495 subs / ~13.7k lines, **byte-deterministic**, PRG-sorted TOC index at top. **Refactor:** extracted `decompile-all.py::bank_subs()` as the shared core so merged + per-bank C are byte-identical; per-bank `bank_NN.c` UNCHANGED (regen-guard verified) and stay canonical. No def-name collisions across banks (verified). **`decompile-all.py` auto-emits `all_banks.c` on a full run** (`--no-merged` to skip) so the per-bank + merged views regen together and never drift; `decompile-merged.py` also works standalone. Registered in tools/README + CONTEXT quick-routes/artifacts. **Open follow-on (optional):** add `bank1_entry`/`bank2_entry`/`bank10_entry` `$8000` labels to the toml for parity with `bank0_entry` (not needed by the tool ‚Äî it resolves via the ROM JMP target).

Verified the coords are real by cross-check vs the bank-4 $8004 adjacency table (adjacent fiefs spatially nearest, median dist-rank 2). Connects to [[project_nobunaga_strategic_tactical_mapping]].

> - **‚úÖ TRACK B1 (ROM data-walk) ‚Äî STRINGS DONE 2026-06-01 (297 ROM strings, ZERO agents).** The reference mechanism is NOT the abs family ‚Äî ROM tables/strings are reached as IMMEDIATE-WORD POINTERS (`$8A/$8C/$8E` with a `$8000+` operand), so data-xref never saw them. Built `tools/rom-xref.py` (the ROM-side twin: index imm-word pointers per (bank,addr), decode NUL-terminated ASCII IN the referencing bank, classify str/table/code-ptr). **Strings are the ORACLE lane** (the decoded text IS the ROM bytes ‚Üí deterministic, no adversarial agent), so all 297 were labeled `msg_<slug>` in one pass ‚Äî `msg_congratulations_my_lord`, `msg_that_daimyo_is_already_taken`, `msg_you_united_japan`, the `%2d`/`%3d` format strings, etc. **Two decompiler enhancements** (so the strings surface in C, both isolated + regen-guarded): (a) imm-word handlers resolve a `$8000+` operand to its label (RAM bases `$6xxx/$7xxx` deliberately left hex so `annotate_array_access` still fires); (b) `annotate_array_access` now accepts a NAMED base, so `(idx + province_to_mapid_table)` stays `province_to_mapid_table[idx]` (caught as the lone regression, fixed ‚Üí future-proofs every table the walk labels). Regen diff = pure `0xADDR`‚Üí`msg_*` substitutions, `effect_grow` byte-identical, determinism held. **‚ñ∂ B1 RESIDUE = ~123 numeric TABLES** (`rom-xref frontier --class tbl`): jump/dispatch tables (lists of code addrs), the combat coord tables `$B0BA/$B0EC` (`select_quadrant_damage_by_direction`), the `$B144` tile table, view-layout tables (`driver_view $FEA6/$FED8`). These are the analytical part ‚Äî name from the referencing function (mostly deterministic) + a small agent fan-out for the genuinely opaque ones. data-xref/rom-xref both registered in tools/README.

> <details><summary>BATCH 1 RESULTS + what the run validated (2026-06-01)</summary>
> **The skill works end-to-end on the oracle-poor bank** (24 agents / 845K tok / ~4.4 min for 3 clusters). Highlights proving the lateral-verify architecture:
> - **`$8003`** AMENDED ‚Üí `display_fullscreen_graphic_sequence`: verifier caught the proposer citing calls ($BA10/$B9FD/$D134) that **don't exist in bank-0 bytecode** (mis-tiled C), corrected from ground truth.
> - **`$88AC`** AMENDED ‚Üí `render_boot_title_screens`: verifier **refuted a "marriage screen" inference** (proved `cc35` is a generic 20-caller screen primitive), traced the sub to the boot entry `vm_bootstrap`.
> - **`$9154`** CONFIRMED ‚Üí `check_daimyo_natural_death`: independently **rediscovered the verified natural-death formula** `(age-10-health/4)/300, age‚â•70` blind from bytecode = known ground truth reproduced = the method is sound without an oracle.

> **TWO TOOLING FIXES the acceptance run earned (the regen guard / link stage doing its job):**
> - **Decompiler dual-bank fix (`decompile-all.py`).** `$8003` and `$8DE1` stayed anon in bank_00.c after writing the labels. Root cause: a switchable-window CPU address can hold a DIFFERENT function in each bank (`$8003` = `display_fullscreen_graphic_sequence` in bank 0 but `prompt_message_and_redraw` in bank 1 ‚Äî both legit, both in the toml). The old `addr‚Üíbank` map (and flattened `vm.labels`) kept only ONE bank/name per address, shadowing bank 0's label with bank 1's. Replaced `_switchable_label_banks` with **`_switchable_section_labels` ‚Üí per-(bank,addr) names parsed straight from the toml sections**; each bank's C now uses its own section's name. Verified: bank_00 picks up both names, bank_01.c `$8003` still `prompt_message_and_redraw`, banks 01/02/15 byte-identical. This generalizes the bank_01 walk's `_switchable_label_banks` fix from "exclude other banks" to "select the right bank's name."
> - **`--by-callgraph` leaves-first mode** added to `cluster-anon-subs.py` (call-graph depth via `native-call-index`; roots land in the last batches). Deterministic.
>
> **CAPTURED (Inbox) ‚Äî `native-call-index` misses VM-internal bytecode CALL opcodes** (`$AC CALL_abs`, `CALL_abs_imm1`): nearly every verifier reported "0 callers" for a sub that *does* have a bytecode caller, then recovered it via grep. Teaching the index to parse `CALL_abs`/`CALL_abs_imm1` edges in `bank_NN_vm.asm` would give proposers real call-graph context and cut verifier grep work. **Also noted:** the `[prg.bank1] "0x8DE1"` entry is a dead label (bank_01.c has no sub there; the real `dedup_owners` function is in bank 0) ‚Äî harmless after the dual-bank fix, candidate for the section-cleanup nicety.

> ### ‚úÖ BANK-01 WALK ‚Äî COMPLETE 2026-05-31 (57/57 anon named; the orchestration-framework proving ground)
> **DONE in ONE session: pilot (7 subs, hand-run) discovered the framework + fixed a decompiler bug; then the `bank01-label-walk` Workflow named the remaining 50 (19 CONFIRMED / 29 AMENDED / 2 REFUTED‚Üí`helper_*`).** `decompiled/bank_01.c` = 0 anon, diff = pure renames (zero logic), other banks byte-identical. Chris's reframe that drove it: don't repeat bank-15's serial coordinator-as-sole-verifier; build a sub-agent pipeline and *work out where verification lives*. Settled empirically (see [[feedback_verification_independence_is_altitude]]):
> - **THE FRAMEWORK:** `propose@decompiled-C ‚Üí independent-verify@bytecode ‚Üí root-writes-survivors`. Two lanes: ORACLE (claim maps to a known formula/data-struct ‚Üí deterministic match, no agent) vs ADVERSARIAL (interpretive ‚Üí independent refuter at LOWER altitude). Root = single writer + integrator (dedup/collision) + regen guard. Verification flows LATERAL (independent sibling), not UP (rubber-stamp) or SELF (correlated).
> - **Three findings, proven by running it:** (1) **recursion-down is unavailable** ‚Äî Agent-tool sub-agents have no Agent tool, so QA can't be owned by a cluster-lead's children; orchestrate from root or via the **Workflow** tool. (2) **self-QA rubber-stamps** ‚Äî the pilot's self-review CONFIRMED 3 wrong names; an independent verifier that dropped to the bytecode (`vm-disasm.py` + ext-op table + call-index) REFUTED 2/3 + amended the 3rd. (3) **the decompiled C is lossy** (`host_call`s render as `?`/TODO) ‚Üí the write-gate must be the bytecode level, never the C (even the coordinator can't grade from C ‚Äî I nearly flagged a correct claim as a hallucination).
> - **PILOT NAMES (written, bytecode-verified) `[prg.bank1]`:** `8250 relations_matrix_get` (HIGH, $6193 getter) ¬∑ `8303 math32_muladddiv` (HIGH, floor((a*b+c)/d)) ¬∑ `8271 relations_rng_predicate` (MED, 0/1 OR-of-two-rolls) ¬∑ `8327 scale_div10_capcheck` (MED, overflow‚Üí-1 sentinel) ¬∑ `8379 apply_two_grows_const1_override` (MED, temp $6D63 2‚Üí1 around two grows) ¬∑ `83A2/83D5 province_window_redraw_ba6f/_ba78` (HIGH-struct).

- **‚ñ∂ NEW EPIC (2026-05-31) ‚Äî NATIVE-CODE FUNCTIONAL LABELING, top-down readability.** Chris's framing: most code is decompiled but carries auto labels (`sub_XXXX`/`b15_cXXXX`), so it's hard to read/find; the apparent "orphans" at `$C000+` (e.g. `$C537`, `$C54F`, `$C567`, `$C570`) **already have good toml names** ‚Äî they just weren't propagated into the disasm/call-sites. Method: walk code linearly ‚Üí assign FUNCTIONAL labels (what it touches / how it ends) ‚Üí then work BACKWARD via the call-graph to refine functional‚Üípurpose names; recursive, divisible into address-range tasks. **The toml is the single propagation hub** ‚Äî label once, it flows to every consumer.
>   - [x] **KEYSTONE BUILT 2026-05-31: `tools/mesen-labels.py` projector** (see Open/Done). `--mlb` loads labels into Mesen; `--asm` names the native disasm (bank 15: 188 call-sites de-anonymized, `jsr b15_c537` ‚Üí `jsr wait_vblank`); `decompiled/*.c` already reads the toml. This is the native analogue of the VM decompiler's Layer-1 mechanical propagation ‚Äî the missing piece that makes "label one sub ‚Üí document all its callers" actually work.

>   - **PHASE 0 (TOOLING) COMPLETE 2026-05-31 ‚Äî ready to walk.** Both keystones built (projector + call-index).
