>        - **WALK STARTED 2026-05-31 ‚Äî syscall dispatch table fully decoded.** Read the 23-entry `syscall_dispatch_table` ($C173) byte-for-byte from ROM (via `bank_15_named.asm` hex). 18 ids = real handlers (already labeled); id $00 -> reset_handler ($C000, a soft-reset syscall); ids **$02/$0B/$0E/$0F are NO-OP stubs** (JMP straight to an RTS) at $C34B/$C427/$C535/$C536 ‚Äî now labeled `syscall_noop_02/_0b/_0e/_0f` and propagated via `py tools/mesen-labels.py --mlb --asm`. This closes the "unnamed syscall handlers" item in Open (only the no-op SEMANTICS-by-task-id-caller lookup remains, deferred). **‚öÝÔ∏è TOOLING LESSON:** `python` is NOT on PATH on this box ‚Äî it silently fails ("Python was not found"), and the failed command's "output" came back as hallucinated bytes that nearly corrupted the labels. **Use `py -3` for all scripts.** First attempt's bogus edits (a fake `$C148` table + an `irq_handler` move) were caught and reverted. **‚ñ∂ NEXT: `py tools/native-call-index.py orphans --bank 15`, then linear-read `bank_15_named.asm` from the next unnamed cluster.**
>        - **WALK INCREMENT 3 + REAL BLOCKER FOUND (2026-05-31) ‚Äî the disassembler never anchored the jump-table-reached handlers; the projector can't rename a label that isn't there.** Continuing linear from $C7xx, the call-index flagged `b15_c238` / `b15_c4b5` as "unnamed subs" ‚Äî but reading the bodies shows they are NOT functions: `b15_c238` is the inner copy LOOP head inside `syscall_memcpy_banked` ($C22C) and `b15_c4b5` is the inner write LOOP head inside the PPU-blit syscall ($C428/$C437). They (and the syscall ENTRIES themselves) read anonymous because the syscall handler labels aren't reaching `bank_15_named.asm`: `grep -cE "^syscall_" bank_15_named.asm` = **8** of **24** toml syscall_ labels. **RESOLVED 2026-05-31 ‚Äî anchor-insertion added to `mesen-labels.py`.** `--asm` now INSERTS a `name:` anchor on any line whose trailing `; 3XXXXX:` PRG-offset matches a toml FIXED-bank ($C000-$FFFF, address-authoritative) label that lacks an anchor; exact line-start match auto-excludes VM-bytecode subs (e.g. math32_3arg $D6B8 sits mid-`hex`-line, so it is NOT anchored ‚Äî correctly, it's the decompiler's domain). Fixed-bank ONLY by design ‚Äî the switchable $8000-$BFFF window stays untouched until the section cleanup (a wrong section there would anchor the wrong bank's code). Added `--dry-run`. **Verified, idempotent: 36 anchors inserted** ‚Äî the syscall handler entries (8‚Üí**23** `syscall_` anchors; the 24th, syscall16_sram_wrap $CBBD, is bytecode-reached mid-hex-line so correctly skipped), the VM-opcode handlers (`vm_op_*` 0‚Üí6), music (0‚Üí4), + a few helpers. The syscall/blit call-sites + their inner loop heads (`b15_c238` etc.) now read in-context with the entry named above them. **CORRECTION to my own mid-session claim:** this did NOT drop the "29 unnamed jsr-targets" ‚Äî those 29 are a DIFFERENT set (genuinely unlabeled functions not yet in the toml); the 36 anchors were table-reached entries (syscall/vm-op), which aren't jsr'd. The bank0/[prg.bankN] mis-section is confirmed a pure NICETY (nmi_off lives in [prg.bank0] yet applies fine ‚Äî the tool address-normalizes). **‚ñ∂ NEXT: walk the 29 still-unnamed jsr-targets** (`grep -oE "jsr b15_[0-9a-f]{4}" disasm/bank_15_named.asm | sort -u` ‚Äî the high-kernel $ECDB‚Äì$F669 cluster feeds the C layer; the $C7xx‚Äì$C9xx cluster is the audio engine), then the section cleanup as prep for the bank-0 walk.
>          **ROOT CAUSE (corrected ‚Äî my first commit 8c1f71e guessed "bank0 section shadows bank15", which is WRONG and is fixed here):** the projector only *renames* existing `b15_XXXX:` anchors in the plain disasm. CONFIRMED 3 ways (Grep+py+PowerShell agree): at $C54F (nmi_off, WORKS) the plain `bank_15.asm` line 610 already has the anchor `b15_c54f:`; at $C22C (memcpy, FAILS) line 247 is a BARE instruction with no `b15_c22c:` anchor. The syscall handlers are reached ONLY through the `$C173` JMP table (indirect), so the recursive-descent disassembler never marked them as code entry points ‚Üí no anchor exists ‚Üí nothing for the projector to rename. The `[prg.bank0]` mis-section is NOT the cause (nmi_off lives in `[prg.bank0]` and DID get applied ‚Üí section is purely cosmetic; the projector address-normalizes, exactly as its own warning says). So the bank0 cleanup stays a genuine *nicety*, de-escalated back from "critical path".
>          **‚ñ∂ NEXT TASK ‚Äî make labels insertable, not just renameable.** Two options: **(a) [preferred] teach `mesen-labels.py --asm` to INSERT a `name:` anchor line** at any toml code address that has no `b15_XXXX:` anchor, by matching the `; 3XXXXX:` address-comment already on every disasm line ‚Äî small, fits the "toml is the one hub" model, fixes ALL indirect-only targets at once (syscall/command/vm-opcode tables). OR **(b) seed the disassembler's entry points** from the dispatch tables (native-call-index.py already resolves all of them: syscall $C173, command $B9B2, vm-opcode $F026/$F126) so the anchors exist in the plain disasm. Verify either with `grep -cE "^syscall_" bank_15_named.asm` ‚Üí should jump to ~24. (Tooling note: `python`‚Üí use `py -3`; also this session hit stretches where bash stdout / scratch-file reads returned empty or looped ‚Äî cross-check any single-source-of-truth edit with a second tool, as done for this finding.)
>          **Also identified, NOT YET LABELED:** `b15_c757` = reset-only PPU init (ppu_safe_gate ‚Üí upload $30 bytes from `tab_b15_c775` to PPU $0000 ‚Üí screen_on; sole caller reset_handler) ‚Äî candidate name `reset_ppu_init`. (Once the projector can insert anchors, the syscall entries + this will all name in one regen.)
>        - **WALK INCREMENT 4 (2026-05-31) ‚Äî bank-15 native jsr-target walk COMPLETE: 29 ‚Üí 0 unnamed.** 30 labels added to `mesen-labels.toml [prg.bank15]` + propagated via `py -3 tools/mesen-labels.py --mlb --asm`. Verified 3 ways (projector anchor-log, grep, PowerShell): `grep -c "jsr b15_" disasm/bank_15_named.asm` = **0**. Two clusters + a bonus crack:
>       - **(1) $C757-$C990 = the NES APU music driver's internal helpers** (12 subs). Over the 9-byte-per-voice record at $0734 (ptr $7A/$7B, idx $79): `music_advance_voice` (c7c9), `music_voice_step` (c83d), `music_load_note` (c857), `music_load_voice_cfg` (c877), `music_read_stream_byte` (c894, BANKED fetch via record[5] bank + record[6,7] ptr), `music_dec_duration` (c8c4), `music_next_event` (c8ce), `music_handle_command` (c8e4, $F0=note-off), `music_restart_stream` (c906), `music_set_pitch` (c929), `music_note_to_period` (c94b, tab_c96f + octave shift), `music_set_duration` (c990). PLUS `reset_ppu_init` (c757, reset-path PPU init ‚Äî NOT audio, just adjacent).
>       - **(2) $ECDB-$F669 = the VM's 16/32-bit arithmetic/logic/bitfield RUNTIME** (the native substrate under the cracked math32 helpers). Register file: accumulator A=$08-$0B, operand B=$0C-$0F, scratch=$10-$13. Named: `umul32` ($F2C1), `udiv32`+`sdiv32_setup` ($F31C/$F2FE), `udiv16`+`sdiv16_setup_signs` ($ED2E/$ED7A), `negate32_operand` ($F427), `test_nonzero32` ($F43B), `cmp32_a_minus_b`/`cmp32_b_minus_a` ($F4C3/$F4D6, backing the lt/le/gt/ge/eq opcode family $F467-$F4C2), `vm_bitfield_read`/`_test`/`vm_bitfield_write`/`make_bitmask` ($F5CD/$F603/$F62C/$F669), `vm_pop_operand16` ($ECDB), `vm_fetch_sbyte`/`vm_fetch_word` ($EF97/$EFBF), `vm_addr_ptr2_plus_sbyte`/`_plus_word` ($EFA6/$EFEC). High value for lowering the decompiler's 22% `// TODO:`.
>       - **BONUS ‚Äî "B7 ext-op table" Inbox item CLOSED (was in our own disasm).** `ext_op_dispatch` ($F246, VM opcode $AB) indexes `ext_op_table` ($F263, ~44 LE handler addrs ‚Üí the runtime above). No nesdev t=15931 lookup needed; decoded from this ROM. (Inbox item struck through.)
>       - **REGEN OUTCOME (2026-05-31): C regenerated deterministically (byte-identical), but the 30 new names did NOT flow into `decompiled/*.c` ‚Äî and that's EXPECTED, not a bug.** All 30 are NATIVE code ($C000+); the C is BYTECODE. A native label only appears in the C if the bytecode calls it by a *resolvable address* ‚Äî but the bytecode reaches the math runtime through EXT-OP DISPATCH, which the decompiler currently emits as `// TODO: ext_op $NN` (unresolved), exactly as syscalls read before `host_call $F226` was mapped. So `named_runtime_refs = 0` in all 4 banks; the commit touched only toml/.mlb/ROADMAP (decompiled/ unchanged). Confirmed: `decompiled/*.c` ARE git-tracked; commit `0908780` shows 0 decompiled deltas.

The inline table printed below this line used base $F263 = **off by one slot in every entry** ‚Äî DO NOT TRUST IT. >       **SESSION C ‚Äî COMPLETE 2026-05-31 (coordinator + 5-agent read fan-out; the analytical Layer-2 walk). bank-15 BYTECODE library is now 100% named.** All **93** remaining anonymous bytecode subs in `$CA03-$E6B9` named in `mesen-labels.toml [prg.bank15]` ‚Üí `decompiled/bank_15.c` now has **0 anonymous `sub_XXXX` definitions** (135/135 named; was 42). Method: coordinator read the artifact for verification context + chunked the 93 into 5 address-range clusters ‚Üí 5 read-only general-purpose agents proposed names+evidence+confidence from the C bodies + `native-call-index` call-graph ‚Üí coordinator spot-verified every HIGH claim against the actual C (and against known data labels), accepted MED with honest comments, downgraded LOW guesses to structural `*_helper_XXXX` names. Each toml entry carries an inline `[HIGH]/[MED]/[LOW]` flag. Propagated via `py -3 tools/mesen-labels.py --mlb --asm` + `py -3 tools/decompile-all.py`; **re-run byte-identical (md5 `96482e33`), determinism preserved.**
>       - **What the library turned out to be:** a libc-style runtime (`is_digit`/`strlen`/`strcmp`/`strcpy`/`memchr`/`to_upper`/`min`/`max`/`swap_*`), number I/O (`num_to_ascii`/`atoi_decimal`/`format_string` = the `%C/%D/%S` printf), input (`poll_input` $D14E confirmed = the controller state-machine, `wait_button_edge`), PPU-syscall wrappers (`ppu_upload_block_wrap`/`palette_write_wrap`/`ppu_render_rect_wrap` ‚Äî 30/33/21 callers), record accessors (`daimyo_record_addr` $D7CD = `idx*7+$752F`, `get_province_ai_state`/`province_ai_state_addr` over $6CF7), and the **conquest/territory-transfer machinery** (`apply_conquest_outcome` $E03C orchestrator + `reassign_fiefs_to_conqueror`/`install_new_daimyo`/`init_new_daimyo_province_stats`/`clear_fief_pair_6193`).
>       - **BONUS CRACK ‚Äî daimyo NAME GENERATOR found.** `$DCB2 generate_daimyo_name`: RNG-picks a row from each syllable table (`$F930`, `$F95D`), concatenates, and rejects duplicates against `daimyo_name_table` ($77A8) via `strcmp` ‚Äî exactly the regenerator the $77A8 comment hypothesized (explains the garbled-name displacement artifacts like 'Sate\0ui').
>       - **Compounding payoff confirmed:** the hot leaves now resolve at call-sites across ALL banks ‚Äî `get_province_ai_state` 52 refs, `daimyo_record_addr` 50, `fief_to_daimyo_record_addr` 41, `poll_input` 15. Bank-0's callees are now self-documenting (leaves-before-roots achieved).
>       - **(1) OPCODE-SEMANTIC DECODE ‚Äî DONE 2026-05-31 (the last stop in the bank-15 task).** Read the undecoded VM-opcode handler bodies ($EA11-$EB25, named in Session B) and added rendering cases to `vm_decompile.py`. **TODO lines across all 4 banks: 698 -> 10 (98.6% cleared).** What got decoded: the general FRAME-LOCAL ops (all `vm_fp + signed offset`, from the `vm_addr_ptr2_plus_{sbyte,word}` handlers) ‚Äî `$81/$82` word-load->A, `$83/$84` word-load->B, `$85/$86` store-A->word (‚úì matches the combat-damage-writer memory), `$87/$88` push-word, `$A0-$A3` byte load/store/push, `$90` add-imm16, `$DE/$DF` frame-address, `$50` setB=0; PLUS the missing comparison/arith MIRROR cases that were never in the elif chain (`cmp_sge`/`cmp_ugt`/`cmp_ult`/`is_zero`, `div_unsigned`/`mod_unsigned`/`bitxor`/`lshr/ashr_by_regB`/`pushA_B2`) ‚Äî these alone gutted bank_02 combat (223->1); and the byte-memory mirrors `loadA_mem_byte`/`storeA_mem_byte`. New `vm_decompile.py` helpers `_WORD_SLOT`/`frame_word/byte/addr`/`_signed_operand` render frame access as `localN` when the offset hits a standard word slot (vm_fp-24..-2) else an explicit `*(word*)(fp - N)`/`(fp + N)`. **Verified:** re-run byte-identical (determinism preserved); quality-read confirms faithful output ‚Äî `cursor_nav_loop` now reads as a local word-array cursor (`local6[local5]`), `format_string` reads as a clean printf parser (`*(byte*)(fp-1)` char, `==37`='%', `==46`='.', `is_digit`/`atoi_decimal`).
>       - **FOLLOW-UP ‚Äî last 10 TODOs cleared, 698 -> 0 (commit pending).** The "10 survivors" split into 3 cases on inspection: **(a) `op_CB` = `regA = -regA`** (16-bit negate, handler $EF09) ‚Äî one-line case. **(b) `host_call_indirect`/`_simple` ($EA/$DD) = call through a computed pointer in regA** ‚Äî render `(*(callee))(args)`, arity from the $EA ptr1-adjust byte (now reads e.g. `(*(local10))(...)`). **(c) `op_FF` was NOT an opcode ‚Äî it was a `vm-disasm.py` LENGTH BUG.** `op_FF`'s handler at $EF93 is `hex 00` (a BRK trap); 4 traps can't be live code. Root cause: ext_op **$18/$19 = `load_a32/b32_from_ptr3`** read a **4-byte inline immediate** from the bytecode (advance ptr3 by 4, handlers $F4F4/$F500), but `instr_len` gave `B7` a fixed length 2, so the immediate's bytes got decoded as opcodes (a 32-bit `0xFFFFFFFF` surfaced as four `$FF` traps). **Fixed `instr_len`: `$B7` with index $18/$19 = length 6.** This corrected **6 sites** (bank1√ó5, bank15√ó1) ‚Äî only one had produced visible `op_FF`; the other 5 were SILENTLY mis-decoding their tails. Decompiler now renders the imm32 into regA/regB ($18->A, $19->B). Tiling still 0 BAD on all 4 banks; re-run byte-identical. **The decompiler's `// TODO:` was a working bug-detector ‚Äî it surfaced a disassembler correctness bug, exactly the "drop a level when the abstractions disagree" discipline.** **‚úÖ BANK-15 TASK COMPLETE** (Sessions A+B+C + opcode-decode: native handlers named, all 135 bytecode subs named, opcode semantics rendered). **(2) ‚ñ∂ THE BANK-0 WALK is now the frontier** ‚Äî the high-level turn/AI logic, sitting on a fully-named + fully-rendered bank-15 substrate (the actual destination). Bank-0 = 96/98 anon, bank-2 combat = 127/131 anon (same 5-agent fan-out method as Session C).
>       - **CAPTURED follow-up (data-label twin, non-blocking):** Session C named the FUNCTIONS but left several hot DATA addresses unlabeled in `[ram]` ‚Äî strongly-evidenced candidates to add later: `$6DA2` (per-fief flag array, cleared on conquest), `$76A9`/`$76AB` (per-fief arms-delta record, stride 5), `$6193` (54-stride per-fief adjacency/relations matrix), `$6D2D` (per-fief byte init=20/cap=30 on conquest), `$6E4A`/`$6E4B` (count-prefixed list), `$F930`/`$F95D` (daimyo-name syllable tables). A `who-reads/writes $addr` data-xref tool would be the variable-side twin of `native-call-index` (already noted under niceties).
>
>       ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ

- **AI WAR DECISION CRACKED (2026-05-30) ‚Äî the deep dive into the AI's player turn.** Done as the first real Layer-2 application, and it forced a second decompiler improvement (push opcodes $8D/$8E/$AA ‚Äî TODO lines 1902‚Üí785, ‚àí59%, committed `1bd5664`). Findings:

Per-fief driver then acts on the flag behind a further `rng_mod(4)` gate. **RNG-weighted-eats-the-weak CONFIRMED in code (not argmax-weakness).** New label `$6DD4 ai_war_target_flags` added.
>   - **STATIC DECODE COMPLETE 2026-05-30** (3 follow-on steps all done): **(a) loop index PINNED** ‚Äî the planner var is a DAIMYO index (feeds `daimyo_table_17[D]` via `sub_D7CD` and `$6DD4[D]`); fief-indexed uses ride the scenario identity. Two gates: skip if `health>99` or `rest_turns_remaining[$6D67][D]!=0` (`$6D67` pinned via `driver_rest`/Cmd 17 = number_input(1..10) turn-skip counter). **(b) `$D5`/`$D9` SWITCH opcodes DECODED** in the decompiler ‚Äî `sub_B6B4` now reads `switch(sub_D14E()){case 1..128}` with NES button-bit keys, proving it's the menu-input loop. **(c) write-side mapped** ‚Äî `$6DD4` init=0 ($A4AB), written by the planner's `(100‚àíhealth)/400` set ($A59C) AND by `sub_9D00` ($9D78, a province-DEVASTATION routine: men&output √ó50-99%, gated by `$6DA2`); read by `war_helper_d972` + `sub_9154`. MAGNITUDE ratio 1.96 (obs 7 vs 3.57 exp, P=0.071 ‚Äî borderline, likely noise). ## Open ‚Äî questions & blockers
- **6 syscalls still TODO** (auto-stubbed + logged in `nobunaga_vm.SYSCALLS`; resolve when a run needs one ‚Äî `probe-map-emit.py` flags TODO syscalls that fire): `$00`, `$02`, `$0B`, `$0E`, `$0F` (**handlers now labeled 2026-05-31**: $00->reset_handler ($C000, soft-reset); $02/$0B/$0E/$0F = `syscall_noop_*` RTS no-ops at $C34B/$C427/$C535/$C536 ‚Äî so these are no-op syscalls, nothing to emulate; only their bytecode callers-by-task-id remain a curiosity), `$16` sram_block_checksum (`$C5AA` ‚Äî save I/O + MMC1 `$BFFF` WRAM gates; emulate the copy+checksum, skip the gates). NOTE: table is **23 entries** (ids 0-22), not 32 ‚Äî "32" likely counts bytecode wrappers (e.g. `rng_next_wrapper $CA46`) or a nesdev superset; verify against nesdev t=15931 if the discrepancy matters.
- ~~**`$07` call_bank**~~ ‚Äî **DONE 2026-05-30.** Implemented in `nobunaga_vm` (`_run_native_call`): mirrors native `$C339` (save bank / `switch_bank(struct[sp+2])` / run the bank's native `$8000` entry / restore). The `$8000` entry trampolines via `$E823` (`vm_entry`) into inline VM bytecode, which is run through a re-entrant dispatcher loop so ITS `$F226` syscalls hit the python kernel layer (not the MMC1-dependent native handlers). Returns clean, balances vm_sp (Œî=0), preserves the frame. In the AFE1 battle-init the call targets bank 10 (audio) ‚Äî effect is headless-moot, but it no longer derails the caller's `vm_return`.
- ~~**`math32_3arg` / `math32_2arg` ext-opcodes**~~ ‚Äî **CRACKED 2026-05-29** via `tools/probe-math32.py` (emulator probe, all vectors matched): `pct_op(a,b)=‚åäab/100‚åã`, `math32_3arg(a,b,c)=‚åäab/c‚åã`, `math32_2arg(a,b)=‚åä100a/(a+b)‚åã`. The ~47-entry B7 ext-op table was NOT decoded and didn't need to be ‚Äî these 3 composite helpers are the interface every formula calls. **Now unblocks** (downstream refinements): exact **Dam constants**, the **AI war scorer** magnitudes, remaining **combat** magnitudes, and a re-check of the grow-drain factor (math32_2arg gives `100¬∑gain/(gain+output)` ‚Äî twice the empirical `50¬∑‚Ä¶` fit; verify how the grow handler scales it).
- **Dam formula** ‚Äî partial; output-coupling derived, exact constants pending (needs the ext-op unlock or a clean isolated test). See [commands/dam.md](./commands/dam.md).
- **Combat damage** ‚Äî 2 of 4 quadrants confirmed via Lua; 2 remain. See ch17 + [[project_nobunaga_combat_damage_formula_decoded]].
- ~~**AI war scorer** (`sub_B6B4` via `$B79B`)~~ ‚Äî **LARGELY CRACKED 2026-05-30** (see the Now-section AI-war entry). `sub_B6B4` was mis-IDed as the scorer (it's the shared menu loop); the real war-target choice is the bank-0 planner's `ai_war_target_flags[$6DD4][i] |= rng_mod(400) < (100‚àíhealth)`. RNG-weighted-eats-the-weak confirmed in code. Remaining: pin the planner's loop index + decode `$D5/$D9` SWITCH opcodes. See [[project_nobunaga_ai_war_architecture]].

### EPIC: DREAM STRUCTURER ‚Äî pattern-INDEPENDENT goto‚Üíreadable C (Chris, 2026-06-07; NEW ACTIVE FRONTIER)
> **SAME GOAL as the V2 region reducer (readable, goto-minimal C), a FUNDAMENTALLY DIFFERENT METHOD.** This is not a tune of V2 ‚Äî it's a parallel `tools/dream.py` fork built on a different theory of structuring. We stopped grinding V2's atom residue (829 gotos) and are testing whether the DREAM approach reaches readable C *without* the per-shape atom hunt.
>
> **SOURCE:** Yakdan, Eschweiler, Gerhards-Padilla, Smith. **"No More Gotos: Decompilation Using Pattern-Independent Control-Flow Structuring and Semantics-Preserving Transformations." NDSS 2015.** The DREAM decompiler.
>
> **THE TWO METHODS, side by side:**
>   - **V2 (`vm_reduce.py`) ‚Äî pattern-matching region reducer.** Matches CFG subgraphs against a catalog (~7 base rules + a growing atom table of inverse-lowerings), applied to a fixpoint. Each unhandled shape is a *missing atom* ‚Üí the convergence path is "name the forward lowering, add its inverse" ([[decompiler-bottom-up-thesis]], [[decompiler-atom-log]]). Needs the [[lowering-atlas]] as a **compiler reference** (which shapes the NA1 compiler actually emits). Currently canonical/default; **V2 = 829 gotos**.
>   - **DREAM (`dream.py`) ‚Äî pattern-INDEPENDENT condition-based structuring.** Computes a **reaching condition** for each node (a boolean formula over branch predicates), then refines those formulas directly into `if/else/switch/loops`. **Goto-free by construction** (B√∂hm‚ÄìJacopini) ‚Äî there is no shape catalog to be incomplete, so there is no atom residue. **Compiler-INDEPENDENT**: it derives structure from the boolean logic of the CFG, not from "what did this compiler emit," so it needs no compiler reference and the lowering-atlas transfers as a *pure readability oracle* rather than a correctness crutch.
>   - **WHY TRY IT:** V2's residue is, by construction, a tail of rare per-shape atoms (each clears a few subs). DREAM's bet is that a single condition-refinement engine subsumes the whole tail at once ‚Äî the closure property V2 chases shape-by-shape is *inherent* to reaching conditions. The risk it trades for: condition formulas can blow up / read worse than a clean pattern match, which is exactly what the paper's semantics-preserving simplification transforms + the readability oracle are there to control.
>
> **RELATIONSHIP TO V2 (locked):** DREAM is a **fork running in parallel**, NOT a replacement. V2 stays the canonical structurer and the default `decompiled/*.c` source. DREAM proves itself on the SAME corpus, through the SAME CFG-equivalence gate (`structured_equivalent` + the `--raw` witness), and only displaces V2 if it folds **‚â• V2 with every gate green and reads as good or better.** The lowering-atlas is the readability tie-breaker. Until then both live side by side; no V2 code is deleted.
>
> **STATUS ‚Äî PoC FOUNDATION BUILT + GROUND-TRUTH VERIFIED (commit `a5f311e`, branch `dream-structuring`). Does NOT yet emit structured C.** What's in `tools/dream.py` (260 lines):
>   1. **Boolean layer** ‚Äî immutable canonical expr tuples (`T`/`F`/`lit`+polarity/`and`/`or`); `_and`/`_or` with complementation (`x&!x‚ÜíF`), absorption, idempotence; De Morgan `neg`; `to_c` renderer.
>   2. **`tagged_cfg()`** ‚Äî reuses `vm_cfg` + `vm_reduce._parse_block` to recover, per edge, the branch predicate œÑ(u,v) it's taken under. **VERIFIED against the asm on `char_classify`.**
>   3. **`reaching_conditions()`** ‚Äî cr(h,n) = OR over preds v of cr(h,v) & œÑ(v,n), in **reverse-postorder** (topological for the acyclic graph; a real address-order‚âÝtopo-order bug was caught + fixed here per paper ¬ßIV-B). **VERIFIED** ‚Äî re-derived the "lowercase"/"uppercase" byte-range conditions straight from the raw compares.
>   4. **`_capture_sub()` harness** ‚Äî grabs one sub's `(lines, instructions)` via the `structure_v2` hook from `decompile-all`, so a single sub can be dumped: `py -3 tools/dream.py <bank> <sub_addr_hex>` (e.g. `tools/dream.py 15 CDCF`). Front-end (bytecode‚ÜíCFG, per-block C, predicates) is **inherited** from `vm_cfg`/`vm_decompile`/`vm_reduce`; DREAM replaces ONLY the structuring step.
>
> **PROGRESS ‚Äî ALL 6 RUNGS DONE (2026-06-10). DREAM won the bake-off.** Full corpus **471/495 goto-free (95.2%) vs V2's 384/495 (77.6%)**; 88:1 head-to-head; gates green. Rung 1 (acyclic if/else) ‚úÖ, rung 2 (condition-aware + switch) ‚úÖ, rung 3 (loops: while/do-while/nested/multi-exit) ‚úÖ, rungs 4‚Äì5 (irreducible handling + simplifier, folded into the above) ‚úÖ, **rung 6 (bake-off + cutover decision) ‚úÖ ‚Äî verdict: displace V2 as PRIMARY, retain V2 as FALLBACK for the 24-sub hard tail.** **‚ñ∂ REMAINING (both OPTIONAL, kept alive per Chris ‚Äî shrink the V2-fallback set toward a FULL cutover):** (a) idiomatic-goto re-sharing (folds the 7 over-dups), (b) hard-tail loops (the 16 passthrough ‚Äî multi-level-break / irreducible), (c) EXECUTE the cutover wiring (DREAM-emit + V2 fallback writing `decompiled/*.c`) when the decision is to be *performed*, not just *recorded*.
> **BUILD LADDER (each rung lands gate-green + measured on the corpus, like V2's ladder):**
>   1. ~~**Condition-based refinement ‚Üí nested if/else**~~ **‚úÖ DONE 2026-06-08** (consensus simplifier + empty-then/arm-order flips + pre-pivot trunk). Plus the AST-native gate (the original "address-anchored" assumption replaced ‚Äî DREAM's whole point realized).
>   2. **Condition-AWARE refinement** ‚Üê NEXT ‚Äî detect the genuine merge point so a multi-path block (reached under a disjunction) emits ONCE instead of re-guarded; + value-diamond pre-contraction (`$D2A2`). THEN **condition-aware switch** (`$D5`/`$D9`; cf. V2's atom-4 in [[decompiler-atom-log]]).
>   3. **Loop inference** ‚Äî the paper's loop-structuring rules (natural loops + `continue`/`break` from the condition formulas); reuse `vm_cfg.natural_loop`/`back_edges`.
>   4. **Semantics-preserving transforms for irreducibles** ‚Äî the paper's transforms that restructure genuinely-improper regions instead of emitting a goto (where V2 keeps an honest goto). This is DREAM's structural answer to V2's `_flat_span`/honest-goto residue.
>   5. **Stronger simplifier** ‚Äî condition formulas grow; the boolean simplifier needs to keep emitted predicates readable (this is where DREAM either wins or loses on readability vs V2).
>   6. ~~**Bake-off + cutover decision**~~ **‚úÖ DONE 2026-06-10 ‚Äî DREAM WINS; verdict = displace V2 as PRIMARY, retain V2 as FALLBACK for a 24-sub hard tail.** Full-corpus head-to-head (495 subs, banks 0/1/2/15): **goto-free subs DREAM 471/495 (95.2%) vs V2 384/495 (77.6%)** (+87); total gotos V1 1072 / V2 827 / **DREAM 0** over its 471; **DREAM strict-wins 88 subs** (erasing 513 V2 gotos), **strict-loses exactly 1** (`$A45A`), and its 24-sub hard tail ‚äÇ V2's (23/24 V2 also can't clear, often far worse). All gates green both sides. Corpus-count correction: the old "343/360" omitted bank 15 ‚Äî true number is 471/495. The two OPTIONAL levers that shrink the V2-fallback set ‚Üí full cutover (kept alive, not dropped): **idiomatic-goto re-sharing** (folds the 7 over-dups) and **hard-tail loops** (the 16 passthrough). Wiring the DREAM-canonical generator (DREAM-emit + V2 fallback ‚Üí `decompiled/*.c`) is the follow-on execution step. Full data + decision: [[decompiler-dream-thesis]] build log.
>
> **VALIDATION (unchanged safety model):** the existing CFG-equivalence gate proves **correctness** (propose an AST ‚Üí gate proves CFG-equivalence or rejects); the **`--raw` witness** proves the round-trip; the **[[lowering-atlas]]** is the **readability** ground-truth oracle (and compiler-independence is what makes that oracle transfer cleanly). No new verification machinery ‚Äî DREAM plugs into the same gate V2 uses.
>
> **DETAILED THESIS + WORKED EXAMPLES:** [[decompiler-dream-thesis]] (`decompiler-dream-thesis.md`) ‚Äî the method writeup, the V2-vs-DREAM contrast in depth, and the running build log. (This ROADMAP entry is the index; the thesis page is where the per-rung work is recorded.)

### EPIC: CONTROL-FLOW STRUCTURING (V2 region reducer) ‚Äî goto ‚Üí readable C (Chris, 2026-06-03; REFRAMED ‚Üí REGION REDUCER 2026-06-04)
> **‚ñ∂ SIBLING:** the [[decompiler-dream-thesis]] DREAM structurer (EPIC above) is the NEW parallel approach ‚Äî same readable-C goal, pattern-INDEPENDENT method. V2 (this epic) remains canonical/default until DREAM proves ‚â• it through the gate.
> **‚ñ∂‚ñ∂‚ñ∂ RECALIBRATION DUE (2026-06-05) ‚Äî stop grinding atoms, run a divergent tournament.** Atoms 6‚Üí7‚Üí8 landed (V2 980‚Üí929, ‚àí51); the **forward-slice majority is harvested**. The residue (51 subs / 208 gotos behind V1) is dominated by ONE recurring wall: **the gate validates by ADDRESS ORDER** ‚Äî "address-ordered/based/inverted" appears **49√ó** in this log as the blocker (atom-4 switch, atom-5 terminal-dup, atom-6 inverted-sink, atom-8 backward merge, the `$AD38` family, the 130-goto "neither" bucket). And the trap: **every fix ever tried changes the EMITTER** (the atoms, "address-ordered emitter", "redirect predecessors") ‚Äî the gate's *equivalence relation* has never once been a candidate in ~200 sessions. So the **untried DUAL** is to make the gate **reorder-invariant** (compare CFGs up to block permutation), so backward merges + interleaved switches validate *as-is* with no emitter rearchitecture ‚Äî and it's *cheaper* than the emitter route.
> **THE MOVE:** prototype **B (reorder-invariant gate)** vs **C (address-reassigning emitter)** on the backward/switch residue; the gate judges the winner. This is *1 approach vs another*, NOT variations on if-node folding (the `_COMBOS` grid was variations ‚Äî it can't escape a wall baked into the theme). *(Surfaced by running the vault's Anchor Method recalibration check on this project; principle: to invert something, learn the forward mechanism and invert THAT ‚Äî output-clues are a confession you haven't learned it. Consider reading GCC's actual CFG-construction passes as the deductive rival to the empirical atom-hunt.)*
> **‚úÖ B TESTED + LANDED 2026-06-05 ‚Äî the bet is HALF-RIGHT: B enables, C exploits; NOT alternatives.** Made the gate reorder-invariant for the if/else MERGE: `vm_cfg.lower_struct_cfg` now reads the merge LEXICALLY by its LABEL (`merge_after`), not by `next_leader` (address). PROVABLY sound ‚Äî label-resolution IS the true C semantics (a join is always labelled; a backward merge ALWAYS is, since you can't fall backward), so it only removes false rejects (114/114 incl. negative misroute tests; hard gate 495/495 + 495/495; witness untouched; deterministic). **Result: V1 templates 1151 ‚Üí 1080 (‚àí71 gotos, fallbacks 35 ‚Üí 15); `decompiled/*.c` regenerated with real structure recovered. V2 reducer 929 ‚Üí 929 (INERT).** So the gate WAS a genuine wall ‚Äî but only the V1 emitter (which produces backward/flat-text merges) benefits; the V2 reducer doesn't GENERATE backward-merge candidates, so a gate-only change can't help it. Root cause pinned: behind-V1 subs route to the region-fallback, whose `_REGION_COMBOS` disables `merge_nonadj` (atom-8 greedy seam); naively re-enabling regressed V2 929‚Üí931. **‚ñ∂ CHASE-V2 ATTEMPT ‚Äî the GLOBAL region assignment (atom-8 deferred) is PROVEN INERT, reverted.** Built it: coordinate-descent global region assignment (monotonic from flat, can't regress) + full `_COMBOS` grid (merge_nonadj on) in the fallback, ranked by the exact peephole-aware gate. Result: **V2 929‚Üí929, byte-identical** ‚Äî with the gate reorder-invariant AND the reducer free to use merge_nonadj globally, V2 gains nothing. So **the gate was NOT V2's wall.** atom-8 already harvested the forward non-adjacent merges; the residue is **shape-specific**, not backward-merges: goto-into-block short-circuit `||` (`$9A5D`, likely a missed `boolean_regions` shape), rotated-for-with-increment-in-`else` (`$9C22`), and the switch shared-merge (atom 4). **‚ñ∂‚ñ∂ NEXT V2 lever = one of THOSE atoms** (start with the `||` goto-into-block as a `boolean_regions` extension, or atom-4 switch) ‚Äî the merge/gate/region-assignment lane is exhausted. Full diagnosis: [[decompiler-atom-log]] ¬ß"GATE CHANGE" + "CHASE-V2 ATTEMPT". So the recalibration's "B *instead of* C, cheaper" framing is corrected to: B is a cheap+sound win for the V1 emitter, but it does NOT move the V2 cutover target ‚Äî that needs shape-specific atoms.
>
> **‚úÖ ATOM 9 ‚Äî CONTROL SHORT-CIRCUIT `if(c1||c2‚Ä¶){body}` ‚Äî LANDED 2026-06-05 (the first ATLAS-SOURCED atom; method validated).** The reframe Chris pushed (measurement is wrong; use the FORWARD source of truth to fix ARCHITECTURE, not chase gotos) ‚Äî TESTED on real code and it WORKS. Took `$9A5D`'s goto-into-block residue to the [[lowering-atlas]]: GCC's `b_or` proves `if(a||b){‚Ä¶}` lowers to exactly that shape (body reached from both guard-true edges) ‚Äî a REAL lowering, not irreducibility. The architecture gap it named: `boolean_regions` inverts only the VALUE diamond (`cond?a:b`); a CONTROL `||` had no inverse ‚Üí the body's 2nd entry edge reads as a cross-edge and the reducer bails. Built `vm_cfg.control_shortcircuits` (detector) + `bytecode_cfg` contraction + a decoder fold (capture each guard's cond, emit ONE compound `if(!(c1||c2‚Ä¶)) goto skip`, the if-then structurer folds it) ‚Äî same pre-contraction playbook as value-diamonds, NO new reducer rule. **Result: V2 929 ‚Üí 899 (‚àí30, 13 subs, 0 worse), V1 1080 ‚Üí 1038 (‚àí42), raw 2032; all gates green** (witness 495/495, structuring 495/495, soundness 114/114, drift clean, disasm 0 BAD, deterministic; `decompiled/*.c` regenerated ‚Äî `$9A5D` reads `if((local11||local10)){‚Ä¶}`). **Two gate-INVISIBLE soundness traps caught (the recurring lesson):** (1) a non-entry guard with a side effect / call-valued cond would be hoisted to run unconditionally ‚Üí detector requires non-entry guards side-effect-free; (2) the first cut broke the WITNESS (`lower(raw)==bytecode`) on 19 subs by assuming the body is the fall-through ‚Üí fixed by requiring the tail fall into the body + address-contiguous chain. **The discovery sub `$9A5D` itself barely moved in V2 (13‚Üí12) ‚Äî the ‚àí30 is almost all OTHER subs: the atom folds BEYOND its purpose (Chris's "real, not chasing" bar ‚Äî MET).** Full writeup: [[decompiler-atom-log]] ¬ß"Atom 9". **‚ñ∂‚ñ∂ NEXT atoms (now clearly atlas-sourceable): mixed `(a&&b)||c` (a guard not branching straight to body), then atom-4 switch shared-merge.**
>
> **‚úÖ ATOM 4 (FIRST SHAPE) ‚Äî SWITCH empty-default==merge ‚Äî LANDED 2026-06-05 (Chris's target, `$A30D`).** The long-deferred switch mini-epic, attacked on `per_period_fief_daimyo_update_driver $A30D`. Atlas-confirmed forward (`06_switch_shared_merge.sm_default_preswitch_share`: `switch{‚Ä¶default:break;}` ‚Üí each case ‚Üí merge, empty default ‚Üí merge). **A correctness catch on the way:** Chris's desired `case 0:‚Ä¶break;` looked like it might drop a fall-through (the TEXT shows `L_A37E`/`L_A385` adjacent) ‚Äî but the bytecode (`A37E‚Üí{A381}`) proved case 0 jumps to the MERGE, not case 1 (the adjacency is the flushed-call display artifact); **case-0 break is correct.** Also pinned the readability gap: V1 "folds" this switch gate-equivalently but emits `case 0: default: L_A381: per_turn_age(); ‚Ä¶` which READS as "default runs per_turn_age" (false) ‚Äî the gate-equivalent-yet-mis-reading case a single metric misses. **Fix (3 coordinated):** (1) `switch_dispatches` detects `default_is_merge` + sets `break_target=M` even when M is interleaved by address; (2) `_structure_switch` pulls M out, converts each case's `goto M`/fall-to-M ‚Üí `break;`, omits the empty default, resumes at M; (3) **gate keystone** ‚Äî `lower_struct` now models `break` inside a switch (split `break_exit` [innermost loop OR switch] vs `continue_hdr` [innermost loop]) + an inlined no-default switch's fall = the LEXICAL merge. **Result: `$A30D` 8‚Üí0 (the EXACT clean break form, reads as game logic); V2 899 ‚Üí 883 (‚àí16, 4 subs, 0 worse); V1 unchanged (`decompiled/*.c` byte-identical)**; all gates green (witness 495/495, soundness 114/114, drift clean, deterministic). The switch-`break` gate model is the REUSABLE keystone for the remaining switch shapes (shared-return `$9C84`, non-empty default). Full writeup: [[decompiler-atom-log]] ¬ß"Atom 4 (FIRST SHAPE)".
>
> **‚ñ∂‚ñ∂ NEXT LEVER (2026-06-05, data-grounded) ‚Äî the EMIT-ORDER GATE (lexical fall-through).** `probe-residue-cause.py` over the 56 behind-V1 subs: **63% (39 subs / 141 gotos) is the "neither" bucket = address-inverted LAYOUT**, plus the blocked atom 5 (terminal-dup, 11 subs / ‚â§56). All ONE capability gap: `lower_struct`'s fall-through is address-based (`next_leader[L]`), so a CORRECT structuring emitted out of address order is rejected. atom B fixed this for if-MERGES (label-anchored `merge_after`); the general fall-through is the lever ‚Äî the hard part is a fall-reached block has NO label to anchor on. A broad atlas-vs-V2 walk is LOWER value now (the shapes are known; the gap is layout-handling, not missing inverse-lowerings). **The method, the lessons (push/pull + atlas grounding + the gate-equivalent‚âÝreads-right / negative-tests-as-backstop / don't-land-inert findings), and a dedicated WORKED-EXAMPLES section for this problem are in [[decompiler-method]]** ‚Äî `$AD38` dissected, `$8172`/`$9A5D`/`$A2D2`/`$B89B` teed up, 3 candidate approaches (lead: the reducer emits a label on a reordered fall target so the gate anchors on it like `merge_after`). Recommended entry = approach B on `$AD38`'s `AD7B‚ÜíAD67` (lands atom 5 + starts the 141-goto majority with one mechanism).
>
> **PURPOSE (the why ‚Äî [[project_nobunaga_decompiler_purpose]]):** convert the codebase into the LLM's *reliable* modality (READING code) so Pass-2 can re-walk the mechanics by reading, not by "put it in a machine and find out what happened." **DONE = the C reads as game logic, NOT goto-count‚Üí0.** Honest gotos in genuinely-irreducible regions are CORRECT (Ghidra/Hex-Rays do the same).
> **THE REFRAME (Chris, 2026-06-04):** the gotos are **assembly leftovers from a structured-C source the compiler flattened** ‚Äî the job is to RECOVER the structure the compiler erased, not to delete gotos (goto-count is a symptom; structure is the thing). This is squarely **Pass-2 / validate-the-VM**, and it should have been an EARLY step ‚Äî the template-matching detour was the tax for not building the reducer first.
>
> **‚õî THE TEMPLATE APPROACH IS RETIRED (decision 2026-06-04).** Phases 0‚Äì3 (the superseded detail below) built a per-shape pattern matcher (`structure_lines` Pattern A/B/short-circuit + `structure_loops` while/do-while/while1/siblings + `structure_switches`). It WORKS and folded the high-value structural shapes (88 loops + 18 switches; 1437‚Üí1151 gotos) ‚Äî but it **structurally cannot converge**: template-matching has no *closure under composition*, so every new combination (e.g. a short-circuit `&&` feeding an if/else with a join ‚Äî `draw_daimyo_portrait` $E76F renders 4 gotos for what is one `if/else`) looks like a brand-new shape and spawns a new sub-step. **That is the "the stack never collapses" pathology** Chris flagged 2026-06-04. Kept below as history + as the fallback structurer until V2 dominates.
>
> **‚ñ∂‚ñ∂ THE ONE OPEN FRAME ‚Äî REGION REDUCER (structural analysis / "No More Gotos").** Replace the menagerie with a single bottom-up CFG reducer:
>   - **Input = the basic-block CFG** (`vm_cfg.bytecode_cfg`), NOT line-text (the flat-text assumption is the source of every hoist/relocation bug in the templates). Leaves carry the C statements the expression layer already emits.
>   - **~7 fixed rules** ‚Äî `sequence ¬∑ if-then ¬∑ if-then-else ¬∑ short-circuit(&&/||) ¬∑ while ¬∑ do-while ¬∑ switch` ‚Äî applied to a **FIXPOINT**. Each firing collapses its subgraph into ONE abstract node consumed *identically to a basic block* ‚Üí **closed under composition** ‚Üí infinite combinations from a fixed grammar (the exact property the templates lack). This is RE-as-parsing: code-gen walks DOWN the grammar, the reducer builds UP the same grammar [[feedback_re_is_multipass_compilation]].
>   - **Irreducible residue** (a goto INTO a block / multi-entry) ‚Üí break one edge with an honest goto, continue. Few, because most of the 1151 are reducible.
>   - **Reuses the expensive half UNCHANGED:** the CFG-equivalence gate (`structured_equivalent` + the `--raw` witness) is the reducer's verifier ‚Äî propose an AST, the gate proves CFG-equivalence or REJECTS. Same safety model, zero new verification work ‚Äî the hard, valuable half is already built.
>   - **Net code DELETION** ‚Äî retires Pattern A/B + all of `structure_loops` + `structure_switches` for ~7 rules + 1 fallback [[feedback_high_quality_code_not_more_code]].
>   - **Safe cutover:** build behind a `STRUCTURE_V2` flag, run it through the SAME gate, diff its output vs the current canonical `*.c`; land it only when it folds ‚â• the templates with every gate green; **delete the templates LAST.** Nested loops + the disguised-if/else cases fall out for FREE ‚Äî they stop being separate tickets.
>   - **TEST CORPUS = the already-discovered gotos (Chris, 2026-06-04: "test it on the discovered gotos to verify it works").** The subs the templates already fold (88 loops + 18 switches + the diamonds/boolean regions) are V2's **regression oracle** ‚Äî V2 must structure them ‚â• as well, every fold gate-green; the current goto residue (35 fallbacks) + the disguised-`if/else` (`$E76F draw_daimyo_portrait`) are its **new-win targets**. Build V2 against this corpus incrementally, one rule at a time, gate-green each step.
>   - **DoD ‚Äî the epic RETURNS here:** V2 is the sole structurer; all gates green (cfg 495/495 witness + 495/495 gated, round-trip 495/45024, drift CLEAN, `--check` 0 BAD √ó4); remaining gotos are *only* genuinely-irreducible regions; `decompiled/*.c` regenerated + a spot-read confirms subs read as game logic; templates deleted.
>   - **BUILD LADDER (Chris's call 2026-06-04: persist + start a FRESH task-scoped session ‚Äî this is its plan).** Integration is one surgical swap: V2 lives behind a `STRUCTURE_V2` flag and replaces the three `structure_*` calls at `vm_decompile.py:1204-1206`, feeding the **UNCHANGED** `structured_equivalent` gate (consumes `(addr,indent,text)` line lists, so V2 must emit the same line format). **New code = a region-tree builder over `vm_cfg.bytecode_cfg` + a tree‚Üílines pretty-printer; the leaves (`state.lines`), the verifier (`structured_equivalent`), and the detectors (`boolean_regions`/`value_diamonds`/`switch_dispatches`/`natural_loop`/`back_edges`/`dominators`/`post_dominators`) ALL already exist in `vm_cfg.py`.** Each rung lands gate-green + measured on the corpus:
>     0. **Harness + passthrough ‚Äî ‚úÖ DONE 2026-06-04.** `tools/vm_reduce.py` (the reducer's home; rung-0 `reduce()` = passthrough returning the raw lines + the full build-ladder docstring), `vm_decompile.STRUCTURE_V2` flag (default OFF) + `structure_v2()` delegate, and the `decompile()` gate-wiring split into a self-contained V2 branch (one-pass full-or-honest-goto gate) vs the untouched V1 template branch (`elif`). `tools/v2-corpus.py` = THE regression oracle, wired first: runs all 495 subs through BOTH structurers, categorises V2 (folded/honest-goto/gate-reject), and reports the **BEHIND-V1 work-list** (subs where V2 leaves more gotos than templates ‚Üí target 0). **Rung-0 numbers:** V2 passthrough = 495 honest-goto / 0 folded / 0 reject; goto totals raw **2068** ‚Üí V1(templates) **1151** ‚Üí V2 **2068**; **296 subs behind V1** = the ladder work-list. Gates green BOTH ways: default path (`STRUCTURE_V2=False`) `decompiled/*.c` **byte-identical**, V1 cfg-gate 495/495 + 495/495 (34 fallbacks = baseline); V2 path (`STRUCTURE_V2=True`) cfg-gate **495/495 + 495/495, 0 fallbacks** (passthrough is trivially CFG-faithful = raw). The harness + gate + oracle are proven BEFORE any reduction rule can introduce a bug.
>     1. **Block model + trivial emit ‚Äî ‚úÖ DONE 2026-06-04.** `vm_reduce._partition` groups the raw leaves into `{leader: [(addr,indent,text)‚Ä¶]}` by `block_of(addr)` (preserving each line's list order within its block), and `reduce()` emits the buckets in leader (address) order. **Faithfulness PROVEN across all 495:** the line MULTISET is unchanged (0 subs add/drop/alter a line) and every block's WITHIN-block order is byte-identical to raw (0 within-block reorders). The only difference from raw is **block-order normalization on 105 subs** ‚Äî the decompiler's flushed-call artifact (a discarded side-effecting CALL is printed at its later flush point but tagged with its earlier call-site addr, so raw prints e.g. `ui_helper_d759()` $8096 *after* the label `L_8099:` though it executes first; per-block emit restores true address/execution order). All 105 are gate-certified CFG-equivalent. V2 cfg-gate **495/495 + 495/495, 0 fallbacks**; default path byte-identical. So the block‚Üîline round-trip is faithful at the block granularity the gate validates ‚Äî the foundation rungs 2-6 build the region tree on.
>     2. **`sequence` + `if-then` + `if-then-else` ‚Äî ‚úÖ DONE 2026-06-04.** `vm_reduce._structure` recursively structures the single-entry region of an ACYCLIC sub (entry‚ÜíEXIT) into a Seq/IfThen/IfElse tree, using the immediate post-dominator as each 2-way branch's merge; `_emit` pretty-prints it. Branch polarity mirrors the decompiler exactly (raw `if (RAWC) goto L_T` ‚Üí then-body = the FALL-THROUGH arm, cond = `_neg(RAWC)`, and `simplify_expression` cleans `!((a<b))`‚Üí`(a>=b)`). **Result: 112 subs folded, gotos 2068‚Üí1845, 0 gate-rejects** (all fallback decisions STRUCTURAL ‚Äî the gate stays a pure backstop, never the control mechanism). Loops (back edge present) and switches bail to the rung-1 flat emit (rungs 4/5). **Two soundness guards earned their keep against real rejects** (the gate caught them; I converted each to a structural rule so they bail to flat, not gate-reject): (1) **merge lexical-adjacency** ‚Äî `next_leader(max consumed) == merge`, else an outer arm laid out between a construct and its shared merge interleaves (`$8F0A`, twin nested if/else sharing one merge); (2) **arm address-disjointness** ‚Äî `max(then_used) < min(else_used)`, else emitting then-then-else reverses address order and the address-based gate mis-routes (`$A853`, a nested if whose arm sits at a higher addr than the outer else-body). Both are the invariant *lexical order == address order* that the gate (and readable C) rely on. **Faithfulness PROVEN over all 495:** the NON-scaffold statement multiset is unchanged (0 subs alter a real statement ‚Äî only `if`/braces/`goto`/labels change). Gate green: V2 cfg-gate **495/495 + 495/495, 0 fallbacks**; default path byte-identical. (Pre-existing cosmetic noise inherited from V1, NOT a regression: empty `if(c){}else{}` diamonds from un-contracted value-diamonds ‚Äî e.g. `read_frame_timer` $D29D, where V2 actually folds the surrounding gotos V1 left.)
>     3. **`short-circuit (&&/||)`** ‚Äî reuse `boolean_regions`/`recover_bool_formula`. Target = the disguised-if/else (`$E76F draw_daimyo_portrait`, `is_tile_in_bounds`).
>     4. **`while` / `do-while` / `while(1)` ‚Äî ‚úÖ DONE 2026-06-04.** `vm_reduce._structure_loop` collapses each natural loop (`back_edges`/`natural_loop`) to ONE `('loop',‚Ä¶)` AST node the surrounding walk consumes like a basic block, so rung-2 if/then/else composes inside AND around loops (the closure payoff ‚Äî no `_emit_break_continue` gymnastics). Form read from the CFG: pre-test `while(C)` (header is the 2-way exit test; rotated for-loops lift ONLY the test expr, the update keeps its addr at the body bottom), post-test `do{}while(C)` (a single latch's 2-way test), `while(1)` (exits via break/return). Inside a body, an edge to the header = `continue`, to the exit = `break`, a bare-return target = an INLINED `return X;` (early-return idiom; kills the shared-return-tail cross-edge that blocked acyclic subs too); in-body merges use a body-LOCAL post-dominator (drop loop-leaving edges + sink-fill, so a breaking arm doesn't pull the merge to EXIT). **Result: 171 subs fold (112‚Üí171), gotos 1845‚Üí1624 (raw 2068), behind-V1 197‚Üí142, 0 gate-rejects** (the reducer is SOUND ‚Äî every emitted fold passes the gate). All fallbacks are STRUCTURAL bails earned against real gate-rejects (57‚Üí0 during the build): nested loops (4d), compound multi-exit-test loops (`while(a&&b)`, need rung 3), a loop whose exit is non-adjacent or a pure-routing/invisible block (loop-as-tail-of-if-arm), an empty then-arm hiding a goto-side body. V2 cfg-gate **495/495 + 495/495, 0 fallbacks**; default `*.c` byte-identical (`vm-cfg-gate.py --v2` added to validate the V2 path). Remaining 142-behind = 97 loops (4d/rung-3), 32 acyclic (rung 3 short-circuit), 13 switch (rung 5).
>     5. **`switch`** ‚Äî reuse `switch_dispatches`. Target = the 18 switches + the 7 nested-in-`if`/`while` residue (the tree nests natively, so they fall out for free).
>     6. **Irreducible local fallback ‚Äî ‚úÖ LARGELY DONE 2026-06-04 (session 6).** The convergence move: when the clean recovery raises on a shape it can't own, DON'T flatten the whole sub ‚Äî keep that ONE edge as an honest goto and structure everything around it. Landed incrementally, every step gate-green + sound (0 gate-rejects throughout; the gate stays a pure backstop, never the control mechanism): **(a) self-loop do-while fix** ‚Äî a self-loop (header==latch) was mis-detected as a pre-test while, walking into its own visited header ‚Üí spurious cross_edge (cross_edge ‚àí13 subs). **(b) bare self-loop fold/keep** ‚Äî `loop=={h}`: while(1){stmts} when it carries statements, else an honest `goto self`; new `_insert_labels` post-pass restores `L_xxxx:` for any kept honest goto (clean folds emit none ‚Üí no-op). **(c) the if/else honest-goto fallback** ‚Äî the big one: a 2-way branch the structurer can't own (shared continuation = cross_edge, non-adjacent merge, goto-past-merge, empty-then, reversed arms) is kept as `if (rawcond) goto L_t;` verbatim (CFG-faithful by construction) and the walk continues at fall. SOUNDNESS GUARD: only when goto_block is reachable FROM fall (else it would orphan the target ‚Üí re-raise, whole-sub bails). **(d) rung 4d nested loops** compose for free (drop the blanket inner-header bail) with two precise structural guards: multi-latch inner, and inner-while-ending-a-do-while-body whose exit is the enclosing do-while's EMPTY latch (renders as `} while` scaffold the gate can't anchor ‚Üí bail). **(e) multi-exit loops via early-return exits** ‚Äî an exit to a bare-return block is an early return (inlined by `_terminal`), not a competing exit; drop those from the count (and in the all-return search-loop case, the header's own non-body successor is the natural exit). **(f) pure-routing exit at top level** ‚Äî only bail it inside a BOUNDED region (if-arm / loop body, where the gate scans past the boundary); at the sub's top level contract() absorbs it. **Session 6 net: behind-V1 127‚Üí82, folded 287‚Üí311, V2 gotos ~1498‚Üí1264, 0 gate-rejects, hard gate 495/495+495/495 both paths, default `*.c` byte-identical.** Remaining 82-behind = genuine multi-exit loops needing break-via-goto (19), cross-edges in loop bodies (18), un-foldable switches (9), goto-past-merge (4), compound pre-tests (6), a few merge/exit-adjacency tails. `$9A0F` fully-rotated loop is ACCEPTED residue (honest goto).
>     7. **Cutover** ‚Äî V2 folds ‚â• templates across all 495, every gate green ‚Üí flip the default on, regen `decompiled/*.c`, spot-read, DELETE `structure_loops`/`structure_lines`/`structure_switches` + dead helpers. Epic RETURNS.
>     **‚ñ∂ AUDIT of the 82 behind-V1 (2026-06-04, "audit first" before writing more reducer code ‚Äî Chris's call).** Verdict: **0 of 82 are genuinely-irreducible residue to accept ‚Äî the cutover bar (behind-V1 == 0) STANDS, relax nothing.** Measured via `v2-corpus.py --behind`, classifying each by V2-gotos vs raw-gotos: **81 of 82 are WHOLE-SUB BAILS** (V2_gotos == raw_gotos ‚Äî V2 gives up structuring the ENTIRE sub over ONE unhandled local shape, discarding the cleanly-reducible loops/branches around it). Canonical example `$A30D` (season-turn): two counted `while` loops + a `switch(current_season)`, all trivially reducible, emitted **100% flat** because the switch's shared-tail cross-edge raised `_NotReducible`. Only `$9F04` is a true partial (V2 1 / V1 0). **ROOT CAUSE: rung-6 local containment is implemented for ONLY the if/then/else 2-way-branch bail** (the `try/except _NotReducible` at `vm_reduce.py:359-441`). Bails from `_structure_loop` (multi_exit_loop / nested_loop / exit_not_adjacent / exit_is_dowhile_latch / compound_pretest, called unguarded at `:299-305`), the linear-strand `cross_edge` raise (`:314`), `multiway` (`:443`), and the `switch_unfoldable` pre-check (`:734`) ALL propagate uncaught to `reduce()`'s top `except` (`:748-750`) ‚Üí whole-sub `_flat_emit`. **THE FIX is ONE structural property, not 12 separate rules:** generalize the if/else local fallback into a `_flat_span` ‚Äî when any rule can't own a region (loop / switch / linear strand), keep THAT region as an honest-goto span and continue structuring around it. Recovers most of the 346 recoverable gotos across ALL bail reasons at once. Lands as a few SOUND increments (the gate anchors by address, so a flat span must stay address-contiguous and the continuation must anchor on the address-next block ‚Äî the same soundness pattern the existing `ifgoto` fallback's `_reaches` guard already proves), biggest-lever first: cross_edge (97 gotos / 18 subs) ‚Üí multi_exit_loop (77 / 19) ‚Üí switch_unfoldable (50 / 9). **This finishes rung 6 (local containment was always its thesis); it is NOT a new open frame.**
>     **‚ñ∂ SESSION 7a ‚Äî cross_edge bucket attacked (2026-06-04). behind-V1 82‚Üí77, V2 gotos 1264‚Üí1242, folded 311‚Üí314, gate-green BOTH paths (V2 495/495+495/495 0-fallback; V1 default byte-identical; drift clean).** Attacking cross_edge surfaced THREE bugs the whole-sub bail had masked (instrumented the raise site ‚Üí split `cross_edge` into `cross_edge_top` [merge/after re-entry] vs `cross_edge_fall` [single-succ fall-into-visited]): **(1)** the `while(1)` endless path pre-marked the header visited then walked the body FROM it ‚Üí instant spurious `cross_edge_top` on its own header (every multi-latch/endless loop bailed); fixed by dropping the pre-add (`_terminal` already maps edges-to-h as `continue`). **(2)** a MULTI-LATCH loop has no sound single-construct form (a `while(1)` body-tail `if(C) continue;` exits via fall, but the gate reads that fall as the back-edge and loses the exit) ‚Äî built the audit's **`_flat_span`** (keep the loop's RAW lines as an honest-goto region, structure everything around it, exactly as V1 leaves them) and routed multi-latch loops to it. **(3)** pre-test fired BEFORE do-while for a loop matching BOTH shapes, rendering an unsound body-tail break; fixed by computing `clean_dowhile` (single 2-way exit-testing latch) and gating pre-test off it (a 1-way for-update latch doesn't divert, so for-loops are unaffected). Canonical win `$88AC` (4 stacked loops incl. one multi-latch): whole-bail 6 gotos ‚Üí folds to **2, matching V1** (multi-latch as honest gotos + a do-while + two do-whiles). Remaining cross_edge: `cross_edge_top` 4 subs/55g (big improper regions), `cross_edge_fall` 10/32 (single-succ cut regresses inside if/else arm probes ‚Äî needs the cut confined to committed strands). **NEXT lever by gain: multi_exit_loop (21/80) ‚Äî `_flat_span` likely generalizes straight to it.**
>     **‚ñ∂ SESSION 7b ‚Äî multi_exit_loop CONVERGENT-EXIT (2026-06-04). behind-V1 77‚Üí75, V2 gotos 1242‚Üí1205 (‚àí37), bank 2 reaches V1 PARITY (401=401), gate-green both paths (V2 0-fallback, V1 byte-identical, drift clean).** Most "multi-exit" loops aren't really multi-exit ‚Äî their N immediate exit targets CONVERGE on one block (the others are loop-private "exit shims" that flow to it). New `_convergent_exit`: pick the convergence block `c` as the single exit and let the shims be walked as in-body break paths (shim-aware `region = loop | shims` drives the exit-adjacency check + consumed accounting). `c` may be a target itself (`$8C45`'s `8C6D`, reached directly + via the `local11=1` shim `8C61`) or a common successor of all targets (`$ADF6`'s `AE77`). Canonical win `$8C45`: whole-bail 5 gotos ‚Üí **0, BEATING V1's 1** (`while(local10){ ‚Ä¶; if(ai_state){ local11=1; break; } local10--; }`). multi_exit_loop 21‚Üí17 subs. Remaining: genuine divergent exits, second/nested loops in the same sub (`$A625`'s `A686`), multi-stmt early-return exits (tried widening the return-exclusion to all EXIT-only blocks ‚Üí net regression + reject, reverted), and shims with multi-hop paths the 2-block region misses (`$ADF6` now reaches `exit_not_adjacent`). **NEXT lever by gain: cross_edge_top (4/55) or switch_unfoldable (9/50, `_flat_span` should port cleanly).**
>     **‚ñ∂ SESSION 7c ‚Äî switch_unfoldable LOCALIZED + orphan self-check (2026-06-04). behind-V1 75‚Üí74, V2 gotos 1205‚Üí1200, folded 316‚Üí321, bank 2 drops BELOW V1 (398<401), gate-green both paths (0-fallback / byte-identical / drift clean).** The old whole-sub `switch_unfoldable` pre-check is replaced by LOCAL handling inside `_structure`: an un-foldable switch dispatch is kept as an honest flat span of its whole TERRITORY (the dispatch + every case body reachable up to its post-dominator merge ‚Äî NOT just the dispatch block, or the goto-only case bodies orphan), continuing the walk at the merge so the code AROUND the switch still folds. Guarded to span the whole forward cone (no continuation) when the merge wraps mid-territory or is a shared continuation with external preds (else the address-based gate mis-routes ‚Äî `$D14E`). `switch_unfoldable` (9 subs/50g) is GONE from the bail histogram ‚Äî 8 fold/improve; the bucket is cleared. **Plus a GENERAL `orphan` STRUCTURAL self-check in `reduce()`:** a sound structuring preserves every real statement (assignment/call/return ‚Äî content the folds emit verbatim, vs scaffolding they rewrite); if a content stmt vanished, a block was orphaned ‚Üí bail to flat BEFORE the gate sees it, keeping the gate a pure backstop and the 0-reject invariant. This caught `$D14E` (two un-foldable switches sharing a continuation that feeds the still-unsolved cross-edge structurer ‚Üí drops blocks); it bails cleanly as `orphan` (1 sub/11g) instead of gate-rejecting. **Session 7 net (a+b+c): behind-V1 82‚Üí74, V2 gotos 1264‚Üí1200 (‚àí64), folded 311‚Üí321, 0 gate-rejects throughout. NEXT levers: exit_not_adjacent (23/66), multi_exit_loop (17/72, divergent/nested), cross_edge (15/93, the deferred improper-region structurer ‚Äî also unblocks `$D14E`).**
>     **‚ñ∂ SESSION 7d ‚Äî cross-edge cut + REDUCER SELF-VALIDATION (2026-06-04). behind-V1 74‚Üí70, V2 gotos 1200‚Üí1139, folded 321‚Üí324 ‚Äî and V2's TOTAL gotos (1139) drop BELOW V1's (1151): the reducer now beats the templates in aggregate.** The cross-edge residue (a `goto` to a shared mid-function continuation ‚Äî `goto cleanup`/`done`, short-circuit-OR) has NO structured-operator equivalent (`break`/`return` already cover loop/fn exits), so the faithful handling KEEPS one honest goto and structures around it ‚Äî what V1 and Ghidra/Hex-Rays do. Landed: **(a)** a FORWARD-only cross-edge cut in the linear walk ‚Äî a single-succ fall into an already-emitted *later* block becomes `goto L_s` (forward never reverses lexical-vs-address order; backward bails). **(b)** relaxed the if/else honest-goto fallback's `_reaches` re-raise guard (it existed to prevent orphaning). **(c)** the keystone ‚Äî `reduce()` now SELF-VALIDATES its output against `structured_equivalent` (the CFG-equivalence gate) and reverts to flat on failure. This is the design's own safety model applied as the reducer's acceptance test: composed local fallbacks (honest-goto cuts / flat spans / convergent exits) can emit a CFG-divergent LAYOUT (lexical‚âÝaddress order, orphaned continuation) that no bespoke structural guard caught ‚Äî rather than enumerate every hazard, PROVE equivalence or revert. Makes "0 gate-rejects downstream" AUTOMATIC and subsumes the ad-hoc orphan check. Simple shared-continuations now fold (‚àí61 gotos this step); genuinely-improper layouts (`$8BEA`, where V1 only wins by physically nesting the goto-target inside a sibling's `else` ‚Äî flat-text trickery a region tree won't do) bail cleanly as `self_gate` (23 subs/106g ‚Äî the new top bucket, mostly genuinely-improper residue). **Session 7 net so far: behind 82‚Üí70, V2 gotos 1264‚Üí1139 (‚àí125), folded 311‚Üí324, 0 rejects. V2 < V1 aggregate.**
>     **‚ñ∂ SESSION 7e ‚Äî REGION-LEVEL PARTIAL FALLBACK (2026-06-04). folded 324‚Üí350 (+26 subs recover structure), V2 gotos 1133 (stays below V1 1151), behind 70‚Üí67, 0 rejects.** The keystone for the whole-bailers: previously ONE improper region (a cross-edge, a non-adjacent-exit loop, a divergent multi-exit) flattened the ENTIRE sub via the all-or-nothing self-gate. Now `reduce()`: (1) tries whole-sub structuring, self-validated; (2) on failure, DECOMPOSES the sub at its post-dominator SPINE (the immediate-post-dom chain entry‚Üí‚Ä¶‚ÜíEXIT ‚Äî the blocks all paths cross) into single-entry/single-exit regions, structures each INDEPENDENTLY, and keeps a region structured only if (it structured + every other region flat) self-validates AND emits ‚â§ the flat span's gotos (an honest-goto cut can turn a raw fall-through into an explicit goto, so over-aggressive structuring is rejected in favour of the leaner flat). Regions join linearly at the articulation points, so a divergence in one improper region no longer destroys the reducible regions around it ‚Äî every kept piece CFG-proven. Also converted the `exit_not_adjacent` / divergent-`multi_exit_loop` loop bails to loop-local flat-spans (the region-fallback's per-loop analogue). **Spot-read `$A30D` (season-turn): was 100% flat, now structures BOTH counted loops (drift-luck + natural-death sweeps) cleanly, keeping only the improper `switch(season)` as honest gotos ‚Äî reads as game logic, the epic's actual DoD.** Cost: region-recovery's O(regions) extra gate calls fire only for the ~70 failing subs; full regen stays ~2.4s. **Session 7 net: behind 82‚Üí67, V2 gotos 1264‚Üí1133 (‚àí131), folded 311‚Üí350 (+39), 0 gate-rejects throughout, V2 < V1 aggregate.** Residual 67 behind are genuinely-improper (V1 wins only via flat-text goto-into-block trickery) or need bespoke loop-model work ‚Äî the case for reframing the cutover bar from "behind-V1==0" to "V2 ‚â§ V1 aggregate + residue genuinely-irreducible" (already MET). Cosmetic polish open: drop redundant `goto L_next; L_next:` at region boundaries (CFG-neutral peephole, guard on next_leader).
>     **‚ñ∂ SESSION 7f ‚Äî backward cuts + self_gate ROOT-CAUSE (2026-06-04). behind 67‚Üí66, V2 gotos 1133‚Üí1126, 0 rejects.** Allowed BACKWARD cross-edge honest-goto cuts (self-validation makes them safe ‚Äî a reversing cut self-gates, a holding one is kept; covers shared `return`-block continuations reached from a later block). Then DIAGNOSED the 22 reduce-level `self_gate` residue (the only subs that render WORSE than V1 ‚Äî whole-flat goto-soup): **they are genuinely IMPROPER regions.** Spine is trivial ([entry, EXIT]) because early returns make every block's post-dominator EXIT (region-recovery can't decompose them), and **14 of 22 are LOOPLESS pure-branch tangles** (`$AD38`: shared `return` block `$AD58` reached from a LATER block `$AD67`; `$A2D2`: a 42-goto switch+branch handler V1 folds to 19). V1 wins ONLY by emitting blocks in ADDRESS-LAYOUT order with gotos ‚Äî physically placing `$AD67` before `$AD7B` and jumping back INTO the then-arm ‚Äî flat-text trickery a control-flow-following region reducer structurally cannot do (confirmed: V2 builds the right-looking tree but the address-based gate rejects the backward continuation `$AD67`<`$AD7B`). **CONCLUSION: matching V1 on these needs an ADDRESS-ORDERED partial-structure emitter** (walk leaders by address; fold loops + address-forward if/else IN PLACE; honest-goto the improper edges) ‚Äî the Ghidra/Hex-Rays model for irreducible regions, a defined ~bounded build that partially re-derives `structure_lines` composably. Per the epic's PURPOSE these 22 ARE the "genuinely-irreducible residue ‚Ä¶ honest gotos are CORRECT" ‚Äî the only gap is V2 flat-spans the WHOLE sub (goto-soup) instead of structuring the reducible parts WITHIN the irreducible layout. **CUTOVER OPTIONS: (a) build the address-ordered emitter ‚Üí the 22 get partial structure (read far better than flat, may still trail V1's goto-count) ‚Üí cleanest; (b) reframe the bar (V2<V1 aggregate + residue genuinely-irreducible, already MET) and cut over now, the 22 rendering as honest-goto until (a) lands.** Session 7 net: behind 82‚Üí66, V2 gotos 1264‚Üí1126 (‚àí138), folded 311‚Üí350, 0 gate-rejects throughout, V2 < V1 aggregate. 7 commits.
