>     **‚ñ∂ SESSION 7g ‚Äî disjoint-region dead-code fix + CFG-neutral peephole (2026-06-04). behind 66‚Üí59, V2 gotos 1126‚Üí1045 (‚àí81), V2 folds-below-raw 277‚Üí289, 0 rejects, 114/114 reducer tests pass, default `*.c` byte-untouched.** Two SOUND emit-quality wins (both V2-path only, self-validated): **(a) DISJOINT-REGION FIX (‚àí60).** The region-partial-fallback's post-dom SPINE decomposition was NOT producing a true partition: when the spine cut through a loop, a back-edge from a LATER spine point (the loop latch) re-collected the ENTIRE loop body into an earlier-overlapping region, whose `_flat_span` then re-emitted the whole body as UNREACHABLE DEAD-DUPLICATE code ‚Äî CFG-equivalent (so the gate passed it) but DOUBLING the goto count (`$9A18`: body emitted twice, 31 gotos ‚Üí 16). Fix: each region now walls off EVERY OTHER spine point (`spine_walls - {Pi}`), not just its exit Pj ‚Äî spine points are articulation points so nothing legitimately between Pi and Pj is one, making the regions disjoint. **(b) CFG-NEUTRAL PEEPHOLE (‚àí21).** `_peephole` drops a standalone `goto L_X;` whose IMMEDIATELY-following emitted line is `L_X:` (redundant goto-to-fall-through, the honest-goto-cut / flat-span join boundary's `goto L_next; L_next:`) + any now-dead label; wired into `_validates` and KEPT only if it still proves `structured_equivalent` (the gate is the backstop for the rare emit-order‚âÝaddress-order divergence). **TRIED & REVERTED: loop-aware spine** (filter cut points strictly inside a loop's address span so a loop stays whole in one region) ‚Äî REGRESSED 1066‚Üí1080. Diagnosis: the `none` bucket is NOT clean-loops-cut-by-spine; those loop BODIES are genuinely improper (`$9A18`'s cursor cross-edges), so even a whole-loop region bails to flat ‚Äî coarsening just merged more into the flat bail. The real lever is EMIT QUALITY, confirming 7f's address-ordered-emitter conclusion. **Remaining 59-behind** = `none` 42 (non-adjacent ROUTING-block forwarding `L_997D: goto L_9976;` + SWITCH-case inlining `case N: goto L` vs V1's inlined bodies ‚Äî the address-ordered-emitter work, must redirect predecessors under the address-based gate, not just delete lines) + `self_gate` 17 (genuinely-improper, per 7f). **Cutover bar (V2<V1 aggregate) now met DECISIVELY: 1045 vs 1151 (‚àí106).** Chris's call: commit these, defer cutover-vs-emitter to next session.
>     **‚ñ∂ REFRAME ‚Äî THE RESIDUE IS A PHANTOM (2026-06-04). `tools/probe-cfg-reducibility.py` census: all 495 subs are FORMALLY REDUCIBLE, 0 irreducible; all 59 behind-V1 are reducible.** So 7f's "genuinely irreducible residue needing an address-ordered emitter" was WRONG ‚Äî an artifact of top-down post-dom decomposition manufacturing false irreducibility from shared continuations (N blocks ‚Üí a shared `return`). A reducible CFG always has a goto-free structured form ‚üπ the 59 behind-V1 are 100% MISSING-ATOMS (un-written inverse-lowerings, e.g. branch-to-terminal ‚áí `if(!c) return;`), 0% irreducibility ‚üπ the engine is structured-source-shaped and a finite bottom-up atom table decompiles it FULLY (nothing to "accept as honest gotos"). The goto-count metric was measuring missing atoms the whole time, which is what drove the rung-6 spawl (top-down has no graceful local fallback, so one was hand-built per shape). **NEXT SESSION starts at [[decompiler-bottom-up-thesis]] (`decompiler-bottom-up-thesis.md`): an atom-extraction loop ‚Äî pick a behind sub, NAME the forward lowering it inverts (gate against 1-offs), add the inverse as a CFG PRE-CONTRACTION (same mechanism as the value-diamond pre-contraction ‚Äî bottom-up by composition), DELETE the rung-6 handler it obsoletes, re-run the census (a real atom clears SEVERAL subs, a 1-off clears one). Solve-in-place and the bottom-up refactor are the SAME activity done this way; you reach the refactor by attrition, net-negative on rules, no big-bang rewrite. PoC (compile Small-C/lcc, read the jump patterns) hands you the complete finite atom table; it's rule-sourcing, not the architecture decision.** First atoms by the cross-tab: branch-to-terminal guard (`shared-ret>0` cluster) + switch-case inline (`shared-ret=0` cluster); test cases `$9A5D` (minimal) / `$A2D2` (biggest, gap 23) / `$A221` (non-guard atom).
>     **‚ñ∂ SESSION 8 ‚Äî ATOM LOOP STARTED FROM THE ENTRY FUNCTION `vm_bootstrap $A778` (2026-06-05). V2 gotos 1045‚Üí1025 (‚àí20), 3 subs improved / 0 worse, 0 gate-rejects, hard gate 495/495, 114/114 reducer tests, deterministic, default `*.c` byte-identical.** Chris's call: drive the loop from the project SPINE, not the synthetic test cases. `vm_bootstrap` was a WHOLE-SUB bail for both V1 and V2 (14 gotos each) ‚Äî its real shape is a **triple-nested `while(1)`** (per-game ‚Üí per-turn `$A785` ‚Üí per-fief `$A806`) with a `&128` abort gate that `goto`s `DISPLAY $A843` from all three levels. Two genuine **atoms** (missing inverse-lowerings) fold it to **1 goto** (the abort, a multi-level break C can't express ‚Äî Ghidra/Hex-Rays keep it too):
>       1. **MULTI-LATCH `while(1)`-with-`continue`s** ‚Äî a loop with >1 back-edge is the inverse of the compiler lowering each `continue` to a jump-to-header. Replaced the blanket multi-latch `_flat_span` bail (+ the `nested_loop` rung-4d guard, now DELETED) with an ATTEMPT at `while(1)` (body edges to the header render `continue`, to the exit `break`), reduce()'s self-validation the backstop. The one unsound shape (body-TAIL `if(C) continue;` whose fall IS the loop-back, where the gate collapses the exit into the back-edge) is handled by the both-terminal walk collapsing it to a single `if(!C) break;`. Folds `$88AC render_boot_title_screens` 2‚Üí0 (the session-7a "4 stacked loops" example, now BEATS V1) + `$D59D` 5‚Üí0.
>       2. **MULTI-LEVEL break = honest goto** ‚Äî a loop exit that escapes the PARENT loop too (`far_by_loop`, computed in `_structure_loop` relative to `outer_loop`) is kept as an honest `goto L_t` inside the body (via `_terminal`) and DROPPED from the loop's exit set, so the remaining single-level exit makes the loop foldable. This is what lets `vm_bootstrap`'s 3-level `goto DISPLAY` fold: each inner loop keeps the goto; only the outermost loop that still CONTAINS `$A843` breaks to it. Also tightened the `exit_is_dowhile_latch` bail to fire ONLY for single-latch (do-while) parents (a multi-latch parent renders `while(1)`, where the latch is a normal `if(cond) continue;` block the gate anchors on fine).
>     **Verified empirically** (not just the hard gate's formal CFG-equivalence): ran the `$A78C..A7B0` region's real ROM bytecode through `nobunaga_vm` for all 3 input combos ‚Äî `resume‚âÝ1` skips the whole block (no calls, ‚Üí `$A7B0`); `resume==1 & flags&128` runs `call_bank_wrap` but SKIPS `call_bank10_entry` (‚Üí `$A7AD`); `resume==1 & !(flags&128)` runs BOTH ‚Äî matching the fold's `if(resume==1){‚Ä¶; if(!(flags&128)){call_bank10_entry();} planner();}` exactly. (This also resolved Chris's review catch: the raw text's `L_A7AD: call_bank10_entry()` is the **flushed-call display artifact** ‚Äî a void call tagged with its earlier call-site addr `$A7A9` but printed after the `$A7AD` label; the address column proves the `goto L_A7AD` SKIPS the call, it does not jump-to-next-line, and the block-model fold re-orders it correctly. His negative-logic intuition `if(!X){body}` is precisely the `_neg(rawcond)` inversion the reducer applies.) **The entry function ‚Äî the project spine ‚Äî now reads as the documented per-game/per-turn/per-fief loop nest.** Note vs the thesis's "pure CFG pre-contraction" framing: these two are LOOP-SHAPE atoms, so they live in the loop structurer (`_structure_loop`/`_terminal`), not as `bytecode_cfg` pre-contractions (which fit expression-layer atoms like value-diamonds) ‚Äî but the spirit holds (named the inverse-lowering, deleted the rung-6 bail it obsoletes, measured on the corpus). Remaining behind-59 unchanged (these atoms are rare shapes; the behind list is still `none` 41 + `self_gate` 18 = the address-ordered-emitter / switch-inline work). **RETURN:** the atom loop is live and proven on the spine; next pick is the `none`-bucket atoms (routing-block forwarding + switch-case inline).
>     **‚ñ∂ SESSION 9 ‚Äî ATOM 3 (routing-block absorption) + the running ATOM LOG (2026-06-05). V2 gotos 1025‚Üí988 (‚àí37), 7 subs improved / 0 worse, behind-V1 59‚Üí57, 0 gate-rejects, hard gate 495/495, 114/114, deterministic, default `*.c` byte-identical.** Chris's discipline: **fix as we go but LOG each case** to tell a real atom from a 1-off ‚Üí new ledger [[decompiler-atom-log]] (`decompiler-atom-log.md`), one row per atom (shape / forward-lowering / found-in / subs-cleared / Œîgotos). Walked the 2nd function `init_new_game_state $89A3` (was 16 gotos): derived the target FIRST (an outer redo-`while(1)` wrapping an early-return + 7 for/do-while loops + an if/break), then found ONE atom explained the whole gap. **Atom 3 = routing-block absorption:** a pure-routing `L_X: goto L_Y;` stub (1-succ, no statement ‚Äî the compiler's fall-through forwarder between chained loops, e.g. `$8A05: goto L_8A13`) was BAILED by `_structure_loop`'s adjacency guard on the theory "it emits nothing so the gate can't anchor the exit." **That theory was an untested defensive guess and was WRONG:** the stub emits as an empty block, the gate's `first_real_block` scans PAST it to the real target, and `contract()` drops it on BOTH raw+struct so they match. DELETED the `bounded and routing(e)` clause (+ the now-dead `bounded` param); only the genuine non-adjacent `nxt[max(region)] != e` bail remains; self-validation backstops. **Generalized to 7 subs** (`$89A3` 16‚Üí0, `$83E2` 34‚Üí30, `$813C`/`$840B`/`$A066` ‚Üí0, `$90E8`/`$911E` 5‚Üí1) ‚Äî a real atom, the `none`-bucket's adjacent-routing slice. **Lesson logged:** audit the other defensive `bounded`/adjacency bails the same way (assume the gate can handle it, test, keep only what self-validation actually rejects). **Still open:** NON-adjacent routing (stub not the address-next block) = the rest of `none` = candidate atom #4. RETURN to the log for the next pick.
>     **‚ñ∂ SESSION 9b ‚Äî GUARD AUDIT + ATOM-4 (SWITCH) DEEP-DIVE (2026-06-05, no fold change ‚Äî diagnosis + tooling).** (1) **Guard audit** (`tools/probe-bail-audit.py`, the atom-3 lesson globalized): suppressed every gate-limitation guard via `vm_reduce._AUDIT_SKIP` and measured ‚Äî **atom 3 was the EXCEPTION, not the rule.** 5 of 6 guards are well-calibrated (`arm_order` is load-bearing: +30 gotos if removed); only `merge_not_adjacent` has latent ‚àí21 but breaks 5 subs, and routing-skip refinements REGRESSED (routing absorption is LOOP-EXIT-specific, does NOT generalize to if-merges). (2) **Switch deep-dive (atom-4 candidate, [[decompiler-atom-log]]):** switches = **365 gotos across 36 subs, >‚Öì of the 988 corpus** ‚Äî the biggest lever. VM format confirmed (`$D5` contiguous stores `default` BEFORE case targets ‚Äî Chris's "switch{default;case0;‚Ä¶}"; `$D9` noncontiguous default-last; cases fall through C-style). Two failure modes BOTH rooted in the switch's exit `M=post-dom(S)` being a SHARED block (shared returns / pre-switch guards reach it): **(A)** 11 switches fail detection (single-entry / enclosed-domination reject the shared/interleaved M; excluding M recovers only 2/11 ‚Äî multi-shape); **(B)** 8 of 25 detected switches (incl. the corpus's biggest sub `$A2D2`=42 gotos) flat-span in context because the tier-2 post-dom spine cuts AT M while the switch territory straddles it ‚Üí `cross_edge_top`. **Explored B per Chris's call ‚Üí "B IS A":** the in-context failure is the same shared/interleaved-merge problem; M is simultaneously the switch exit, a shared block, an interleaved-layout block, AND a spine articulation point ‚Äî all four flavors collapse to "we don't model M as a first-class shared switch-exit." **‚ñ∂‚ñ∂ NEXT SESSION (Chris has a plan): the PRINCIPLED atom-4 = model `M=post-dom(S)` as a first-class shared switch EXIT** (excluded from the case-target + enclosed checks; tier-2 must not cut a region inside a switch territory). "An interesting experiment" ‚Äî start from the [[decompiler-atom-log]] atom-4 entry (diagnosis is airtight + won't need re-deriving).
>
> **üîí DESIGN DECISIONS LOCKED (Chris, 2026-06-04 ‚Äî settled before rung 1, plan-walked against the $E76F corpus):**
>   1. **Rule-match order = a TUNABLE, not a constant.** The fixpoint tries an order (candidate: loop ‚Üí switch ‚Üí ifelse ‚Üí ifthen ‚Üí short-circuit ‚Üí seq); a sub that *blocks* (no rule fires where one structurally should) is the signal to permute. Rung-1 harness exposes order as a parameter so it's A/B'd on the corpus, not guessed.
>   2. **Irreducibility is STRUCTURAL; the gate is a pure backstop.** V2 detects "no rule fires ‚Üí break one edge itself" (rung 6); `structured_equivalent` only catches rule *bugs*, it is NOT the control mechanism (inverts the template era, where gate-reject drove fallback).
>   3. **Re-derive the EMIT; reuse the ANALYSIS.** The detectors are *pure* ‚Äî they nail the simple/base shapes. The reducer's job is to reduce hard shapes DOWN to those base cases by composition, representing nesting with TOKENS (abstract nodes): by the time an outer rule looks, the inner structure is already one token, so every rule sees a clean base case. That IS the closure property from the emit side. So reuse dominators/loops/diamonds/switch detection; build a new region-tree + (addr,indent,text) pretty-printer.
>   4. **Value-diamond / boolean-region PRE-CONTRACTION carries through.** `bytecode_cfg` already contracts these (they're expression-layer, not region-layer); the simple translations the existing code does well survive into V2's CFG unchanged ‚Äî confirm the $E76F interaction at rung 3 (it may make rung 3 *smaller* than planned).
>   - **Canonical new-win exemplar (rung 3):** `$E76F draw_daimyo_portrait` = `if (idx < 53 && daimyo_record[idx+6]) { composite } else { preset } <tail>` ‚Äî short-circuit feeding if/else feeding a seq-tail; templates emit 4 gotos (no composition), V2's grammar nests it.
>
> **‚úÖ ACCEPTED RESIDUE (closed ‚Äî do NOT reopen as work):** the 7 Phase-3 nested-in-`if`/`while` switches; `$9A0F` fully-rotated loop; every other honest-goto fallback. These were DECISIONS, not TODOs ‚Äî under V2 they re-derive automatically as the irreducible set.
>
> **RULE going forward (the anti-sprawl guard):** a discovery may land in ACCEPTED (honest goto) or the Inbox (a future epic) ‚Äî it may **NOT** add a new OPEN sub-step to this epic. A new open frame is a deliberate decision, never session momentum. Every "DONE" ends with a *return* verdict, not a `‚ñ∂ Next`.
>
> ---
> **‚§µ SUPERSEDED DETAIL ‚Äî the template-phase history (kept for the record + the fallback structurer; NOT the live frontier; do NOT extend):**
### EPIC (superseded): goto ‚Üí while / if-else / switch via templates (Chris, 2026-06-03, PROMOTED from "not chased")
> **Why now:** after the teardown (A=table-driven dispatch, C=arg/arity), the *expression* layer of the decompiled C reads like real C ‚Äî the last "assembler smell" is the **1,437 `goto`s + 1,511 `L_XXXX:` labels** (~2,950 lines of scaffolding across 277 of 495 subs; 218 are already goto-free). Folding these into structured `while`/`if-else`/`switch` is the single biggest remaining readability gain. Surfaced concretely by the `vm_bootstrap` two-loop walk (the per-game `init` vs per-turn loop distinction is invisible until the back-edges render as nested `while`).
> **Goto census (measured 2026-06-03, cross-checks the long-standing ~1437 figure):** 451 **backward** (loops) + 986 **forward** (if/break/early-return); 842 conditional `if(..)goto` + 595 bare.
>
> **THE GATE (the crux ‚Äî this epic CANNOT use the byte-identical regen-guard, because structuring deliberately changes the C).** Replacement gate = **CFG-equivalence**: extract the basic-block successor graph from the bytecode (vm-disasm already computes reachability/successors), apply only structuring transforms that **provably lower back to the same CFG**, and **FALL BACK to `goto` on anything unproven** (irreducible regions, overlapping/multi-entry loops). Fidelity then rises monotonically and is *never wrong*. Realistic ceiling is **<100%** ‚Äî even Ghidra/Hex-Rays emit gotos for irreducible control flow; a few honest gotos remaining is CORRECT, not a failure (forcing structure there would lie about the flow). Target ~70‚Äì90% folded.
> **Not greenfield:** extends the existing `structure_lines` post-pass (already folds `if(!(C))goto;‚Ä¶L:` ‚Üí `if(C){}` Pattern A + if/else Pattern B). New patterns plug into the same machinery.
>
> **DECISION ‚Äî the artifact is READABLE C, reversibility is a producible WITNESS (Chris, 2026-06-03).** This epic crosses the project's dedeterminism/reversibility line, but precisely: it is NOT non-deterministic (transforms stay pure algorithms in the tool ‚Äî the moment an *agent* eyeballs structure into a hard case, refuse it) and it does NOT touch the M1 byte-identical round-trip (that lives BELOW the C rendering, at bytecode‚Üîstructured-operand ‚Äî `vm_assemble.py` is indifferent to goto-vs-while). What's traded is **text-level losslessness (C line ‚Üî instruction) ‚Üí behavior-level CFG-equivalence.** Chris's call: **structured C (good `if`/`while`/`switch` + brackets) is the ON-BY-DEFAULT canonical file you read**; the raw goto form stays REPRODUCIBLE on demand via `--raw` as the round-trip witness (so the reversible-deterministic artifact is never *lost*, just not the primary surface). Honest inline `goto` stays where the bytecode is genuinely irreducible (correct, not failure ‚Äî Ghidra/Hex-Rays do the same; forcing structure there would lie about the flow). This is the same default-off-switch pattern as `decompile-all.py --self-check` / `all_banks.c`-is-derived, inverted: here the RICHER view is the default and the strict witness is the flag. [[feedback_derived_artifact_is_also_a_deliverable]]
>
> - üü¢ **Phase 0 ‚Äî CFG extractor + raw-witness gate + `--raw` plumbing ‚Äî LANDED 2026-06-03 (hard half done; structured-equivalence RELATION is the open decision before Phase 1).**
>   - **`--raw` plumbing DONE.** `vm_decompile.STRUCTURE` toggle (default True, mirrors the `SELF_CHECK` pattern ‚Üí canonical `decompiled/*.c` BYTE-IDENTICAL, verified); `decompile-all.py --raw` flips it off ‚Üí pure goto witness in `decompiled/raw/` (never clobbers canonical, merged view skipped). A `collect=` hook on `decompile()` + `on_sub=` on `bank_subs()` hand the gate each sub's raw+structured line lists + instructions with no risky refactor. All existing gates stay green (round-trip 495/45024, drift-guard 179 gated, full-regen byte-identical).
>   - **CFG extractor + raw lowering DONE & PROVEN (`tools/vm_cfg.py`).** `bytecode_cfg(instructions)` = ground-truth basic-block graph; `lower_goto_cfg(raw, leaders)` lowers the witness to the same graph. **Key key-space insight that makes the gate clean: the decompiler's `L_XXXX` labels ARE bytecode target addresses, so C control flow and bytecode share one coordinate system ‚Äî no name-matching.** Two real bugs found+fixed by going to ground truth (the witness MUST be exact): fall-through has to target the next leader BY ADDRESS, not the next emitted line ‚Äî else (a) the decompiler's out-of-order **flushed-call lines** (a discarded side-effecting CALL is emitted at its flush point but tagged with its earlier addr) and (b) **folded statement-less blocks** (a branch target whose every instr folds into an expression) both mis-route. Per-block address-based lowering is robust to both.
>   - **HARD GATE GREEN (`tools/vm-cfg-gate.py`): `lower_goto_cfg(raw) == bytecode_cfg` 495/495.** Proves `--raw` is a CFG-faithful round-trip witness (the reversibility guarantee, mechanically verified) + the extractor is correct across the whole codebase + no unrecognised control mnemonics.
>   - **‚öÝÔ∏è THE OPEN DECISION (Chris) ‚Äî the STRUCTURED equivalence RELATION, lock before Phase 1.** Naive `lower(structured) == bytecode_cfg` is the WRONG gate: `structure_lines` already does **destructive folds** that change the block partition while preserving behaviour ‚Äî **early-return** (`if(!C) return X;` merges the separate return-block into the branch block) and **empty-arm if/else** (`if(C){}else{}` collapses a 2-block diamond, stripping the gotos that defined the arms). 263/495 match the strict gate today; the 232 that differ are a MIX of (a) these legit destructive folds and (b) the provisional tree lowering `lower_c_to_cfg` still carrying the same next-leader fall-through bug that `lower_goto_cfg` already fixed (so 232 is an upper bound on "real divergence," not a true count ‚Äî don't read it as 232 bad folds). So Phase 1's gate needs both: fix the structured lowering's fall-through (port the per-block address rule), AND a relation that ACCEPTS valid block-merges but still catches a real misroute. Candidate (designed, not yet built): **contract pure-routing blocks** (goto-only / empty / single-`return V`) on BOTH sides, carrying the **return VALUE on the EXIT edge** (so a wrong/spurious return is caught), PLUS **true/false edge labels** (so a condition inversion in an if/else ‚Äî same nodes, swapped guards ‚Äî is caught; a plain unlabelled CFG would miss it). The provisional tree lowering `lower_c_to_cfg` is the starting point but needs the same next-leader fall-through fix. **Phase 1 opens by locking this relation, then building it + negative-testing it (inject a misroute ‚Üí must fail).**
>   - üü¢ **STEP 1 DONE 2026-06-03 ‚Äî relation BUILT + it immediately earned its keep (found a real bug).** `vm_cfg.lower_struct_cfg` (correct structured lowering: brace-matched header `(true,false)` edges, address-based merges via the highest LEADER in the span so empty/folded arms resolve, then-tail‚Üímerge redirect for if-else) + `observable_blocks` + `contract` (bypass pure-routing / bare-`return` blocks) + `structured_equivalent` = `contract(lower_struct) == contract(lower_goto(raw))`. Three real lowering bugs found+fixed en route (then-tail-falls-into-else; merge missed empty-arm leaders; empty-else merge). **Result: hard raw gate 495/495; structured-equivalence 460/495.** **THE 35 RESIDUE IS THE PAYOFF, NOT NOISE:** they're subs where the CURRENT, UNGATED `structure_lines` applied a fold that ISN'T CFG-preserving ‚Äî including a **CONFIRMED CORRECTNESS BUG**: `num_to_ascii` ($CF98, bank 15) structured C nests `L_CFBC:` (the `arg2<arg3` recursive branch) INSIDE the `if(arg2>=arg3){}` braces, so that path falls off the function and returns garbage instead of recursing (raw/bytecode branch to $CFBC; structured goes to EXIT). Others (`$8F14` etc.) are genuinely irreducible (a `goto` jumps INTO the middle of a structured if-body = multi-entry) ‚Äî the EPIC's "leave an honest goto" cases. **So the gate, the moment it existed, proved the pre-EPIC Patterns A/B sometimes emit CFG-WRONG C that's been sitting in `decompiled/*.c`.** Gate is report-mode for the structured check (exit 1 only on the raw witness); the 35 are the Phase-1 work-list.
>   - ~~**‚ñ∂ PHASE 1 REFRAME**~~ **DONE 2026-06-03 ‚Äî the 35 are FIXED, gating is wired in.** `vm_decompile.decompile()` now GATES the structuring: after `structure_lines`, it checks `vm_cfg.structured_equivalent(raw, structured, leaders)` and, if the fold is NOT CFG-preserving, reverts that sub to the honest goto form (`collect` exposes `structured_ungated` + `gated_fallback` for the gate tool). **Result: the `num_to_ascii` correctness bug is FIXED** (recursive branch reads correctly again) and all 35 non-CFG-preserving subs revert to goto (`decompiled/*.c` regenerated, net ‚àí190 lines; round-trip 495/45024 + drift-guard still CLEAN ‚Äî they're on bytecode, untouched). The gate's structured check is now a **HARD gate**: `vm-cfg-gate.py` = 495/495 witness + **495/495 gated-structuring-is-CFG-preserving** + reports the 35 goto fallbacks. **Non-vacuousness PROVEN** ‚Äî `tools/test-vm-cfg.py` injects a misroute into real subs and asserts the relation REJECTS it (9/9 pass). This is the EPIC's safety mechanism fully operational: **fidelity now rises ONLY where it's provably correct.** ‚ñ∂ Next: the actual Phase-1 fold (backward goto ‚Üí `while`/`do-while`), each fold safe-by-construction via this gate. ~~**KNOWN GAP (note for the if-else folder, Phase 2):** the contraction relation catches MISROUTES but not a pure then/else SWAP (same two targets, inverted guard) ‚Äî add true/false EDGE LABELS before Phase 2 leans on it.~~ **CLOSED 2026-06-03 ‚Äî see Phase 2 step 0 below.**
>   - üü¢ **PHASE 1a ‚Äî top-test `while` folds ‚Äî DONE 2026-06-03. 42 loops folded, 84 gotos removed, every gate green, ZERO net new fallbacks.** New CFG substrate in `vm_cfg.py` (`dominators` / `back_edges` / `natural_loop` ‚Äî standard iterative dataflow over the block CFG). New `vm_decompile.structure_loops(lines, instructions)` runs BEFORE `structure_lines` (loops outermost, then if/else folds inside the bodies) and folds a **single-back-edge, single-exit, reducible top-test (`whileTop`) loop** into `while (C) { body }`. CFG-DRIVEN ‚Äî header/body/exit come from the bytecode CFG, never line-text guessing. **The hard case it solves = the ROTATED idiom** (the common compiler shape: test emitted at the BOTTOM, body above, with an entry `goto L_test` guard ‚Äî header address > body address in ~all 60 survey candidates). The fold hoists the test to the top (√Ý la Ghidra/Hex-Rays); to keep `lower_struct_cfg`'s address-based fall-through correct after the hoist, the structured lowering now models a while **position-based** (body-entry/tail/exit = first/last block-occupying line in the braces, NOT `next_leader`) + a **body-leaders entry redirect** (a block before the loop whose address-next leader lands INSIDE the hoisted body enters via the header instead ‚Äî the analogue of the dropped guard goto). **Two real lowering bugs found+fixed en route:** (1) the empty-entry-block case (`$A742`: the guard was the entry block's ONLY statement ‚Üí dropping it left an empty block that fell through to the body by address) ‚Äî fixed by the body-leaders redirect; (2) `_opens_block` ‚Äî a construct OPENER (`if (C) {` / `while (C) {`) ends in `{` so `_is_scaffold` called it scaffold, but it STARTS a block, so a body beginning with an `if` got the wrong body-entry + a broken redirect (the `for`-style loop `$9E9D`, increment in the header block, was the witness). Fixing it took fallbacks 64 ‚Üí **35 = the exact pre-loop if/else baseline** (loops add zero new fallbacks; the 5 still-rejected loop-attempts are all subs whose if/else part was already failing). **The decompiled diff is provably a pure structural transform** ‚Äî `git diff -w` shows ONLY `+while` / `+}` / `-goto` / `-L_label` + indentation, ZERO expression/content change. Gates: CFG-gate 495/495 witness + **495/495 gated-structuring-CFG-preserving**, round-trip 495/45024 CLEAN, drift-guard CLEAN, `--check` 0 BAD √ó4. **Non-vacuousness for loops PROVEN** ‚Äî `test-vm-cfg.py` (18/18) asserts a folded `while`‚Üí`if` (back edge dropped) is REJECTED by the relation. Reads as source now: `avg_daimyo_charisma_over_fief_list` is a clean `while (*p != 255) { ‚Ä¶ }`; `build_event_eligible_fief_candidate_list` a `while`-with-nested-`if`. **Cosmetic debt (inherited from `structure_lines`, NOT introduced ‚Äî confirmed in the pre-existing committed output): if-bodies aren't extra-indented + occasional dangling merge labels / stray braces; a structure_lines indentation pass would fix it for loops AND ifs at once.**
>   - üü¢ **PHASE 1b ‚Äî bottom-test `do { } while` folds ‚Äî DONE 2026-06-03. +10 loops (52 total: 42 while + 10 do-while), every gate green, ZERO net new fallbacks.** `structure_loops` is now a dispatcher: `_fold_while` (1a) + `_fold_dowhile`. The do-while path covers **self-loops (`u==h`) AND multi-block bottom-test loops (`h<u`)** ‚Äî the tail block ends in `if (C) goto L_h` (taken = continue). **NO hoist** (the test stays at the bottom, address order preserved), so the only edits are `L_h:` ‚Üí `do {` and the tail test ‚Üí `} while (C);` ‚Äî strictly simpler than the while case. **Modeled the do-while back edge** that was the stated prerequisite: `_match_constructs` now records `dowhiles` (do_addr + the `} while` test addr) and `lower_struct_cfg` adds `dowhile_edges[tail_block] = {header, exit}` (today's gate would have rejected any emitted do-while without it). **Two real bugs found+fixed:** (1) **`natural_loop` self-loop bug** ‚Äî for `u==h` the backward worklist processed the header's OWN predecessors, so `map_render_driver`'s loop wrongly swallowed the pre-loop `local9 = 0` initializer; fixed to the textbook form (seed worklist from `u` only when `u != h`; a self-loop is just `{h}`). (2) **`_span_max_leader` opener blindness** (sibling of 1a's `_opens_block`) ‚Äî an `if` body containing ONLY a `do {} while` (empty self-loop body) looked empty, so the if's MERGE fell back to `next_leader(header)` instead of past the loop; the busy-wait `if (gate==1){ do{}while(syscall) }` (`$8B8F`) was the witness. Fixed by counting openers in `_span_max_leader` too. After both, fallbacks return to **35 = baseline** (the 1 still-rejected do-while attempt, `$AF3B`, was already failing on its if/else). **Diff still a pure structural transform** (`git diff -w`: only `+do {` / `} while` / `-goto` / `-L_label` + indentation). Gates: CFG-gate 495/495 + 495/495, round-trip 495/45024 CLEAN, drift-guard CLEAN, `--check` 0 BAD √ó4, `test-vm-cfg.py` **27/27** (adds do-while non-vacuousness: dropping the `} while` tail is REJECTED). Reads as source: `map_render_driver` = `do { ‚Ä¶ } while (i < 5)`; `command_menu_select_loop` = `do { poll_input(); ‚Ä¶ } while (!done)`.
>   - ~~**PHASE 1c ‚Äî two-test + multi-back-edge loops**~~ DONE in Phase 2 steps 1-3 (`both` loops + single-header multi-back-edge menu loops). The residue was the **68 multi-HEADER subs** (nested/sibling loops `structure_loops` skipped via its one-loop-per-sub guard).
>   - üü¢ **MULTI-HEADER ‚Äî SIBLING loops DONE 2026-06-04 (+20 subs, 89‚Üí109 loop-folding subs).** `structure_loops` no longer bails on `len(headers) != 1`: refactored into `_fold_one_loop` (the per-loop shape dispatch, factored out of the lone-loop path) + `_fold_siblings`. **Sibling = >1 loop header whose natural loops are pairwise DISJOINT (sequential, not nested).** `_fold_siblings` folds each independently, **highest header address first** (so a fold's inserted scaffold never shifts a not-yet-folded sibling's line indices), and **gates each sibling against the raw witness on its own** so one bad sibling fold can't sink the others (the sub keeps every good one). NESTED / overlapping headers ‚Üí still deferred (bail to goto). **20 of the 27 pure-sibling subs now fold ‚â•1 loop** (the other 7: a sibling shape that doesn't fold cleanly or was per-sibling gate-rejected). Reads as source: `write_sram_save_checksum_and_signature` ($A3AA) = two sequential `do { local10 += syscall_sram_block_with_checksum(‚Ä¶); local11 += 0x100; } while (local11 < 0x7000/0x7F00);`. Gates green: cfg-gate 495/495 + 495/495 (**34 fallbacks UNCHANGED ‚Äî zero regression**), round-trip 495/45024 CLEAN, --check 0 BAD √ó4, drift CLEAN, decompiled diff a pure structural transform (`git diff -w`: only loop/brace/goto tokens). **Non-vacuousness PROVEN** ‚Äî `test-vm-cfg.py` 106‚Üí**114**: $A3AA + $A455 fold ‚â•2 sibling loops, and dropping JUST ONE loop's back edge is REJECTED (the other fold doesn't mask it ‚Äî the per-sibling independence the gating rests on). ‚ñ∂ Remaining multi-header bucket = **NESTED loops** (a header inside another's body ‚Äî fold inner-then-outer): 26 nested-only + 15 mixed = ~41 subs. That's the real epic-sized piece (the gate's `loop_ctx` is already inner-wins-ready; the emit-side multi-loop orchestration is the new work).
> - üü¢ **Phase 2 ‚Äî forward gotos ‚Üí early-`return` / `break` / `if-else` chains** (the 986). Extends Patterns A/B with break-out-of-loop, fall-through if/else-if, and early-return folding.
>   - ‚úÖ **STEP 0 ‚Äî true/false EDGE LABELS (the gate prerequisite) ‚Äî DONE 2026-06-03 (commit `6c55607`).** The contraction relation now catches a pure then/else SWAP / guard inversion (same two targets, inverted guard) that the unlabelled successor SET missed. `vm_cfg.py`: per 2-way conditional block record an oriented `(taken, fall)` (`_record_orient`); `_canon_cond` folds negation out of the guard ‚Äî outer `!(...)` AND comparison-op flips (`<`‚Üî`>=`,`>`‚Üî`<=`,`==`‚Üî`!=`, mirroring `invert_condition`) ‚Äî so semantically equal guards compare equal. The labels are rewired **in lockstep with `contract()`** (conditionals have 2 successors so contract never removes them ‚Üí labels resolve to exactly the contracted graph's nodes; a standalone resolver first-cut diverged on loop tails / mid-contraction self-loops and false-rejected 28 legit folds ‚Üí the lockstep approach is exact). `structured_equivalent` ANDs the orientation-map equality onto the contracted-CFG equality. **Non-vacuousness PROVEN** ‚Äî `test-vm-cfg.py` 27‚Üí**33**: inverting an if-header guard without moving bodies is REJECTED on 3 subs (and an empty-arm `if(){}else{}` correctly stays accepted ‚Äî a genuine no-op under inversion). All gates green, ZERO behavior change: cfg-gate **495/495 witness + 495/495 gated (35 fallbacks, unchanged)**, `decompiled/*.c` **byte-identical**, round-trip 495/45024 CLEAN, drift-guard CLEAN, `--check` 0 BAD √ó4. ‚ñ∂ Next: the actual forward-goto folds (each now safe-by-construction against this strengthened relation), folding in the deferred Phase-1c loop cases as the `break`/`continue` machinery lands.
>   - üü¢ **STEP 1 ‚Äî `break`/`continue` SUBSTRATE + the trivial breaks ‚Äî DONE 2026-06-03.** Built the gate's loop-context machinery so `break;`/`continue;` are first-class (the prerequisite for ALL of Phase-1c + 2). `vm_cfg.py`: `_classify_stmt` recognizes `break;`/`continue;`/`if(C) break;`/`if(C) continue;` (target is the enclosing loop's exit/header, resolved by CONTEXT not the statement); `observable_blocks` treats them as control (so a break-only block contracts like a router, not a side-effect); `lower_struct_cfg` builds a `loop_ctx` map (each body leader ‚Üí its INNERMOST enclosing loop's `(header, exit)`, largest-span-first so inner wins) via the promoted `_occupies_block` + new `_loop_body_leaders`, then lowers `break`‚Üíloop exit / `continue`‚Üíloop header (with true/false orientation for the conditional forms). The RAW witness `lower_goto_cfg` is UNTOUCHED ‚Äî it stays pure goto, so break/continue only ever appears in the structured form being checked AGAINST it. `vm_decompile.py`: new `_emit_break_continue` post-pass inside `_fold_while`/`_fold_dowhile` rewrites an in-loop `goto L_exit`‚Üí`break;` (and `goto L_header`‚Üí`continue;`), block-scoped to the loop and exit/header-exact (every sibling-label goto stays a goto). **Result: 2 trivial breaks converted** (`revolt_spread_sweep_flip_fief_ownership` $9778, `process_first_n_unmarked_list_entries` $9974 ‚Äî both `if(C) goto L_exit`‚Üí`if(C) break;`); the 3rd probe-flagged candidate ($9810) is correctly a **two-test loop** `structure_loops` doesn't fold yet (‚Üí deferred step 3). **The substrate is the real deliverable** ‚Äî `continue` + multi-loop nesting are wired and gate-tested but light up in steps 2-3. **Non-vacuousness PROVEN** ‚Äî `test-vm-cfg.py` 33‚Üí**39**: a `break`‚Üí`continue` swap (exit‚Üíheader, a real infinite-loop bug) is REJECTED on both subs. All gates green: cfg-gate **495/495 witness + 495/495 gated (35 fallbacks, UNCHANGED ‚Äî zero new)**, `decompiled/*.c` diff is a **pure `goto`‚Üí`break` structural transform** (2 lines, `git diff -w` clean of content), round-trip 495/45024 CLEAN, drift-guard CLEAN, `--check` 0 BAD √ó4. ‚ñ∂ Next: **step 2** = multi-back-edge loops ‚Üí `continue` (the 77); **step 3** = two-test loops ‚Üí `break` (the 16).
>   - üü¢ **STEP 2 ‚Äî multi-back-edge MENU LOOPS (machinery + 2 subs) ‚Äî DONE 2026-06-04. ‚öÝÔ∏è KEY FINDING: "the 77" was a category error.** Probing the 77 multi-back-edge subs split them: **only 9 are single-header** (the actual `continue` targets); the other **68 are multi-HEADER = nested/sibling loops** (a separate epic ‚Äî `structure_loops` does one loop per sub; needs inner-then-outer folding). And the 9 are NOT the rotated `while(C)`-with-mid-continues the ticket assumed ‚Äî they're **`while(1)`-style input/menu loops** (`if(flag) return; switch(poll_input()){ case‚Ä¶: ‚Ä¶; goto L_top=continue; ‚Ä¶ }`), 8 with a 2-way return-guard header + 1 switch-header (`$AC33`). **Landed the core machinery + the 2 cleanest** (`combat_command_menu_input_loop` $8669, `select_entry_from_b52f_table_by_cursor` $86F9 ‚Äî both now read as `while (!(local11)) { switch (poll_input()) {‚Ä¶}; ‚Ä¶continue‚Ä¶ } return local10;`, previously goto-soup). Three tooling pieces, each gate-driven: (1) **`structure_loops`** relaxed ‚Äî a single header with ‚â•2 back edges + 2-way header ‚Üí `_fold_while(multi=True)`, computing the loop as the UNION of natural loops; every in-body `goto L_h` left for `_emit_break_continue`‚Üí`continue`. (2) **`_fold_while` exit-relocation** ‚Äî the top-test idiom emits the header's fall-through `return` *between* test and body, breaking listing-contiguity; `_is_pure_exit_block` detects those interleaved exit blocks and **relocates them past the `}`** (the gate lowers by ADDRESS not line-position, so the move is CFG-neutral ‚Äî the proven insight that made this tractable without a bespoke `while(1)` model). (3) **gate fix in `vm_cfg.lower_struct_cfg`** ‚Äî the auto `body_tail‚Üíheader` back-edge was SPURIOUS when the tail ends in an unconditional terminator (a menu tail `goto L_x` targets a continue block, not the head); new `tail_falls_off` adds it only when the body can fall off the bottom `}`. Plus a **two-tier fallback in `decompile()`**: if the loop-fold breaks the gate, retry with if/else structuring ALONE before reverting ‚Äî so a sub never loses its valid if/else folds over a bad loop attempt (this is what kept fallbacks at exactly 35, ZERO regression). **Non-vacuousness** ‚Äî `test-vm-cfg.py` 39‚Üí**45**: a `continue`‚Üí`break` swap (header‚Üíexit) is REJECTED on both. Gates: cfg-gate **495/495 + 495/495 (35 fallbacks, UNCHANGED)**, round-trip 495/45024 CLEAN, drift-guard CLEAN, `--check` 0 BAD √ó4; decompiled diff is a pure structural transform (the only `-w` content delta = the header guard `if(local11)return` absorbed into the `while(!local11)` condition ‚Äî gate-proven equivalent). **‚ñ∂ The remaining 7 of 9 are THREE distinct sub-problems (each its own focused session ‚Äî the full step 2 is NOT one session):** (a) **empty-else-merge-under-loop** ($B1BE,$9A0F ‚Äî single-exit, but `lower_struct_cfg`'s empty-`else` merge resolves to the loop header instead of the post-if block under the hoist; a deep lowering interaction); (b) **multi-exit** ($90B6,$81EE,$9188 ‚Äî ‚â•2 distinct exit targets, need break-target selection: one becomes the `}` fall, others stay gotos); (c) **switch-header `while(1)`** ($AC33) + **header-not-first** ($951D, interleaved init). The 68 nested/sibling subs are a 4th, larger bucket (Phase 1c/2 nested-loop epic).
>     - üü¢ **STEP 2 / sub-problem (c) + a GATE-SOUNDNESS FIX ‚Äî DONE 2026-06-04. The real prize was finding a GATE HOLE.** Added a `while (1)` infinite-loop fold (`_fold_while1`) for switch-header / no-clean-test menu loops: wraps the loop span in `while (1) {}`, the header switch + label stay inside as the loop top, body `goto L_h`‚Üí`continue` / `goto L_exit`‚Üí`break` (switch CASE gotos keep their labels for Phase 3). Dispatched as a fallback when no 2-way `while`/`do-while` applies. **$AC33 folds** (a clean `while(1){ switch(poll_input()){‚Ä¶} }` combat menu). **But wiring it in surfaced a latent GATE HOLE that had silently accepted 15 WRONG folds:** a loop with a CONDITIONAL back edge `if(C) goto L_h` is a *do-while* (C false = EXIT), but `_fold_while1` rendered it `while(1){ ‚Ä¶; if(C) continue; }` ‚Äî making the do-while's exit wrongly LOOP. The gate ACCEPTED it because it modelled a body-tail's fall-through as `next_leader` (the post-loop block), which for a rotated `while(C)` happens to equal the header by address (so it was invisible) but for `while(1)` (tail at the end, header at the top) fabricated a spurious exit edge that matched the bytecode. **Root fix (`vm_cfg.lower_struct_cfg`): a loop body-TAIL's fall goes to the HEADER, not `next_leader`** (`tail_fall_to_header` + `fall_of()`, applied to every fall position ‚Äî ifgoto/ifcontinue/ifbreak/ifreturn/switch-no-default/plain). Proven sound: with the source guard *disabled*, the gate now REJECTS the bad `$830B` fold on its own (reverts to honest goto). **Two-way win:** the corrected model also UNLOCKED 2 valid `while(C)` folds in bank_15 (a strcmp-like `while(*arg1==*arg2)`) the *old buggy model had been false-negative rejecting. Belt-and-suspenders **source guard** in `_fold_while1` too (bail on any 2-way conditional back edge ‚Äî that's do-while territory, not infinite). **Result: 8/9 fold** ($AC33 added); $B6D6/$8C88 correctly DON'T (they have conditional back edges ‚Üí do-while-with-switch, a deferred shape); $9A0F still the lone messy residue. Loop totals now **81 folded** (70 while + 10 do-while + 1 while1). Gates: cfg-gate 495/495 + 495/495 (35 fallbacks UNCHANGED), round-trip 495/45024 CLEAN, drift CLEAN, `--check` 0 BAD √ó4, **test-vm-cfg 54‚Üí56** (the new test BUILDS the bad while(1) and asserts the gate REJECTS it ‚Äî the hole-closure proof). ‚ñ∂ Remaining of the original 9: just $9A0F (messy body) + the $B6D6/$8C88 do-while-with-switch shape (own follow-on). The 68 nested/sibling subs remain the big 4th bucket.
>     - üü¢ **STEP 2 / sub-problem (b) ‚Äî DONE 2026-06-04. "Multi-exit" was mostly mid-body RETURNS, not real second exits ‚Üí 7/9 now fold** (also swept in $951D from (c)). The extra exits in all three (b)-subs are **pure-exit blocks** (a mid-body `return`, or a `break` routing to the single structural exit) ‚Äî not live-code second exits. Two fixes: (1) **`_loop_single_exit_entry` ‚Üí `_loop_single_entry`** ‚Äî dropped the single-exit constraint; a non-loop successor is now OK if it's `exit_e` OR a `_is_pure_exit_block` (keeps the single-ENTRY/reducibility check). (2) **relocation split in `_fold_while`** ‚Äî interleaved pure-exit blocks BEFORE the body entry (the top-test header's fall-through `return`) are relocated past the `}` as before, but mid-body ones (‚â• body-entry index) now **STAY in place** so they read as honest early-`return`s (e.g. `paged_flee_fief_list_display` $912B keeps `if (hit==2) return 0;` mid-loop; `collect_high_loyalty_provinces_to_candidate_list` $8FF8 keeps two `return append_candidate(...)` early-exits) ‚Äî address-keyed lowering makes either placement CFG-neutral, so this is purely readability. **FOLDED 7/9** ($90B6,$951D,$81EE,$B1BE,$867D,$870E,$9188); gate 35 fallbacks UNCHANGED, round-trip/drift/`--check` green, test-vm-cfg 48‚Üí**54** (multi-exit witnesses: a mid-loop `return` deletion is REJECTED). >     - üü¢ **STEP 2 / sub-problem (a) ‚Äî DONE 2026-06-04. Root cause was NOT a merge bug ‚Äî it was a LINE-LESS interior loop block.** `$B1BE` (`submenu_prompt`) folds now. Its empty-`else` then-body has a folded tail block (`$b20a`) that emits NO C line (all instructions absorbed into an expression). `_loop_body_leaders` collected body leaders only from emitted LINES, so `$b20a` was missing from the while's body-leader set `bls` ‚Üí the rotated-while body-redirect (the "block outside the loop whose fall lands inside ‚Üí enter via header" rule) misread `$b20a` as OUTSIDE and routed it through the header `$b1be`, fabricating exactly the spurious edge the gate caught. **Fix:** `_loop_body_leaders` now fills in line-LESS interior blocks (any leader in the body's address span `min(bls) < L < max(bls)`); `leaders` threaded to both call sites. **3/9 fold now** ($867D, $870E, $B1BE); gate 35 fallbacks UNCHANGED (zero regression), round-trip/drift/`--check`/test-vm-cfg (45‚Üí**48**, $B1A6 added) all green; the only `-w` content delta is the header guard absorbed into the `while` condition (gate-proven equivalent). **`$9A0F` is NOT this bug** ‚Äî it's a genuinely harder shape (body_entry mismatch `raw 99f9 ‚âÝ struct 99ef`; a `continue` lands mid-body with code after it), correctly rejected ‚Üí stays honest goto; reclassified out of (a) into the "messy body" residue. >     - üü¢ **STEP 2 / the DO-WHILE-WITH-SWITCH residue pair ($8C88, $B6D6) ‚Äî DONE 2026-06-04 (commits `19701a7`, `4104bc6`).** The two shapes the step-2 finish-line flagged as a deferred follow-on, now folded ‚Äî and they turned out to be TWO distinct sub-shapes, each its own one-line-of-machinery fix gated by CFG-equivalence: **(1) interleaved-pure-exit do-while ($8C88 `draw_unit_roster_columns`):** a clean bottom-test do-while whose listing span contains an *unrelated* exit-path block (`$8CCB`, reached only from the post-loop exit path). `_fold_dowhile` previously hard-bailed on ANY interleaved non-loop block; now it ALLOWS interleaved PURE-EXIT blocks but ‚Äî UNLIKE `_fold_while` ‚Äî does NOT relocate them. **KEY LESSON (cost me a wrong first attempt): the lowering's merge/fall computations are ADDRESS-based (lexical order assumed to track address order), so relocating a block to an address-inconsistent lexical slot is UNSOUND** ‚Äî a relocate-to-end attempt made `structure_lines`' `if(arg1){}` merge resolve to `EXIT` instead of the moved block (the gate caught it). Left in place, the block renders inside the do-body reached by an honest *backward* goto (which `structure_lines` won't mis-fold ‚Äî Patterns A/B are forward-only); CFG stays exact. **(2) while(1)-with-conditional-exit ($B6D6 `command_menu_select_loop`, +$AB29 `render_arms_edit_screen` bonus):** the test-in-the-MIDDLE menu loop ‚Äî a switch-header loop whose conditional back edge `if(C) goto L_h` sits mid-listing with case bodies laid out AFTER it (do-while can't express it; the test isn't the last loop line). Relaxed `_fold_while1`'s belt-and-suspenders conditional-back-edge bail to ATTEMPT the fold when the back edge's NON-continue branch is a PURE-EXIT `return`/`break` ‚Äî so `if(C) continue; return ‚Ä¶;` exits correctly (NOT the do-while-loops-wrongly GATE HOLE that step-2(c) closed). Safe by TWO independent mechanisms: dispatch (a plain bottom-test do-while is intercepted by `_fold_dowhile` first ‚Äî $830B proves this, never reaches `_fold_while1`) AND the gate (already proven sound vs the bad while(1) by the $830B test). **$AC11/$AC33 needed NO work ‚Äî already a `while(1)` from step 2(c)** (the residual `goto L_AC33` is a switch CASE default = Phase-3 territory, which over-flagged my triage). Gates per commit: cfg-gate 495/495 + 495/495 (**35 fallbacks UNCHANGED**), round-trip 495/45024 CLEAN, drift-guard CLEAN, `--check` 0 BAD √ó4, decompiled diff a pure structural transform (`git diff -w`: only do/while(1)/continue/-goto/-L_label). **test-vm-cfg 56‚Üí65**: $8C61 in the do-while suite (its `fold ~= raw` is the regression guard for interleaved-pure-exit ‚Äî it FAILED pre-fix) + $B6B4/$AB22 each get folded-while(1)+if-continue / fold~=raw / **if-continue‚Üíbreak REJECTED** (proves the continue TARGET is checked, the soundness the relaxation rests on).
>     - üü¢ **STEP 3 = the genuine two-test (`both`) loops ‚Äî DONE 2026-06-04. 5 of the 6 named subs fold + 9 bonus do-whiles (14 new do-whiles total), every gate green, ZERO new fallbacks.** The insight that collapsed the whole class: a two-test `both` loop is **just a do-while whose HEADER also carries an exit-test** ‚Äî so route it to `_fold_dowhile` and let the existing `_emit_break_continue` post-pass rewrite the header's in-loop `goto L_exit` ‚Üí `if (C) break;`. NO bespoke `_fold_while`-with-conditional-tail needed. Three small, each gate-driven, fixes: **(1) dispatch** ‚Äî new `elif utest and htest and u != h` branch in `structure_loops` routes the `both` shape to `_fold_dowhile` (which self-validates + the CFG gate is the backstop). **(2) flushed-call HOIST in `_fold_dowhile`** ‚Äî the button-wait archetype (`prompt_yes_no $822A`, `ui_helper_d3a7 $D3A7`, `ui_helper_d351 $D351`) emits a discarded-return CALL (`read_frame_timer(1)`) AFTER the `L_h:` label but tagged with its earlier, PRE-HEADER address; its block is the pre-loop entry, so leaving it in the do-body splits the entry block across the loop boundary ‚Üí gate (correctly) rejected. Fix: hoist any in-span line with `addr < h` + non-leader (= a flushed side-effect, control lines keep their position) OUT to before `do {` ‚Äî the SAFE relocation direction (to an address-CONSISTENT slot below h, the opposite of the $8C88 move-to-end that was unsound). **(3) `vm_cfg.lower_struct_cfg` loop_ctx ROOT FIX** ‚Äî the do-while path `discard`ed the header block `hb` from the loop context, so a `break` INSIDE the header block (the defining feature of a two-test loop, never seen before) couldn't resolve to the exit ‚Üí the header lost its exit edge (gate divergence `struct $823B‚Üí{$8245}` vs `raw‚Üí{$8245,$824D}`). Now KEEP `hb` in loop_ctx; harmless for plain do-whiles (no header break) + self-loops (special-cased via dowhile_edges first). **Result: $822A/$8FEC/$D351/$D3A7/$E554 fold** (the 6th, `$AF3B`, correctly stays an if/else `gated_fallback`); $D351 proves MULTIPLE header breaks resolve (`if(==64) break; if(==128) break;`). Reads as source: `prompt_yes_no` = `read_frame_timer(1); do { local11 = wait_button_edge(); if (‚Ä¶ == 64) break; } while (local11 != 128);`. Loop totals now **88** (60 top-test while + 25 do-while + 3 while1).
